// ===== src/services/cryptoService.js =====
import crypto from "crypto";
import fs from "fs/promises";
import path from "path";

const ALGORITHM = "aes-256-gcm";
const IV_LENGTH = 16;
const DECRYPT_FAILED_MESSAGE = "Encrypted data cannot be decrypted. The application secret may have changed.";

function createDecryptError() {
  return Object.assign(new Error(DECRYPT_FAILED_MESSAGE), { code: "DECRYPT_FAILED" });
}

class CryptoService {
  constructor(dataDir) {
    this.dataDir = dataDir;
    this.secretFile = path.join(this.dataDir, ".app-secret");
    this.cachedKey = null;
  }

  async ensureSecret() {
    if (this.cachedKey) {
      return this.cachedKey;
    }

    const envSecret = process.env.APP_SECRET?.trim();
    if (envSecret) {
      this.cachedKey = crypto
        .createHash("sha256")
        .update(envSecret)
        .digest();
      return this.cachedKey;
    }

    try {
      const existing = await fs.readFile(this.secretFile, "utf8");
      this.cachedKey = Buffer.from(existing.trim(), "hex");
      if (this.cachedKey.length !== 32) {
        throw new Error("Stored application secret is invalid. Expected a 32-byte hex key.");
      }
      await fs.chmod(this.secretFile, 0o600).catch(() => {});
      return this.cachedKey;
    } catch (error) {
      if (error.code !== "ENOENT") {
        throw error;
      }
    }

    await fs.mkdir(this.dataDir, { recursive: true, mode: 0o700 });
    const randomSecret = crypto.randomBytes(32);
    await fs.writeFile(this.secretFile, randomSecret.toString("hex"), { encoding: "utf8", mode: 0o600 });
    this.cachedKey = randomSecret;
    return this.cachedKey;
  }

  async encryptText(plainText) {
    if (!plainText) {
      return null;
    }

    const key = await this.ensureSecret();
    const iv = crypto.randomBytes(IV_LENGTH);
    const cipher = crypto.createCipheriv(ALGORITHM, key, iv);

    const encrypted = Buffer.concat([
      cipher.update(String(plainText), "utf8"),
      cipher.final(),
    ]);

    const authTag = cipher.getAuthTag();

    return {
      iv: iv.toString("hex"),
      authTag: authTag.toString("hex"),
      ciphertext: encrypted.toString("hex"),
    };
  }

  async decryptPayload(payload) {
    if (!payload?.ciphertext || !payload?.iv || !payload?.authTag) {
      return "";
    }

    const key = await this.ensureSecret();
    try {
      const decipher = crypto.createDecipheriv(
        ALGORITHM,
        key,
        Buffer.from(payload.iv, "hex")
      );

      decipher.setAuthTag(Buffer.from(payload.authTag, "hex"));

      const decrypted = Buffer.concat([
        decipher.update(Buffer.from(payload.ciphertext, "hex")),
        decipher.final(),
      ]);

      return decrypted.toString("utf8");
    } catch {
      throw createDecryptError();
    }
  }
}

export default CryptoService;


// ===== src/services/wolService.js =====
import dgram from "dgram";

const DEFAULT_PORT = 9;
const MAGIC_PREFIX = Buffer.from([0xff, 0xff, 0xff, 0xff, 0xff, 0xff]);

function parseMacAddress(mac) {
  const cleaned = String(mac).replaceAll(/[^0-9a-fA-F]/g, "");
  if (cleaned.length !== 12) {
    throw new Error(`Invalid MAC address: "${mac}". Expected 12 hex digits.`);
  }
  return Buffer.from(cleaned, "hex");
}

export function sendWoL(macAddress, { address = "255.255.255.255", port = DEFAULT_PORT } = {}) {
  return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
    const macBuffer = parseMacAddress(macAddress);
    const magicPacket = Buffer.alloc(MAGIC_PREFIX.length + macBuffer.length * 16);
    MAGIC_PREFIX.copy(magicPacket, 0);
    for (let i = 0; i < 16; i++) {
      macBuffer.copy(magicPacket, MAGIC_PREFIX.length + i * macBuffer.length);
    }

    const socket = dgram.createSocket("udp4");
    socket.on("error", (err) => {
      socket.close();
      reject(err);
    });

    socket.on("listening", () => {
      socket.setBroadcast(true);
    });

    socket.send(magicPacket, port, address, (err) => {
      socket.close();
      if (err) {
        reject(err);
      } else {
        resolve({ sent: true, mac: macAddress, address, port });
      }
    });
  });
}

export default { sendWoL };

// ===== src/services/keyStoreService.js =====
import fs from "fs/promises";
import path from "path";
import { createHash, randomUUID } from "crypto";
import ssh2 from "ssh2";

const { utils: sshUtils } = ssh2;

function validatePrivateKeyText(privateKeyText) {
  const text = String(privateKeyText || '').trim();

  if (!text) {
    throw new Error('Private key text is required');
  }

  const supportedHeaders = [
    '-----BEGIN OPENSSH PRIVATE KEY-----',
    '-----BEGIN RSA PRIVATE KEY-----',
    '-----BEGIN DSA PRIVATE KEY-----',
    '-----BEGIN EC PRIVATE KEY-----',
    '-----BEGIN PRIVATE KEY-----',
  ];

  const looksLikeSupportedPrivateKey = supportedHeaders.some((header) => text.includes(header));
  const looksLikePublicKey = /^(ssh-(rsa|ed25519)|ecdsa-sha2-)/m.test(text);
  const looksLikePuttyKey = /^PuTTY-User-Key-File-(2|3):/m.test(text);

  if (looksLikePublicKey) {
    throw new Error(
      'That looks like a public key, not a private key. Paste or upload the private key instead.'
    );
  }

  if (!looksLikeSupportedPrivateKey && !looksLikePuttyKey) {
    throw new Error(
      'Unsupported private key format. Use an OpenSSH, PEM, or PuTTY PPK private key.'
    );
  }

  return text;
}


function getPublicKeyFingerprint(privateKeyText) {
  try {
    const parsed = sshUtils.parseKey(privateKeyText);
    const key = Array.isArray(parsed) ? parsed[0] : parsed;
    if (key instanceof Error || !key?.getPublicSSH) {
      return "";
    }
    const digest = createHash("sha256")
      .update(key.getPublicSSH())
      .digest("base64")
      .replace(/=+$/, "");
    return `SHA256:${digest}`;
  } catch {
    return "";
  }
}

class KeyStoreService {
  constructor({ keyDir, cryptoService }) {
    this.keyDir = keyDir;
    this.cryptoService = cryptoService;
  }

  async init() {
    await fs.mkdir(this.keyDir, { recursive: true, mode: 0o700 });
    await fs.chmod(this.keyDir, 0o700).catch(() => {});
  }

  keyPath(id) {
    return path.join(this.keyDir, `${id}.json`);
  }

  detectKeyFormat(privateKeyText) {
    const text = String(privateKeyText || '').trim();

    if (/^PuTTY-User-Key-File-(2|3):/m.test(text)) {
      return 'ppk';
    }

    if (text.includes('-----BEGIN OPENSSH PRIVATE KEY-----')) {
      return 'openssh';
    }

    if (
      text.includes('-----BEGIN RSA PRIVATE KEY-----') ||
      text.includes('-----BEGIN DSA PRIVATE KEY-----') ||
      text.includes('-----BEGIN EC PRIVATE KEY-----') ||
      text.includes('-----BEGIN PRIVATE KEY-----')
    ) {
      return 'pem';
    }

    return 'unknown';
  }

  async listKeys() {
    const files = await fs.readdir(this.keyDir).catch(() => []);
    const records = [];

    for (const file of files) {
      if (!file.endsWith('.json')) {
        continue;
      }
      const raw = await fs.readFile(path.join(this.keyDir, file), 'utf8');
      const parsed = JSON.parse(raw);
      records.push({
        id: parsed.id,
        name: parsed.name,
        createdAt: parsed.createdAt,
        updatedAt: parsed.updatedAt,
        fingerprintHint: parsed.fingerprintHint || '',
        keyFormat: parsed.keyFormat || 'unknown',
        ownerId: parsed.ownerId || null,
      });
    }

    return records.sort((a, b) => new Date(b.updatedAt) - new Date(a.updatedAt));
  }

  async createKey({ name, privateKeyText, ownerId }) {
    const normalizedKeyText = validatePrivateKeyText(privateKeyText);

    const id = randomUUID();
    const now = new Date().toISOString();
    const encrypted = await this.cryptoService.encryptText(normalizedKeyText);

    const payload = {
      id,
      name: name?.trim() || `Key ${id.slice(0, 8)}`,
      encrypted,
      keyFormat: this.detectKeyFormat(normalizedKeyText),
      fingerprintHint: getPublicKeyFingerprint(normalizedKeyText),
      createdAt: now,
      updatedAt: now,
      ownerId: ownerId || null,
    };

    await fs.writeFile(this.keyPath(id), JSON.stringify(payload, null, 2), { encoding: 'utf8', mode: 0o600 });
    return {
      id: payload.id,
      name: payload.name,
      createdAt: payload.createdAt,
      updatedAt: payload.updatedAt,
      fingerprintHint: payload.fingerprintHint,
      keyFormat: payload.keyFormat,
      ownerId: payload.ownerId,
    };
  }

  async readKey(id) {
    const raw = await fs.readFile(this.keyPath(id), 'utf8');
    const parsed = JSON.parse(raw);
    let decrypted;
    try {
      decrypted = await this.cryptoService.decryptPayload(parsed.encrypted);
    } catch {
      throw Object.assign(
        new Error('Stored key cannot be decrypted. The application secret may have changed. Delete and re-save the key.'),
        { code: 'KEY_DECRYPT_FAILED' }
      );
    }
    return validatePrivateKeyText(decrypted);
  }

  async removeKey(id) {
    await fs.unlink(this.keyPath(id));
    return { deleted: true };
  }
}

export default KeyStoreService;


// ===== src/services/llmService.js =====
import OpenAI from "openai";

function collectTextParts(value, options = {}) {
  const { includeReasoning = false } = options;
  if (!value) {
    return [];
  }
  if (typeof value === "string") {
    return [value];
  }
  if (Array.isArray(value)) {
    return value.flatMap((item) => collectTextParts(item, options));
  }
  if (typeof value !== "object") {
    return [];
  }

  const type = String(value.type || "").toLowerCase();
  if (!includeReasoning && /reason|thinking|thought/.test(type)) {
    return [];
  }

  return [
    value.text,
    value.content,
    includeReasoning ? value.reasoning : null,
    value.output_text,
    value.summary,
    value.explanation,
    value.value,
  ].flatMap((item) => collectTextParts(item, options));
}

function normalizeChoiceMessage(choice) {
  const message = choice?.message || {};
  const content = collectTextParts(message.content)
    .map((item) => item.trim())
    .filter(Boolean)
    .join("\n\n")
    .trim();
  const reasoning = collectTextParts(message.reasoning, { includeReasoning: true })
    .map((item) => item.trim())
    .filter(Boolean)
    .join("\n\n")
    .trim();
  const fallback = [
    content,
    ...collectTextParts(message.output_text),
    ...collectTextParts(message.summary),
    ...collectTextParts(message.explanation),
  ]
    .map((item) => item.trim())
    .filter(Boolean)
    .join("\n\n")
    .trim();

  if (fallback) {
    return {
      content: content || fallback,
      reasoning: reasoning && reasoning !== content ? reasoning : "",
    };
  }

  const finishReason = choice?.finish_reason || choice?.native_finish_reason;
  if (finishReason === "length") {
    return {
      content:
        "The model stopped before producing a final answer. Try again with a shorter prompt or a higher token limit.",
      reasoning: "",
    };
  }

  return {
    content: "No response returned.",
    reasoning: "",
  };
}

class LlmService {
  constructor({ storage, cryptoService }) {
    this.storage = storage;
    this.cryptoService = cryptoService;
  }

  async getSettings() {
    const state = await this.storage.getState();
    const stored = state.llmSettings || {};
    let apiKey = process.env.LLM_API_KEY || "";

    if (stored.apiKeyEncrypted) {
      apiKey = await this.cryptoService.decryptPayload(stored.apiKeyEncrypted);
    } else if (stored.apiKey) {
      apiKey = stored.apiKey;
      const apiKeyEncrypted = await this.cryptoService.encryptText(apiKey);
      await this.storage.updateLlmSettings({ apiKeyEncrypted });
    }

    const settings = { ...stored, apiKey };
    delete settings.apiKeyEncrypted;
    return settings;
  }

  async saveSettings(patch = {}) {
    const existing = await this.getSettings();
    const apiKey = Object.prototype.hasOwnProperty.call(patch, "apiKey")
      ? String(patch.apiKey || "")
      : existing.apiKey || "";
    const apiKeyEncrypted = apiKey
      ? await this.cryptoService.encryptText(apiKey)
      : null;

    const saved = await this.storage.updateLlmSettings({
      ...patch,
      apiKeyEncrypted,
      apiKey: undefined,
    });
    const result = { ...saved, apiKey };
    delete result.apiKeyEncrypted;
    return result;
  }

  async assist({
    mode = "interpret",
    outputSnippet = "",
    userMessage = "",
    connectionName = "",
    recentCommands = [],
  }) {
    const settings = await this.getSettings();

    if (!settings.enabled || !settings.apiKey || !settings.model) {
      return {
        content:
          "LLM help is not configured yet. Open **LLM Settings** in the sidebar, add an API key, base URL, and model, then try again.",
      };
    }

    const client = new OpenAI({
      apiKey: settings.apiKey,
      baseURL: settings.baseUrl,
    });

    const modeInstruction =
      mode === "suggest"
        ? [
            "The user wants terminal command help.",
            "Recommend commands conservatively.",
            "Return the command in a fenced bash code block.",
            "Add only a very short explanation after the code.",
            "Flag destructive or risky commands clearly.",
            "Avoid long explanations unless the user explicitly asks for details.",
          ].join(" ")
        : [
            "The user wants help interpreting terminal output.",
            "Summarize the important signals first.",
            "Call out errors, warnings, and likely next steps.",
            "If suggesting inline code or commands, provide only the code and a very short explanation.",
            "Avoid long explanations unless the user explicitly asks for details.",
          ].join(" ");

    const prompt = [
      `Connection: ${connectionName || "Unknown"}`,
      recentCommands?.length
        ? `Recent commands:\n${recentCommands.map((item) => `- ${item}`).join("\n")}`
        : "Recent commands: none",
      outputSnippet ? `Terminal output:\n${outputSnippet}` : "Terminal output: none provided",
      userMessage ? `User request:\n${userMessage}` : "User request: none provided",
    ].join("\n\n");

    const response = await client.chat.completions.create({
      model: settings.model,
      temperature: mode === "suggest" ? 0.2 : 0.1,
      max_tokens: 1200,
      messages: [
        {
          role: "system",
          content: `${settings.systemPrompt || ""}\n\n${modeInstruction}`.trim(),
        },
        {
          role: "user",
          content: prompt,
        },
      ],
    });

    const normalized = normalizeChoiceMessage(response.choices?.[0]);

    return {
      content: normalized.content,
      reasoning: normalized.reasoning,
      usage: response.usage || null,
    };
  }
}

export default LlmService;


// ===== src/services/sshService.js =====
import { EventEmitter } from "events";
import ssh2 from "ssh2";
import fs from "fs/promises";
import path from "path";
import { createHash, randomUUID } from "crypto";
import mime from "mime-types";
import { redactSecrets } from "../security/redaction.js";

const { Client, utils: sshUtils } = ssh2;

function toErrorMessage(error) {
  if (!error) {
    return "Unknown SSH error";
  }
  return error.message || String(error);
}

function withContext(error, extras = {}) {
  const wrapped = error instanceof Error ? error : new Error(String(error || "Unknown error"));
  wrapped.details = {
    ...(wrapped.details || {}),
    ...extras,
  };
  return wrapped;
}

function normalizeAuthOverrides(source = {}) {
  const authOverrides = source?.authOverrides && typeof source.authOverrides === "object"
    ? source.authOverrides
    : source;

  return {
    usernameOverride:
      typeof authOverrides?.usernameOverride === "string" && authOverrides.usernameOverride.trim()
        ? authOverrides.usernameOverride.trim()
        : "",
    passwordOverride:
      typeof authOverrides?.passwordOverride === "string" && authOverrides.passwordOverride.length
        ? authOverrides.passwordOverride
        : "",
  };
}

function getPuttyKeyInfo(privateKeyText = "") {
  const match = String(privateKeyText || "").match(/^PuTTY-User-Key-File-(\d+):\s*([^\r\n]+)/m);
  if (!match) {
    return null;
  }

  return {
    version: match[1],
    algorithm: match[2].trim(),
    format: `PPK v${match[1]}`,
  };
}

function createUnsupportedPuttyKeyError(keyInfo = {}) {
  const version = keyInfo.version ? `v${keyInfo.version}` : "this";
  const algorithm = keyInfo.algorithm ? ` ${keyInfo.algorithm}` : "";
  const error = new Error(
    `Cannot parse privateKey: Unsupported key format (${version}${algorithm}).`
  );
  error.details = {
    ppkVersion: keyInfo.version || null,
    ppkAlgorithm: keyInfo.algorithm || null,
    troubleshootingHint:
      "The installed SSH key parser could not read this PuTTY key. Upgrade ssh2, or convert the key to OpenSSH and re-import it.",
    conversion:
      "PuTTYgen: load the .ppk, then Conversions > Export OpenSSH key. CLI: puttygen key.ppk -O private-openssh -o key.openssh",
    supportedFormats: ["OpenSSH private key", "PEM private key", "PuTTY PPK"],
  };
  return error;
}

function summarizeTerminalWrite(value = "") {
  const text = String(value || "");
  const preview = redactSecrets(text)
    .replace(/\x1b/g, "\\x1b")
    .replace(/\r/g, "\\r")
    .replace(/\n/g, "\\n")
    .replace(/\t/g, "\\t")
    .slice(0, 180);

  return {
    bytes: Buffer.byteLength(text),
    chars: text.length,
    hasBracketedPasteStart: text.includes("\x1b[200~"),
    hasBracketedPasteEnd: text.includes("\x1b[201~"),
    hasNewline: /[\r\n]/.test(text),
    preview,
  };
}

function createSftpPromise(connectionConfig, handler, hooks = {}) {
  return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
    const client = new Client();
    const { sftpOperationTimeoutMs, ...connectConfig } = connectionConfig;
    const timeoutMs = Number(sftpOperationTimeoutMs || 0) || Number(connectConfig.readyTimeout || 15000) + 15000;
    let settled = false;

    const finish = (callback, value) => {
      if (settled) {
        return;
      }
      settled = true;
      clearTimeout(timeout);
      try {
        client.end();
      } catch {}
      callback(value);
    };

    const safeResolve = (value) => finish(resolve, value);
    const safeReject = (error) => finish(reject, error instanceof Error ? error : new Error(String(error)));
    const timeout = setTimeout(() => {
      safeReject(new Error(`SFTP operation timed out after ${Math.round(timeoutMs / 1000)} seconds`));
    }, timeoutMs);

    hooks.attachClientHandlers?.(client);

    client
      .on("ready", () => {
        hooks.onReady?.();
        client.sftp(async (error, sftp) => {
          if (error) {
            client.end();
            safeReject(error);
            return;
          }

          try {
            const result = await handler(sftp, client);
            safeResolve(result);
          } catch (handlerError) {
            safeReject(handlerError);
          }
        });
      })
      .on("error", (error) => {
        hooks.onError?.(error);
        safeReject(error);
      })
      .on("banner", (message) => hooks.onBanner?.(message))
      .connect(connectConfig);
  });
}

function isSftpSymlinkEntry(entry) {
  return entry.attrs?.isSymbolicLink?.() || entry.longname?.startsWith("l") || false;
}

function sftpRealpath(sftp, remotePath) {
  return new Promise((resolve) => {
    if (typeof sftp.realpath !== "function") {
      resolve(remotePath);
      return;
    }

    sftp.realpath(remotePath, (error, resolvedPath) => {
      resolve(error ? remotePath : resolvedPath || remotePath);
    });
  });
}

async function directoryEntryToJson(sftp, parentPath, entry) {
  const fullPath = path.posix.join(parentPath || ".", entry.filename);
  let targetStats = null;
  if (isSftpSymlinkEntry(entry)) {
    try {
      targetStats = await sftpStat(sftp, fullPath);
    } catch {
      const isReadableDirectory = await sftpCanReadDirectory(sftp, fullPath);
      if (isReadableDirectory) {
        targetStats = { isDirectory: () => true };
      }
    }
  }

  return {
    name: entry.filename,
    path: fullPath,
    isDirectory:
      entry.longname?.startsWith("d") ||
      entry.attrs?.isDirectory?.() ||
      targetStats?.isDirectory?.() ||
      false,
    isSymlink: isSftpSymlinkEntry(entry),
    size: targetStats?.size || entry.attrs?.size || 0,
    modifiedAt: targetStats?.mtime
      ? new Date(targetStats.mtime * 1000).toISOString()
      : entry.attrs?.mtime
        ? new Date(entry.attrs.mtime * 1000).toISOString()
        : null,
    permissions: entry.longname || "",
  };
}

function normalizeRelativePath(value = "") {
  return String(value || "").replace(/\\/g, "/").replace(/^\/+/, "").replace(/\/+$/, "");
}

function shellQuote(value = "") {
  return `'${String(value).replace(/'/g, `'\\''`)}'`;
}

function rsyncRemoteSpec(config = {}) {
  const username = String(config.username || "").trim();
  const host = String(config.host || "").trim();
  if (!username || !host) {
    throw new Error("Remote rsync target is missing username or host.");
  }
  return `${username}@${host}`;
}

function validateRsyncRelativePath(relativePath = "") {
  const normalized = normalizeRelativePath(relativePath);
  if (
    !normalized ||
    normalized.includes("\n") ||
    normalized.includes("\r") ||
    normalized.includes("\t") ||
    normalized.split("/").some((part) => part === "..")
  ) {
    throw new Error(`Cannot direct-sync unsafe relative path: ${relativePath}`);
  }
  return normalized;
}

function parseIgnorePatterns(patterns = []) {
  const source = Array.isArray(patterns) ? patterns : String(patterns || "").split(/[\n,]+/);
  return source
    .map((pattern) => String(pattern || "").trim().replace(/\\/g, "/").replace(/^\/+/, ""))
    .filter(Boolean);
}

function escapeRegExp(value = "") {
  return String(value).replace(/[|\\{}()[\]^$+?.]/g, "\\$&");
}

function wildcardPatternToRegex(pattern = "") {
  const normalized = normalizeRelativePath(pattern);
  if (!normalized) {
    return null;
  }

  const directoryPattern = /\/$/.test(String(pattern).trim());
  const prepared = directoryPattern ? `${normalized}/**` : normalized;
  const subtreePattern = prepared.endsWith("/**");
  const globSource = subtreePattern ? prepared.slice(0, -3) : prepared;
  let source = "";

  for (let index = 0; index < globSource.length; index += 1) {
    const char = globSource[index];
    const next = globSource[index + 1];
    if (char === "*" && next === "*") {
      source += ".*";
      index += 1;
    } else if (char === "*") {
      source += "[^/]*";
    } else if (char === "?") {
      source += "[^/]";
    } else {
      source += escapeRegExp(char);
    }
  }

  if (subtreePattern) {
    if (!globSource.includes("/")) {
      return new RegExp(`(^|/)${source}(?:/.*)?$`, "i");
    }
    return new RegExp(`^${source}(?:/.*)?$`, "i");
  }
  if (!globSource.includes("/")) {
    return new RegExp(`(^|/)${source}$`, "i");
  }
  return new RegExp(`^${source}$`, "i");
}

function createIgnoreMatcher(patterns = []) {
  const regexes = parseIgnorePatterns(patterns).map(wildcardPatternToRegex).filter(Boolean);
  if (!regexes.length) {
    return () => false;
  }

  return (relativePath = "") => {
    const normalized = normalizeRelativePath(relativePath);
    if (!normalized) {
      return false;
    }
    return regexes.some((regex) => regex.test(normalized));
  };
}

function filterIgnoredEntries(entries = [], patterns = []) {
  const ignored = createIgnoreMatcher(patterns);
  let ignoredCount = 0;
  const filtered = [];

  entries.forEach((entry) => {
    const relativePath = normalizeRelativePath(entry.relativePath);
    const ignoredEntry = ignored(relativePath) || relativePath.split("/").some((_part, index, parts) => {
      const directoryPath = parts.slice(0, index + 1).join("/");
      return index < parts.length - 1 && ignored(directoryPath);
    });
    if (ignoredEntry) {
      ignoredCount += 1;
      return;
    }
    filtered.push(entry);
  });

  return { entries: filtered, ignoredCount, patterns: parseIgnorePatterns(patterns) };
}

function sftpStat(sftp, remotePath) {
  return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
    sftp.stat(remotePath, (error, stats) => {
      if (error) {
        reject(error);
        return;
      }
      resolve(stats);
    });
  });
}

function sftpCanReadDirectory(sftp, remotePath) {
  return new Promise((resolve) => {
    sftp.readdir(remotePath, (error) => {
      resolve(!error);
    });
  });
}

function sftpMkdir(sftp, remotePath) {
  return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
    sftp.mkdir(remotePath, (error) => {
      if (error) {
        reject(error);
        return;
      }
      resolve({ ok: true });
    });
  });
}

async function sftpMkdirp(sftp, remotePath) {
  const normalized = String(remotePath || "").replace(/\\/g, "/").replace(/\/+$/, "");
  if (!normalized || normalized === "." || normalized === "/") {
    return { ok: true };
  }

  const absolute = normalized.startsWith("/");
  const parts = normalized.split("/").filter(Boolean);
  let current = absolute ? "/" : "";

  for (const part of parts) {
    current = absolute
      ? path.posix.join(current, part)
      : current
        ? path.posix.join(current, part)
        : part;

    try {
      const stats = await sftpStat(sftp, current);
      if (!stats?.isDirectory?.()) {
        throw new Error(`${current} exists and is not a directory`);
      }
    } catch (error) {
      if (error?.code === 2 || /No such file/i.test(error?.message || "")) {
        await sftpMkdir(sftp, current);
        continue;
      }
      throw error;
    }
  }

  return { ok: true };
}

function createSftpTimeout(operation, timeoutMs) {
  const error = new Error(`${operation} timed out after ${Math.round(timeoutMs / 1000)} seconds`);
  error.code = "SFTP_TIMEOUT";
  return error;
}

function readSftpBuffer(sftp, remotePath, { timeoutMs = 60_000 } = {}) {
  return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
    const chunks = [];
    let settled = false;
    let stream;
    const finish = (callback, value) => {
      if (settled) return;
      settled = true;
      clearTimeout(timer);
      callback(value);
    };
    const timer = setTimeout(() => {
      try { stream?.destroy?.(); } catch {}
      finish(reject, createSftpTimeout(`Reading ${remotePath}`, timeoutMs));
    }, timeoutMs);

    try {
      stream = sftp.createReadStream(remotePath);
      stream.on("data", (chunk) => chunks.push(Buffer.from(chunk)));
      stream.once("error", (error) => finish(reject, error));
      stream.once("end", () => finish(resolve, Buffer.concat(chunks)));
    } catch (error) {
      finish(reject, error);
    }
  });
}

function sftpOpen(sftp, remotePath, flags, attrs = {}) {
  return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
    sftp.open(remotePath, flags, attrs, (error, handle) => {
      if (error) {
        reject(error);
        return;
      }
      resolve(handle);
    });
  });
}

function sftpWrite(sftp, handle, buffer, offset, length, position) {
  return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
    sftp.write(handle, buffer, offset, length, position, (error) => {
      if (error) {
        reject(error);
        return;
      }
      resolve({ ok: true });
    });
  });
}

function sftpClose(sftp, handle) {
  return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
    sftp.close(handle, (error) => {
      if (error) {
        reject(error);
        return;
      }
      resolve({ ok: true });
    });
  });
}

async function writeSftpBufferDirect(sftp, remotePath, buffer) {
  const handle = await sftpOpen(sftp, remotePath, "w", { mode: 0o666 });
  let closeError = null;
  try {
    let offset = 0;
    while (offset < buffer.length) {
      const length = Math.min(buffer.length - offset, 32 * 1024);
      await sftpWrite(sftp, handle, buffer, offset, length, offset);
      offset += length;
    }
  } finally {
    try {
      await sftpClose(sftp, handle);
    } catch (error) {
      closeError = error;
    }
  }
  if (closeError) {
    throw closeError;
  }
  return { ok: true };
}

function writeSftpBuffer(sftp, remotePath, buffer, { timeoutMs = 60_000 } = {}) {
  return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
    let settled = false;
    let stream;
    const finish = (callback, value) => {
      if (settled) return;
      settled = true;
      clearTimeout(timer);
      callback(value);
    };
    const timer = setTimeout(() => {
      try { stream?.destroy?.(); } catch {}
      finish(reject, createSftpTimeout(`Writing ${remotePath}`, timeoutMs));
    }, timeoutMs);

    try {
      if (
        typeof sftp.open === "function" &&
        typeof sftp.write === "function" &&
        typeof sftp.close === "function"
      ) {
        writeSftpBufferDirect(sftp, remotePath, buffer)
          .then((result) => finish(resolve, result))
          .catch((error) => finish(reject, error));
        return;
      }

      stream = sftp.createWriteStream(remotePath, {
        flags: "w",
        mode: 0o666,
        autoClose: true,
      });
      stream.once("error", (error) => finish(reject, error));
      stream.once("finish", () => finish(resolve, { ok: true }));
      stream.end(buffer);
    } catch (error) {
      finish(reject, error);
    }
  });
}

export async function writeAndVerifySftpText(
  sftp,
  remotePath,
  content,
  { timeoutMs = 60_000, operationId = randomUUID(), onStage = () => {} } = {}
) {
  const expected = Buffer.from(content ?? "", "utf8");
  const expectedHash = createHash("sha256").update(expected).digest("hex");
  const stage = async (event, message, details = {}, level = "info") => {
    await onStage({ event, message, details, level, operationId, remotePath });
  };

  await stage("sftp-write-start", "Opening remote file for a complete overwrite.", {
    byteLength: expected.length,
    sha256: expectedHash,
  });
  await writeSftpBuffer(sftp, remotePath, expected, { timeoutMs });
  await stage("sftp-write-finished", "Remote write stream finished.", {
    byteLength: expected.length,
  });

  await stage("sftp-write-verify-start", "Reading the remote file back for verification.");
  const actual = await readSftpBuffer(sftp, remotePath, { timeoutMs });
  const actualHash = createHash("sha256").update(actual).digest("hex");

  if (actual.length !== expected.length || actualHash !== expectedHash || !actual.equals(expected)) {
    const error = new Error("Remote file verification failed after saving.");
    error.code = "SFTP_SAVE_VERIFY_FAILED";
    error.details = {
      operationId,
      remotePath,
      expectedByteLength: expected.length,
      actualByteLength: actual.length,
      expectedSha256: expectedHash,
      actualSha256: actualHash,
    };
    await stage("sftp-write-verify-failed", error.message, error.details, "error");
    throw error;
  }

  const result = {
    ok: true,
    verified: true,
    operationId,
    remotePath,
    byteLength: actual.length,
    sha256: actualHash,
  };
  await stage("sftp-write-verified", "Remote file contents match the submitted editor contents.", result);
  return result;
}

class SshService extends EventEmitter {
  constructor({ storage, keyStore, cryptoService, logService, uploadDir }) {
    super();
    this.storage = storage;
    this.keyStore = keyStore;
    this.cryptoService = cryptoService;
    this.logService = logService;
    this.uploadDir = uploadDir;
    this.terminals = new Map();
  }

  sanitizeConfigSummary(connectionRecord, originalConfig, resolvedConfig, authOverrideMeta = {}) {
    const privateKeyHeader = originalConfig?.privateKey
      ? String(originalConfig.privateKey).split(/\r?\n/, 1)[0].trim()
      : null;

    return {
      connectionId: connectionRecord?.id || null,
      connectionName: connectionRecord?.name || null,
      host: resolvedConfig?.host || originalConfig?.host || null,
      port: resolvedConfig?.port || originalConfig?.port || 22,
      username: resolvedConfig?.username || originalConfig?.username || null,
      authType: connectionRecord?.authType || (resolvedConfig?.privateKey ? "privateKey" : "password"),
      privateKeyId: connectionRecord?.privateKeyId || null,
      hasPassphrase: Boolean(resolvedConfig?.passphrase || originalConfig?.passphrase),
      hasPassword: Boolean(resolvedConfig?.password),
      privateKeyHeader,
      ppkDetected: /^PuTTY-User-Key-File/i.test(privateKeyHeader || ""),
      usingPasswordOverride: Boolean(authOverrideMeta.passwordOverride),
      usingPasswordOnlyFallback: Boolean(authOverrideMeta.usingPasswordOnlyFallback),
      authMethodsConfigured: this.buildAuthMethodsConfigured(resolvedConfig),
      readyTimeoutMs: resolvedConfig?.readyTimeout || 15000,
      keepaliveIntervalMs: resolvedConfig?.keepaliveInterval || 10000,
    };
  }

  buildAuthMethodsConfigured(config) {
    const methods = [];
    if (config?.privateKey) {
      methods.push("privateKey");
    }
    if (config?.password) {
      methods.push("password");
    }
    if (config?.tryKeyboard && config?.password) {
      methods.push("keyboardInteractive");
    }
    return methods;
  }

  applyAuthOverrides(baseConfig, connectionRecord, authOverrides = {}) {
    const normalized = normalizeAuthOverrides(authOverrides);
    const config = { ...baseConfig };
    let usingPasswordOnlyFallback = false;

    if (normalized.usernameOverride) {
      config.username = normalized.usernameOverride;
    }

    if (normalized.passwordOverride) {
      config.password = normalized.passwordOverride;
      config.tryKeyboard = true;

      if (config.privateKey || connectionRecord?.privateKeyId) {
        delete config.privateKey;
        delete config.passphrase;
        usingPasswordOnlyFallback = true;
      }
    } else if (config.password) {
      config.tryKeyboard = true;
    }

    return {
      config,
      authOverrideMeta: {
        ...normalized,
        usingPasswordOnlyFallback,
      },
    };
  }

  inspectPrivateKey(config = {}) {
    if (!config.privateKey) {
      return null;
    }

    try {
      const parsed = parsePrivateKeyOrThrow(config.privateKey, config.passphrase || undefined);
      const key = Array.isArray(parsed) ? parsed[0] : parsed;
      return {
        ok: true,
        type: key?.type || null,
        comment: key?.comment || null,
        keyCount: Array.isArray(parsed) ? parsed.length : 1,
      };
    } catch (error) {
      const keyInfo = getPuttyKeyInfo(config.privateKey);
      return {
        ok: false,
        error: error.message,
        parserMessage: error?.details?.parserMessage || null,
        ppkVersion: keyInfo?.version || null,
        ppkAlgorithm: keyInfo?.algorithm || null,
      };
    }
  }

  addPreviousAttemptDetails(error, previousError) {
    const wrapped = error instanceof Error ? error : new Error(String(error || "Unknown error"));
    wrapped.details = {
      ...(wrapped.details || {}),
      previousAttempt: {
        message: previousError?.message || toErrorMessage(previousError),
        details: previousError?.details || null,
      },
    };
    return wrapped;
  }


  buildPasswordOnlyFallbackConfig(config = {}) {
    const passwordOnlyConfig = { ...config };
    delete passwordOnlyConfig.privateKey;
    delete passwordOnlyConfig.passphrase;
    if (passwordOnlyConfig.password) {
      passwordOnlyConfig.tryKeyboard = true;
    }
    return passwordOnlyConfig;
  }

  shouldRetryWithStoredPassword(error, config = {}, debugMeta = {}) {
    const authFailure = /All configured authentication methods failed/i.test(toErrorMessage(error));
    return Boolean(
      authFailure &&
        config?.privateKey &&
        config?.password &&
        !debugMeta?.usingPasswordOnlyFallback &&
        !debugMeta?.usingPasswordOverride
    );
  }

  async debug(entry = {}) {
    return this.logService.appendDebug({ area: "ssh", ...entry });
  }

  buildDebugLogger(baseMeta = {}) {
    return (message, level = "debug") => {
      const normalized = String(message || "").trim();
      if (!normalized) {
        return;
      }
      this.debug({
        ...baseMeta,
        level,
        event: "client-debug",
        message: normalized,
      }).catch(() => {});
    };
  }

  attachClientDebugHandlers(client, baseMeta = {}, authContext = {}) {
    client.on("banner", (message) => {
      this.debug({
        ...baseMeta,
        level: "info",
        event: "banner",
        message: String(message || "").trim(),
      }).catch(() => {});
    });

    client.on("keyboard-interactive", (name, instructions, lang, prompts, finish) => {
      const promptTexts = Array.isArray(prompts)
        ? prompts.map((prompt) => prompt?.prompt || "").filter(Boolean)
        : [];

      this.debug({
        ...baseMeta,
        level: "warn",
        event: "keyboard-interactive",
        message: "Server requested keyboard-interactive authentication.",
        details: {
          prompts: promptTexts,
          hasPassword: Boolean(authContext.password),
        },
      }).catch(() => {});

      if (authContext.password) {
        finish(promptTexts.map(() => authContext.password));
        return;
      }

      finish([]);
    });

    client.on("end", () => {
      this.debug({
        ...baseMeta,
        level: "info",
        event: "client-end",
        message: "SSH client ended.",
      }).catch(() => {});
    });

    client.on("close", () => {
      this.debug({
        ...baseMeta,
        level: "info",
        event: "client-close",
        message: "SSH client connection closed.",
      }).catch(() => {});
    });
  }

  enrichError(error, baseMeta = {}, fallbackMessage = "SSH connection failed") {
    const originalMessage = toErrorMessage(error);
    const summaryMessage = `${fallbackMessage}: ${originalMessage}`;
    const authFailure = /All configured authentication methods failed/i.test(originalMessage);

    const details = {
      ...baseMeta,
      originalMessage,
      level: error?.level || null,
      code: error?.code || null,
      description: error?.description || null,
      authFailure,
      canRetryWithPasswordPrompt:
        authFailure &&
        !baseMeta.usingPasswordOverride &&
        !baseMeta.hasPassword,
      troubleshootingHint: authFailure
        ? "Authentication was rejected by the server. Check username, selected key, passphrase, password fallback, and whether the remote account allows this auth method."
        : null,
    };

    return withContext(new Error(summaryMessage), details);
  }

  async connectionConfigFromSaved(connectionId, authOverrides = {}) {
    const connection = await this.storage.getById("connections", connectionId);
    if (!connection) {
      throw new Error("Connection not found");
    }
    const normalizedAuthOverrides = normalizeAuthOverrides(authOverrides);
    const usingPasswordOverride = Boolean(normalizedAuthOverrides.passwordOverride);

    const base = {
      host: connection.host,
      port: Number(connection.port || 22),
      username: connection.username,
      readyTimeout: 15000,
      keepaliveInterval: 10000,
      keepaliveCountMax: 5,
      tryKeyboard: false,
    };

    if (connection.privateKeyId && !usingPasswordOverride) {
      base.privateKey = await this.keyStore.readKey(connection.privateKeyId);
      if (connection.passphraseEncrypted) {
        try {
          base.passphrase = await this.cryptoService.decryptPayload(connection.passphraseEncrypted);
        } catch {
          throw Object.assign(
            new Error("Stored passphrase cannot be decrypted. The application secret may have changed. Delete and re-save the connection."),
            { code: "DECRYPT_FAILED" }
          );
        }
      }
    }

    if (connection.passwordEncrypted && !usingPasswordOverride) {
      try {
        base.password = await this.cryptoService.decryptPayload(connection.passwordEncrypted);
      } catch {
        throw Object.assign(
          new Error("Stored password cannot be decrypted. The application secret may have changed. Delete and re-save the connection."),
          {
            code: "DECRYPT_FAILED",
            details: {
              canRetryWithPasswordPrompt: true,
              troubleshootingHint:
                "Enter the SSH password again for this attempt, then save the connection to replace the stale encrypted password.",
            },
          }
        );
      }
      base.tryKeyboard = true;
    }

    const { config, authOverrideMeta } = this.applyAuthOverrides(base, connection, normalizedAuthOverrides);
    if (!config.privateKey && !config.password) {
      throw new Error("Connection must have either a password or private key.");
    }

    const debugMeta = this.sanitizeConfigSummary(connection, base, config, authOverrideMeta);
    const keyInspection = this.inspectPrivateKey(config);

    await this.debug({
      ...debugMeta,
      level: "info",
      event: "config-built",
      message: "Built SSH connection config from saved connection.",
      details: {
        hasUsernameOverride: Boolean(authOverrideMeta.usernameOverride),
        hasPasswordOverride: Boolean(authOverrideMeta.passwordOverride),
      },
    });

    if (keyInspection) {
      await this.debug({
        ...debugMeta,
        level: keyInspection.ok ? "info" : "error",
        event: keyInspection.ok ? "private-key-parse-ok" : "private-key-parse-error",
        message: keyInspection.ok
          ? "Private key parsed successfully before SSH connection attempt."
          : "Private key could not be parsed before SSH connection attempt.",
        details: keyInspection,
      });
    }

    return {
      connectionRecord: connection,
      config,
      debugMeta,
    };
  }

  async testConnection(connectionId, authOverrides = {}) {
    const { config, debugMeta } = await this.connectionConfigFromSaved(connectionId, authOverrides);

    const attempt = (attemptConfig, attemptMeta) => new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
      const connectConfig = {
        ...attemptConfig,
        debug: this.buildDebugLogger({ ...attemptMeta, eventScope: "test" }),
      };
      const client = new Client();
      this.attachClientDebugHandlers(client, { ...attemptMeta, eventScope: "test" }, { password: attemptConfig.password });

      client
        .on("ready", async () => {
          await this.debug({
            ...attemptMeta,
            level: "info",
            event: "test-ready",
            message: "SSH connection test succeeded.",
          });
          client.end();
          resolve({ ok: true });
        })
        .on("error", async (error) => {
          const enriched = this.enrichError(error, attemptMeta, "SSH test failed");
          await this.debug({
            ...attemptMeta,
            level: "error",
            event: "test-error",
            message: enriched.message,
            details: enriched.details,
          });
          reject(enriched);
        })
        .connect(connectConfig);
    });

    await this.debug({
      ...debugMeta,
      level: "info",
      event: "test-start",
      message: "Testing SSH connection.",
    });

    try {
      return await attempt(config, debugMeta);
    } catch (error) {
      if (this.shouldRetryWithStoredPassword(error, config, debugMeta)) {
        const retryConfig = this.buildPasswordOnlyFallbackConfig(config);
        const retryMeta = {
          ...debugMeta,
          usingPasswordOnlyFallback: true,
          authMethodsConfigured: this.buildAuthMethodsConfigured(retryConfig),
        };
        await this.debug({
          ...retryMeta,
          level: "warn",
          event: "test-retry-password-only",
          message: "Private-key SSH test failed. Retrying with saved password fallback only.",
          details: {
            previousAttempt: {
              message: error.message,
              details: error.details || null,
            },
          },
        });
        try {
          return await attempt(retryConfig, retryMeta);
        } catch (retryError) {
          throw this.addPreviousAttemptDetails(retryError, error);
        }
      }
      throw error;
    }
  }

  async createTerminal({ connectionId, cols = 120, rows = 30, title = "", authOverrides = {}, ownerId, privateMode = false }) {
    const { connectionRecord, config, debugMeta } = await this.connectionConfigFromSaved(connectionId, authOverrides);
    const terminalId = randomUUID();

    const attempt = (attemptConfig, attemptMeta) => new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
      const client = new Client();
      const connectConfig = {
        ...attemptConfig,
        debug: this.buildDebugLogger({ ...attemptMeta, terminalId, eventScope: "terminal" }),
      };

      const onError = async (error) => {
        const enriched = this.enrichError(
          error,
          { ...attemptMeta, terminalId },
          "Terminal SSH connection failed"
        );
        this.emit("terminal:error", {
          terminalId,
          ownerId,
          message: enriched.message,
        });
        await this.debug({
          ...attemptMeta,
          terminalId,
          level: "error",
          event: "terminal-connect-error",
          message: enriched.message,
          details: enriched.details,
        });
        reject(enriched);
      };

      this.attachClientDebugHandlers(client, { ...attemptMeta, terminalId, eventScope: "terminal" }, { password: attemptConfig.password });

      client
        .on("ready", async () => {
          await this.debug({
            ...attemptMeta,
            terminalId,
            level: "info",
            event: "terminal-ready",
            message: "SSH connection ready. Opening shell.",
          });

          client.shell(
            {
              term: "xterm-256color",
              cols,
              rows,
            },
            async (error, stream) => {
              if (error) {
                await onError(error);
                client.end();
                return;
              }

              const log = this.logService.getOrCreate(terminalId, { persist: !privateMode });

              const terminal = {
                terminalId,
                connectionId,
                connectionName: connectionRecord.name,
                title: title || connectionRecord.name,
                client,
                stream,
                createdAt: new Date().toISOString(),
                log,
                ownerId,
                privateMode: Boolean(privateMode),
              };

              this.terminals.set(terminalId, terminal);

              stream.on("data", (chunk) => {
                log.append(chunk);
                this.emit("terminal:data", {
                  terminalId,
                  ownerId,
                  data: chunk.toString("utf8"),
                });
              });

              stream.on("close", async () => {
                await this.debug({
                  ...attemptMeta,
                  terminalId,
                  level: "info",
                  event: "terminal-stream-close",
                  message: "Terminal stream closed.",
                });
                await this.closeTerminal(terminalId, false);
              });

              stream.stderr?.on("data", (chunk) => {
                log.append(chunk);
                this.emit("terminal:data", {
                  terminalId,
                  ownerId,
                  data: chunk.toString("utf8"),
                });
              });

              this.emit("terminal:status", {
                terminalId,
                ownerId,
                status: "connected",
                connectionName: connectionRecord.name,
              });

              resolve({
                terminalId,
                connectionId,
                connectionName: connectionRecord.name,
                title: terminal.title,
                privateMode: terminal.privateMode,
              });
            }
          );
        })
        .on("error", onError)
        .on("close", async () => {
          if (this.terminals.has(terminalId)) {
            await this.closeTerminal(terminalId, false);
          }
        })
        .connect(connectConfig);
    });

    await this.debug({
      ...debugMeta,
      terminalId,
      level: "info",
      event: "terminal-connect-start",
      message: "Starting terminal SSH connection.",
    });

    try {
      return await attempt(config, debugMeta);
    } catch (error) {
      if (this.shouldRetryWithStoredPassword(error, config, debugMeta)) {
        const retryConfig = this.buildPasswordOnlyFallbackConfig(config);
        const retryMeta = {
          ...debugMeta,
          usingPasswordOnlyFallback: true,
          authMethodsConfigured: this.buildAuthMethodsConfigured(retryConfig),
        };
        await this.debug({
          ...retryMeta,
          terminalId,
          level: "warn",
          event: "terminal-retry-password-only",
          message: "Private-key terminal connection failed. Retrying with saved password fallback only.",
          details: {
            previousAttempt: {
              message: error.message,
              details: error.details || null,
            },
          },
        });
        try {
          return await attempt(retryConfig, retryMeta);
        } catch (retryError) {
          throw this.addPreviousAttemptDetails(retryError, error);
        }
      }
      throw error;
    }
  }

  requireOwnedTerminal(terminalId, ownerId = "") {
    const terminal = this.terminals.get(terminalId);
    if (!terminal) {
      const error = new Error("Terminal not found");
      error.statusCode = 404;
      throw error;
    }
    if (ownerId && terminal.ownerId !== ownerId) {
      const error = new Error("Access denied to terminal");
      error.statusCode = 403;
      throw error;
    }
    return terminal;
  }

  listActiveTerminals() {
    return Array.from(this.terminals.values()).map((item) => ({
      terminalId: item.terminalId,
      connectionId: item.connectionId,
      connectionName: item.connectionName,
      ownerId: item.ownerId,
      title: item.title,
      createdAt: item.createdAt,
      privateMode: Boolean(item.privateMode),
      logFile: item.privateMode ? null : path.join("data", "logs", `${item.terminalId}.log`),
      outputTail: item.log?.getTail(1000) || "",
    }));
  }

  input(terminalId, data, meta = {}) {
    const terminal = this.requireOwnedTerminal(terminalId, meta.ownerId);
    const summary = summarizeTerminalWrite(data);
    if (process.env.DEBUG_TERMINAL_INPUT === "1" && (process.env.NODE_ENV !== "production" || process.env.ALLOW_SENSITIVE_DEBUG === "1")) {
      console.info("[ssh terminal:input]", {
        terminalId,
        connectionId: terminal?.connectionId || null,
        connectionName: terminal?.connectionName || null,
        source: meta.source || "unknown",
        socketId: meta.socketId || null,
        ...summary,
      });
    }


    this.debug({
      terminalId,
      connectionId: terminal.connectionId,
      connectionName: terminal.connectionName,
      level: "debug",
      event: "terminal-input",
      message: "Writing terminal input to SSH stream.",
      details: { source: meta.source || "unknown", socketId: meta.socketId || null, ...summary },
    }).catch(() => {});

    terminal.stream.write(data);
  }

  resize(terminalId, cols, rows, meta = {}) {
    const terminal = this.requireOwnedTerminal(terminalId, meta.ownerId);
    terminal.stream.setWindow(rows, cols, rows, cols);
  }

  sendBatch(terminalId, commandsText = "", meta = {}) {
    const terminal = this.requireOwnedTerminal(terminalId, meta.ownerId);
    const incomingSummary = summarizeTerminalWrite(commandsText);
    if (process.env.DEBUG_TERMINAL_INPUT === "1" && (process.env.NODE_ENV !== "production" || process.env.ALLOW_SENSITIVE_DEBUG === "1")) {
      console.info("[ssh terminal:sendBatch]", {
        terminalId,
        connectionId: terminal.connectionId,
        connectionName: terminal.connectionName,
        source: meta.source || "batch",
        socketId: meta.socketId || null,
        ...incomingSummary,
      });
    }


    const normalized = String(commandsText || "")
      .replace(/\r\n/g, "\n")
      .replace(/\r/g, "\n")
      .trim();

    if (!normalized) {
      this.debug({
        terminalId,
        connectionId: terminal.connectionId,
        connectionName: terminal.connectionName,
        level: "debug",
        event: "terminal-batch-empty",
        message: "Ignoring empty terminal batch command.",
        details: { source: meta.source || "batch", socketId: meta.socketId || null, ...incomingSummary },
      }).catch(() => {});
      return;
    }

    const payload = normalized
      .split("\n")
      .map((line) => `${line}\r`)
      .join("");

    this.debug({
      terminalId,
      connectionId: terminal.connectionId,
      connectionName: terminal.connectionName,
      level: "debug",
      event: "terminal-batch",
      message: "Writing terminal batch command to SSH stream.",
      details: {
        source: meta.source || "batch",
        socketId: meta.socketId || null,
        incoming: incomingSummary,
        outgoing: summarizeTerminalWrite(payload),
      },
    }).catch(() => {});

    terminal.stream.write(payload);
  }

  async closeTerminal(terminalId, closeClient = true, ownerId = "") {
    const terminal = this.terminals.get(terminalId);
    if (!terminal) {
      return;
    }
    if (ownerId && terminal.ownerId !== ownerId) {
      const error = new Error("Access denied to terminal");
      error.statusCode = 403;
      throw error;
    }

    this.terminals.delete(terminalId);

    try {
      if (closeClient) {
        terminal.stream.end("exit\n");
      }
    } catch {}

    try {
      if (closeClient) {
        terminal.client.end();
      }
    } catch {}

    await this.logService.close(terminalId);

    this.emit("terminal:closed", {
      terminalId,
      ownerId: terminal.ownerId,
      privateMode: Boolean(terminal.privateMode),
    });
  }

  async withSftp(connectionId, remotePath, operationName, handler, authOverrides = {}) {
    const { config, debugMeta } = await this.connectionConfigFromSaved(connectionId, authOverrides);
    const operationTimeouts = {
      tree: 5 * 60 * 1000,
      write: 5 * 60 * 1000,
      upload: 5 * 60 * 1000,
    };

    const attempt = async (attemptConfig, attemptMeta) => {
      const connectConfig = {
        ...attemptConfig,
        sftpOperationTimeoutMs: operationTimeouts[operationName],
        debug: this.buildDebugLogger({ ...attemptMeta, eventScope: `sftp:${operationName}`, remotePath }),
      };

      return createSftpPromise(connectConfig, handler, {
        attachClientHandlers: (client) => {
          this.attachClientDebugHandlers(
            client,
            { ...attemptMeta, eventScope: `sftp:${operationName}`, remotePath },
            { password: attemptConfig.password }
          );
        },
        onReady: () => {
          this.debug({
            ...attemptMeta,
            remotePath,
            level: "info",
            event: "sftp-ready",
            message: `SFTP ready for ${operationName}.`,
          }).catch(() => {});
        },
        onError: (error) => {
          const enriched = this.enrichError(
            error,
            { ...attemptMeta, remotePath },
            `SFTP ${operationName} failed`
          );
          this.debug({
            ...attemptMeta,
            remotePath,
            level: "error",
            event: "sftp-error",
            message: enriched.message,
            details: enriched.details,
          }).catch(() => {});
        },
        onBanner: (message) => {
          this.debug({
            ...attemptMeta,
            remotePath,
            level: "info",
            event: "sftp-banner",
            message: String(message || "").trim(),
          }).catch(() => {});
        },
      });
    };

    await this.debug({
      ...debugMeta,
      remotePath,
      level: "info",
      event: "sftp-start",
      message: `Starting SFTP ${operationName}.`,
    });

    try {
      const result = await attempt(config, debugMeta);
      await this.debug({
        ...debugMeta,
        remotePath,
        level: "info",
        event: "sftp-success",
        message: `SFTP ${operationName} succeeded.`,
      });
      return result;
    } catch (error) {
      if (this.shouldRetryWithStoredPassword(error, config, debugMeta)) {
        const retryConfig = this.buildPasswordOnlyFallbackConfig(config);
        const retryMeta = {
          ...debugMeta,
          usingPasswordOnlyFallback: true,
          authMethodsConfigured: this.buildAuthMethodsConfigured(retryConfig),
        };
        await this.debug({
          ...retryMeta,
          remotePath,
          level: "warn",
          event: "sftp-retry-password-only",
          message: `Private-key SFTP ${operationName} failed. Retrying with saved password fallback only.`,
          details: {
            previousAttempt: {
              message: error.message,
              details: error.details || null,
            },
          },
        });
        try {
          return await attempt(retryConfig, retryMeta);
        } catch (retryError) {
          throw this.addPreviousAttemptDetails(retryError, error);
        }
      }
      throw this.enrichError(error, { ...debugMeta, remotePath }, `SFTP ${operationName} failed`);
    }
  }

  async sftpList(connectionId, remotePath = ".", authOverrides = {}) {
    return this.withSftp(connectionId, remotePath, "list", async (sftp) => {
      const items = await new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
        sftp.readdir(remotePath, (error, list) => {
          if (error) {
            reject(error);
            return;
          }
          resolve(list || []);
        });
      });

      const entries = await Promise.all(
        items
          .filter((item) => ![".", ".."].includes(item.filename))
          .map((item) => directoryEntryToJson(sftp, remotePath, item))
      );

      return entries.sort((a, b) => {
        if (a.isDirectory !== b.isDirectory) {
          return a.isDirectory ? -1 : 1;
        }
        return a.name.localeCompare(b.name);
      });
    }, authOverrides);
  }

  async sftpListTree(connectionId, remotePath = ".", authOverrides = {}) {
    return this.withSftp(connectionId, remotePath, "tree", async (sftp) => {
      const rootPath = String(remotePath || ".").replace(/\/+$/, "") || ".";
      const entries = [];
      const visitedDirectoryTargets = new Set();

      const walk = async (currentRemotePath, relativeBase = "") => {
        const realCurrentPath = await sftpRealpath(sftp, currentRemotePath);
        if (visitedDirectoryTargets.has(realCurrentPath)) {
          return;
        }
        visitedDirectoryTargets.add(realCurrentPath);

        const items = await new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
          sftp.readdir(currentRemotePath, (error, list) => {
            if (error) {
              reject(error);
              return;
            }
            resolve(list || []);
          });
        });

        for (const item of items.filter((entry) => ![".", ".."].includes(entry.filename))) {
          const entry = await directoryEntryToJson(sftp, currentRemotePath, item);
          const relativePath = relativeBase ? path.posix.join(relativeBase, item.filename) : item.filename;

          entries.push({
            ...entry,
            relativePath,
          });

          if (entry.isDirectory) {
            await walk(entry.path, relativePath);
          }
        }
      };

      try {
        await walk(rootPath);
      } catch (error) {
        if (error?.code === 2 || /No such file/i.test(error?.message || "")) {
          return [];
        }
        throw error;
      }
      return entries.sort((a, b) =>
        a.relativePath.localeCompare(b.relativePath, undefined, { numeric: true, sensitivity: "base" })
      );
    }, authOverrides);
  }

  async sftpFileEntry(connectionId, remotePath, authOverrides = {}) {
    return this.withSftp(connectionId, remotePath, "stat", async (sftp) => {
      try {
        const stats = await sftpStat(sftp, remotePath);
        if (stats?.isDirectory?.()) {
          throw new Error(`${remotePath} is a directory. Select a file for single-file sync.`);
        }
        const name = path.posix.basename(String(remotePath || ""));
        return {
          name,
          path: remotePath,
          relativePath: name,
          isDirectory: false,
          size: stats?.size || 0,
          modifiedAt: stats?.mtime ? new Date(stats.mtime * 1000).toISOString() : null,
          permissions: "",
        };
      } catch (error) {
        if (error?.code === 2 || /No such file/i.test(error?.message || "")) {
          return null;
        }
        throw error;
      }
    }, authOverrides);
  }

  async sftpSearch(connectionId, remotePath = ".", query = "", options = {}, authOverrides = {}) {
    const searchQuery = String(query || "").trim().toLowerCase();
    const limit = Math.min(Math.max(Number(options.limit) || 200, 1), 500);

    if (!searchQuery) {
      return { entries: [], truncated: false };
    }

    return this.withSftp(connectionId, remotePath, "search", async (sftp) => {
      const rootPath = String(remotePath || ".").replace(/\/+$/, "") || ".";
      const entries = [];
      let truncated = false;
      const visitedDirectoryTargets = new Set();

      const walk = async (currentRemotePath, relativeBase = "") => {
        if (entries.length >= limit) {
          truncated = true;
          return;
        }
        const realCurrentPath = await sftpRealpath(sftp, currentRemotePath);
        if (visitedDirectoryTargets.has(realCurrentPath)) {
          return;
        }
        visitedDirectoryTargets.add(realCurrentPath);

        const items = await new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
          sftp.readdir(currentRemotePath, (error, list) => {
            if (error) {
              reject(error);
              return;
            }
            resolve(list || []);
          });
        });

        for (const item of items.filter((entry) => ![".", ".."].includes(entry.filename))) {
          if (entries.length >= limit) {
            truncated = true;
            return;
          }

          const entry = await directoryEntryToJson(sftp, currentRemotePath, item);
          const relativePath = relativeBase ? path.posix.join(relativeBase, item.filename) : item.filename;

          if (String(item.filename || "").toLowerCase().includes(searchQuery)) {
            entries.push({
              ...entry,
              relativePath,
            });
          }

          if (entry.isDirectory) {
            await walk(entry.path, relativePath);
          }
        }
      };

      try {
        await walk(rootPath);
      } catch (error) {
        if (error?.code === 2 || /No such file/i.test(error?.message || "")) {
          return { entries: [], truncated: false };
        }
        throw error;
      }

      return {
        entries: entries.sort((a, b) =>
          a.relativePath.localeCompare(b.relativePath, undefined, { numeric: true, sensitivity: "base" })
        ),
        truncated,
      };
    }, authOverrides);
  }

  async sftpReadText(connectionId, remotePath, authOverrides = {}) {
    return this.withSftp(connectionId, remotePath, "read", async (sftp) => {
      const buffer = await readSftpBuffer(sftp, remotePath, { timeoutMs: 60_000 });
      return buffer.toString("utf8");
    }, authOverrides);
  }

  async sftpWriteText(connectionId, remotePath, content, authOverrides = {}, operationMeta = {}) {
    const operationId = operationMeta.operationId || randomUUID();
    return this.withSftp(connectionId, remotePath, "write", async (sftp) => {
      return writeAndVerifySftpText(sftp, remotePath, content, {
        operationId,
        timeoutMs: Number(operationMeta.timeoutMs || 60_000),
        onStage: async (entry) => {
          const logEntry = {
            ...entry,
            connectionId,
            userId: operationMeta.userId || null,
          };
          await Promise.allSettled([
            this.debug(logEntry),
            this.logService.appendFileSave?.(logEntry),
          ]);
        },
      });
    }, authOverrides);
  }

  async sftpMkdir(connectionId, remotePath, authOverrides = {}) {
    return this.withSftp(connectionId, remotePath, "mkdir", async (sftp) => {
      return sftpMkdirp(sftp, remotePath);
    }, authOverrides);
  }

  async sftpDelete(connectionId, remotePath, isDirectory = false, authOverrides = {}) {
    return this.withSftp(connectionId, remotePath, "delete", async (sftp) => {
      await new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
        const done = (error) => {
          if (error) {
            reject(error);
            return;
          }
          resolve();
        };

        if (isDirectory) {
          sftp.rmdir(remotePath, done);
        } else {
          sftp.unlink(remotePath, done);
        }
      });

      return { ok: true };
    }, authOverrides);
  }

  async sftpRename(connectionId, oldPath, newPath, authOverrides = {}) {
    return this.withSftp(connectionId, oldPath, "rename", async (sftp) => {
      await new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
        sftp.rename(oldPath, newPath, (error) => {
          if (error) {
            reject(error);
            return;
          }
          resolve();
        });
      });

      return { ok: true };
    }, authOverrides);
  }

  async sftpUploadLocalFile(connectionId, localPath, remotePath, authOverrides = {}) {
    return this.withSftp(connectionId, remotePath, "upload", async (sftp) => {
      await sftpMkdirp(sftp, path.posix.dirname(remotePath));
      await new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
        sftp.fastPut(localPath, remotePath, (error) => {
          if (error) {
            reject(error);
            return;
          }
          resolve();
        });
      });
      return { ok: true };
    }, authOverrides);
  }

  async sftpDownloadToTemp(connectionId, remotePath, authOverrides = {}) {
    const filename = path.posix.basename(remotePath);
    const localPath = path.join(this.uploadDir, `${Date.now()}-${filename}`);

    await fs.mkdir(this.uploadDir, { recursive: true });

    await this.withSftp(connectionId, remotePath, "download", async (sftp) => {
      await new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
        sftp.fastGet(remotePath, localPath, (error) => {
          if (error) {
            reject(error);
            return;
          }
          resolve();
        });
      });
      return { ok: true };
    }, authOverrides);

    return {
      localPath,
      filename,
      contentType: mime.lookup(filename) || "application/octet-stream",
    };
  }

  async getTerminalCwd(terminalId) {
    const terminal = this.terminals.get(terminalId);
    if (!terminal || !terminal.client) {
      throw new Error("Terminal connection not found");
    }

    const command = `
# 1. Try process tree method (Linux)
my_sshd_pid=$PPID
if [ -n "$my_sshd_pid" ]; then
  connection_sshd_pid=$(ps -o ppid= -p $my_sshd_pid | tr -d ' ')
  if [ -n "$connection_sshd_pid" ] && [ "$connection_sshd_pid" -ne 1 ]; then
    siblings=$(pgrep -P $connection_sshd_pid | grep -v $my_sshd_pid)
    for sibling in $siblings; do
      shell_pids=$(pgrep -P $sibling)
      for spid in $shell_pids; do
        if [ -d "/proc/$spid/cwd" ]; then
          cwd=$(readlink "/proc/$spid/cwd")
          if [ -n "$cwd" ]; then
            echo "$cwd"
            exit 0
          fi
        fi
      done
    done
  fi
fi

# 2. Fallback to searching active shell processes with controlling TTY
for pid in $(pgrep -u $(whoami) -f '^(bash|zsh|sh|tcsh|ksh)'); do
  tty=$(ps -o tty= -p $pid)
  if [ "$tty" != "?" ] && [ -n "$tty" ]; then
    if [ -d "/proc/$pid/cwd" ]; then
      cwd=$(readlink "/proc/$pid/cwd")
    else
      # macOS fallback using lsof
      cwd=$(lsof -p $pid -a -d cwd -Fn 2>/dev/null | awk 'NR==2{print substr($0,2)}')
    fi
    if [ -n "$cwd" ]; then
      echo "$cwd"
      exit 0
    fi
  fi
done

# 3. Last resort fallback
pwd
`;

    return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
      terminal.client.exec(command, (error, stream) => {
        if (error) {
          reject(error);
          return;
        }
        let stdout = "";
        stream.on("data", (data) => {
          stdout += data.toString();
        });
        stream.on("close", () => {
          resolve(stdout.trim());
        });
      });
    });
  }

  async executeRemoteCommand(connectionId, command, authOverrides = {}) {
    return this.withSftp(connectionId, "", "exec", async (sftp, client) => {
      return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
        client.exec(command, (error, stream) => {
          if (error) {
            reject(error);
            return;
          }

          let stdout = "";
          let stderr = "";

          stream
            .on("data", (data) => {
              stdout += data.toString();
            })
            .stderr.on("data", (data) => {
              stderr += data.toString();
            });

          stream.on("close", (code, signal) => {
            resolve({ code, signal, stdout, stderr });
          });
        });
      });
    }, authOverrides);
  }

  executeRemoteCommandOnClient(client, command) {
    return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
      client.exec(command, (error, stream) => {
        if (error) {
          reject(error);
          return;
        }

        let stdout = "";
        let stderr = "";

        stream
          .on("data", (data) => {
            stdout += data.toString();
          })
          .stderr.on("data", (data) => {
            stderr += data.toString();
          });

        stream.on("close", (code, signal) => {
          resolve({ code, signal, stdout, stderr });
        });
      });
    });
  }

  async executeRemoteCommandOnClientChecked(client, command) {
    const result = await this.executeRemoteCommandOnClient(client, command);
    if (result.code !== 0) {
      const output = [result.stderr, result.stdout].filter(Boolean).join("\n").trim();
      throw new Error(output || `Remote command failed with exit code ${result.code}`);
    }
    return result;
  }

  writeTextToSftp(sftp, remotePath, content, options = {}) {
    return writeAndVerifySftpText(sftp, remotePath, content, options);
  }

  async downloadAndCleanupArchive(connectionId, zipRemotePath, tarRemotePath, authOverrides = {}) {
    return this.withSftp(connectionId, "", "download-archive", async (sftp) => {
      let chosenRemotePath = null;
      let filename = "";

      const checkExists = (remoteFilePath) => new Promise((resolve) => {
        sftp.stat(remoteFilePath, (err) => {
          resolve(!err);
        });
      });

      const zipExists = await checkExists(zipRemotePath);
      if (zipExists) {
        chosenRemotePath = zipRemotePath;
        filename = path.posix.basename(zipRemotePath);
      } else {
        const tarExists = await checkExists(tarRemotePath);
        if (tarExists) {
          chosenRemotePath = tarRemotePath;
          filename = path.posix.basename(tarRemotePath);
        }
      }

      if (!chosenRemotePath) {
        throw new Error("Compression failed: archive file not found on remote server.");
      }

      const localPath = path.join(this.uploadDir, `${Date.now()}-${filename}`);
      await fs.mkdir(this.uploadDir, { recursive: true });

      await new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
        sftp.fastGet(chosenRemotePath, localPath, (error) => {
          if (error) {
            reject(error);
            return;
          }
          resolve();
        });
      });

      await new Promise((resolve) => {
        sftp.unlink(chosenRemotePath, () => {
          resolve();
        });
      });

      return {
        localPath,
        filename,
        contentType: mime.lookup(filename) || "application/octet-stream",
      };
    }, authOverrides);
  }

  async withTwoSftps(connectionIdA, connectionIdB, handler, authOverridesA = {}, authOverridesB = {}) {
    const { config: configA } = await this.connectionConfigFromSaved(connectionIdA, authOverridesA);
    const { config: configB } = await this.connectionConfigFromSaved(connectionIdB, authOverridesB);

    const clientA = new Client();
    const clientB = new Client();

    const connectClient = (client, config) => new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
      client
        .on("ready", () => {
          client.sftp((error, sftp) => {
            if (error) {
              client.end();
              reject(error);
            } else {
              resolve(sftp);
            }
          });
        })
        .on("error", (error) => {
          reject(error);
        })
        .connect(config);
    });

    try {
      const [sftpA, sftpB] = await Promise.all([
        connectClient(clientA, configA),
        connectClient(clientB, configB)
      ]);

      try {
        const result = await handler(sftpA, sftpB, clientA, clientB);
        return result;
      } finally {
        clientA.end();
        clientB.end();
      }
    } catch (error) {
      clientA.end();
      clientB.end();
      throw error;
    }
  }

  buildRemoteSyncPlan({ direction, entriesA, entriesB, pathA, pathB, connectionIdA, connectionIdB, includeDeletes, conflictPolicy, ignorePatterns = [] }) {
    const filteredA = filterIgnoredEntries(entriesA, ignorePatterns);
    const filteredB = filterIgnoredEntries(entriesB, ignorePatterns);
    entriesA = filteredA.entries;
    entriesB = filteredB.entries;

    const mkdirA = [];
    const mkdirB = [];
    const copyAtoB = [];
    const copyBtoA = [];
    const deleteA = [];
    const deleteB = [];
    const conflicts = [];
    let unchangedCount = 0;

    const addMissingDirs = (sourceDirs, targetMap, targetSide) => {
      sourceDirs.forEach(entry => {
        const relativePath = path.posix.join(entry.relativePath);
        if (!targetMap.has(relativePath)) {
          const action = targetSide === "a" ? "mkdir_a" : "mkdir_b";
          const op = { ...entry, action };
          if (targetSide === "a") mkdirA.push(op);
          else mkdirB.push(op);
        }
      });
    };

    const dirsA = entriesA.filter(e => e.isDirectory);
    const dirsB = entriesB.filter(e => e.isDirectory);
    const filesA = entriesA.filter(e => !e.isDirectory);
    const filesB = entriesB.filter(e => !e.isDirectory);

    const fileMapA = new Map(filesA.map(f => [f.relativePath, f]));
    const fileMapB = new Map(filesB.map(f => [f.relativePath, f]));
    const dirMapA = new Map(dirsA.map(d => [d.relativePath, d]));
    const dirMapB = new Map(dirsB.map(d => [d.relativePath, d]));

    if (direction === "a-to-b") {
      addMissingDirs(dirsA, dirMapB, "b");
    } else if (direction === "b-to-a") {
      addMissingDirs(dirsB, dirMapA, "a");
    } else {
      addMissingDirs(dirsA, dirMapB, "b");
      addMissingDirs(dirsB, dirMapA, "a");
    }

    const allFilePaths = new Set([...fileMapA.keys(), ...fileMapB.keys()]);

    allFilePaths.forEach(relativePath => {
      const fileA = fileMapA.get(relativePath);
      const fileB = fileMapB.get(relativePath);

      if (direction === "a-to-b") {
        if (fileA && !fileB) {
          copyAtoB.push({ ...fileA, action: "copy_a_to_b" });
        } else if (fileA && fileB) {
          if (fileA.size === fileB.size && fileA.modifiedAt === fileB.modifiedAt) {
            unchangedCount++;
          } else {
            copyAtoB.push({ ...fileA, action: "update_b" });
          }
        } else if (!fileA && fileB && includeDeletes) {
          deleteB.push({ ...fileB, action: "delete_b" });
        }
      } else if (direction === "b-to-a") {
        if (!fileA && fileB) {
          copyBtoA.push({ ...fileB, action: "copy_b_to_a" });
        } else if (fileA && fileB) {
          if (fileA.size === fileB.size && fileA.modifiedAt === fileB.modifiedAt) {
            unchangedCount++;
          } else {
            copyBtoA.push({ ...fileB, action: "update_a" });
          }
        } else if (fileA && !fileB && includeDeletes) {
          deleteA.push({ ...fileA, action: "delete_a" });
        }
      } else {
        if (fileA && !fileB) {
          copyAtoB.push({ ...fileA, action: "copy_a_to_b" });
        } else if (!fileA && fileB) {
          copyBtoA.push({ ...fileB, action: "copy_b_to_a" });
        } else if (fileA && fileB) {
          if (fileA.size === fileB.size && fileA.modifiedAt === fileB.modifiedAt) {
            unchangedCount++;
          } else {
            if (conflictPolicy === "a-wins") {
              copyAtoB.push({ ...fileA, action: "update_b" });
            } else if (conflictPolicy === "b-wins") {
              copyBtoA.push({ ...fileB, action: "update_a" });
            } else if (conflictPolicy === "newer") {
              const timeA = new Date(fileA.modifiedAt).getTime();
              const timeB = new Date(fileB.modifiedAt).getTime();
              if (timeA > timeB) {
                copyAtoB.push({ ...fileA, action: "update_b" });
              } else if (timeB > timeA) {
                copyBtoA.push({ ...fileB, action: "update_a" });
              } else {
                unchangedCount++;
              }
            } else {
              conflicts.push({
                relativePath,
                fileA,
                fileB,
                action: "conflict_skip"
              });
            }
          }
        }
      }
    });

    const totalOperations = mkdirA.length + mkdirB.length + copyAtoB.length + copyBtoA.length + deleteA.length + deleteB.length;

    return {
      mkdirA,
      mkdirB,
      copyAtoB,
      copyBtoA,
      deleteA,
      deleteB,
      conflicts,
      unchangedCount,
      totalOperations,
      direction,
      pathA,
      pathB,
      connectionIdA,
      connectionIdB,
      includeDeletes,
      conflictPolicy,
      ignorePatterns: filteredA.patterns,
      ignoredCount: filteredA.ignoredCount + filteredB.ignoredCount,
    };
  }

  buildRemoteFileSyncPlan({ direction, fileA, fileB, pathA, pathB, connectionIdA, connectionIdB, includeDeletes, conflictPolicy }) {
    const baseA = path.posix.dirname(pathA || ".");
    const baseB = path.posix.dirname(pathB || ".");
    const nameA = path.posix.basename(pathA || "");
    const nameB = path.posix.basename(pathB || "");
    const entryA = fileA ? { ...fileA, relativePath: nameA, targetRelativePath: nameB } : null;
    const entryB = fileB ? { ...fileB, relativePath: nameB, targetRelativePath: nameA } : null;
    const copyAtoB = [];
    const copyBtoA = [];
    const deleteA = [];
    const deleteB = [];
    const conflicts = [];
    let unchangedCount = 0;

    if (direction === "a-to-b") {
      if (entryA && !entryB) copyAtoB.push({ ...entryA, action: "copy_a_to_b" });
      else if (entryA && entryB) {
        if (entryA.size === entryB.size && entryA.modifiedAt === entryB.modifiedAt) unchangedCount++;
        else copyAtoB.push({ ...entryA, action: "update_b" });
      } else if (!entryA && entryB && includeDeletes) deleteB.push({ ...entryB, action: "delete_b" });
    } else if (direction === "b-to-a") {
      if (!entryA && entryB) copyBtoA.push({ ...entryB, action: "copy_b_to_a" });
      else if (entryA && entryB) {
        if (entryA.size === entryB.size && entryA.modifiedAt === entryB.modifiedAt) unchangedCount++;
        else copyBtoA.push({ ...entryB, action: "update_a" });
      } else if (entryA && !entryB && includeDeletes) deleteA.push({ ...entryA, action: "delete_a" });
    } else if (entryA && !entryB) {
      copyAtoB.push({ ...entryA, action: "copy_a_to_b" });
    } else if (!entryA && entryB) {
