      copyBtoA.push({ ...entryB, action: "copy_b_to_a" });
    } else if (entryA && entryB) {
      if (entryA.size === entryB.size && entryA.modifiedAt === entryB.modifiedAt) {
        unchangedCount++;
      } else if (conflictPolicy === "a-wins") {
        copyAtoB.push({ ...entryA, action: "update_b" });
      } else if (conflictPolicy === "b-wins") {
        copyBtoA.push({ ...entryB, action: "update_a" });
      } else if (conflictPolicy === "newer") {
        const timeA = new Date(entryA.modifiedAt).getTime();
        const timeB = new Date(entryB.modifiedAt).getTime();
        if (timeA > timeB) copyAtoB.push({ ...entryA, action: "update_b" });
        else if (timeB > timeA) copyBtoA.push({ ...entryB, action: "update_a" });
        else unchangedCount++;
      } else {
        conflicts.push({ relativePath: `${nameA} <-> ${nameB}`, fileA: entryA, fileB: entryB, action: "conflict_skip" });
      }
    }

    return {
      mode: "file",
      mkdirA: [],
      mkdirB: [],
      copyAtoB,
      copyBtoA,
      deleteA,
      deleteB,
      conflicts,
      unchangedCount,
      totalOperations: copyAtoB.length + copyBtoA.length + deleteA.length + deleteB.length,
      direction,
      pathA: baseA,
      pathB: baseB,
      connectionIdA,
      connectionIdB,
      includeDeletes,
      conflictPolicy,
      ignorePatterns: [],
      ignoredCount: 0,
    };
  }

  buildDirectRsyncScript() {
    return `#!/bin/sh
set -eu

SRC_BASE=$1
DEST=$2
DEST_BASE=$3
DEST_BASE_SH=$4
LIST_FILE=$5
AUTH_MODE=$6
AUTH_FILE=$7
PORT=$8

require_command() {
  if ! command -v "$1" >/dev/null 2>&1; then
    echo "Missing required command on source host: $1" >&2
    exit 127
  fi
}

validate_rel() {
  case "$1" in
    ""|/*|../*|*/../*|*/..|..)
      echo "Unsafe relative path for direct sync: $1" >&2
      exit 2
      ;;
  esac
}

quote_squote() {
  printf "'%s'" "$(printf '%s' "$1" | sed "s/'/'\\\\''/g")"
}

require_command rsync
require_command ssh

SSH_COMMON="-p $PORT -o StrictHostKeyChecking=no -o UserKnownHostsFile=/dev/null -o ConnectTimeout=15"

if [ "$AUTH_MODE" = "key" ]; then
  SSH_CMD="ssh -i $AUTH_FILE $SSH_COMMON -o BatchMode=yes"
elif [ "$AUTH_MODE" = "password" ]; then
  require_command sshpass
  SSH_CMD="sshpass -f $AUTH_FILE ssh $SSH_COMMON -o BatchMode=no -o PreferredAuthentications=password -o PubkeyAuthentication=no"
else
  echo "Unsupported auth mode: $AUTH_MODE" >&2
  exit 2
fi

$SSH_CMD "$DEST" "mkdir -p -- $DEST_BASE_SH"

while IFS="$(printf '\t')" read -r SRC_REL DEST_REL || [ -n "$SRC_REL" ]; do
  [ -n "$DEST_REL" ] || DEST_REL="$SRC_REL"
  validate_rel "$SRC_REL"
  validate_rel "$DEST_REL"
  DEST_REL_DIR=$(dirname -- "$DEST_REL")
  if [ "$DEST_REL_DIR" != "." ]; then
    $SSH_CMD "$DEST" "mkdir -p -- $DEST_BASE_SH/$(quote_squote "$DEST_REL_DIR")"
  fi
  SRC="\${SRC_BASE%/}/./$SRC_REL"
  rsync -a --protect-args -e "$SSH_CMD" "$SRC" "$DEST:\${DEST_BASE%/}/$DEST_REL"
done < "$LIST_FILE"
`;
  }

  selectDirectRsyncAuth(targetConfig = {}) {
    if (targetConfig.privateKey && !targetConfig.passphrase) {
      if (/^PuTTY-User-Key-File/i.test(String(targetConfig.privateKey).trim())) {
        throw new Error(
          "Direct remote sync cannot use PuTTY PPK keys on the source host. Convert the target key to OpenSSH format or add a saved password fallback."
        );
      }
      return {
        mode: "key",
        secret: String(targetConfig.privateKey),
        fileName: "target_key",
      };
    }

    if (targetConfig.privateKey && targetConfig.passphrase && targetConfig.password) {
      return {
        mode: "password",
        secret: String(targetConfig.password),
        fileName: "target_password",
      };
    }

    if (targetConfig.privateKey && targetConfig.passphrase) {
      throw new Error(
        "Direct remote sync cannot use passphrase-protected target keys yet. Add a saved password fallback for the target connection or use an unencrypted deploy key limited to rsync."
      );
    }

    if (targetConfig.password) {
      return {
        mode: "password",
        secret: String(targetConfig.password),
        fileName: "target_password",
      };
    }

    throw new Error("Direct remote sync target must have a private key or password.");
  }

  async runDirectRsyncCopyBatch({
    sourceSftp,
    sourceClient,
    targetConnectionId,
    sourceBasePath,
    targetBasePath,
    entries,
    authOverridesTarget = {},
    onProgress = () => {},
    label = "copy",
  }) {
    if (!entries.length) {
      return;
    }

    const { config: targetConfig } = await this.connectionConfigFromSaved(targetConnectionId, authOverridesTarget);
    const targetAuth = this.selectDirectRsyncAuth(targetConfig);
    const targetSpec = rsyncRemoteSpec(targetConfig);
    const targetPort = Number(targetConfig.port || 22);
    const tempDir = `/tmp/terminal-direct-sync-${randomUUID()}`;
    const scriptPath = `${tempDir}/sync.sh`;
    const listPath = `${tempDir}/files.txt`;
    const authPath = `${tempDir}/${targetAuth.fileName}`;
    const transferPairs = entries.map((entry) => ({
      source: validateRsyncRelativePath(entry.relativePath),
      target: validateRsyncRelativePath(entry.targetRelativePath || entry.relativePath),
    }));

    if (!sourceSftp || !sourceClient) {
      throw new Error("Direct remote sync requires an active source SSH/SFTP connection.");
    }

    await this.executeRemoteCommandOnClientChecked(
      sourceClient,
      `umask 077 && mkdir -p -- ${shellQuote(tempDir)}`
    );

    try {
      await this.writeTextToSftp(sourceSftp, scriptPath, this.buildDirectRsyncScript());
      await this.writeTextToSftp(
        sourceSftp,
        listPath,
        `${transferPairs.map((pair) => `${pair.source}\t${pair.target}`).join("\n")}\n`
      );
      await this.writeTextToSftp(sourceSftp, authPath, targetAuth.secret);

      await this.executeRemoteCommandOnClientChecked(
        sourceClient,
        `chmod 700 -- ${shellQuote(tempDir)} && chmod 700 -- ${shellQuote(scriptPath)} && chmod 600 -- ${shellQuote(authPath)} ${shellQuote(listPath)}`
      );

      await this.executeRemoteCommandOnClientChecked(
        sourceClient,
        `${shellQuote(scriptPath)} ${shellQuote(sourceBasePath)} ${shellQuote(targetSpec)} ${shellQuote(targetBasePath)} ${shellQuote(shellQuote(targetBasePath))} ${shellQuote(listPath)} ${shellQuote(targetAuth.mode)} ${shellQuote(authPath)} ${shellQuote(String(targetPort))}`
      );

      entries.forEach((entry, index) => {
        onProgress(`${label}: ${entry.relativePath}`, index + 1, entries.length);
      });
    } finally {
      await this.executeRemoteCommandOnClient(sourceClient, `rm -rf -- ${shellQuote(tempDir)}`).catch(() => {});
    }
  }

  async executeRemoteSync(plan, onProgress = () => {}, authOverridesA = {}, authOverridesB = {}) {
    const {
      connectionIdA,
      connectionIdB,
      pathA,
      pathB,
      mkdirA,
      mkdirB,
      copyAtoB,
      copyBtoA,
      deleteA,
      deleteB,
    } = plan;

    await this.withTwoSftps(connectionIdA, connectionIdB, async (sftpA, sftpB) => {
      let completedOps = 0;
      const totalOps = plan.totalOperations;

      const incrementProgress = (msg) => {
        completedOps++;
        const percent = totalOps > 0 ? Math.round((completedOps / totalOps) * 100) : 100;
        onProgress(msg, percent);
      };

      // 1. Create folders on A
      for (const dir of mkdirA) {
        const fullPath = path.posix.join(pathA, dir.relativePath);
        const percent = totalOps > 0 ? Math.round((completedOps / totalOps) * 100) : 0;
        onProgress(`Creating directory on A: ${dir.relativePath}`, percent);
        await new Promise((resolve) => sftpA.mkdir(fullPath, () => resolve()));
        incrementProgress(`Created directory on A: ${dir.relativePath}`);
      }

      // 2. Create folders on B
      for (const dir of mkdirB) {
        const fullPath = path.posix.join(pathB, dir.relativePath);
        const percent = totalOps > 0 ? Math.round((completedOps / totalOps) * 100) : 0;
        onProgress(`Creating directory on B: ${dir.relativePath}`, percent);
        await new Promise((resolve) => sftpB.mkdir(fullPath, () => resolve()));
        incrementProgress(`Created directory on B: ${dir.relativePath}`);
      }

      // 3. Delete files/folders on A
      for (const entry of deleteA) {
        const fullPath = path.posix.join(pathA, entry.relativePath);
        const percent = totalOps > 0 ? Math.round((completedOps / totalOps) * 100) : 0;
        onProgress(`Deleting on A: ${entry.relativePath}`, percent);
        await new Promise((resolve) => {
          if (entry.isDirectory) {
            sftpA.rmdir(fullPath, () => resolve());
          } else {
            sftpA.unlink(fullPath, () => resolve());
          }
        });
        incrementProgress(`Deleted on A: ${entry.relativePath}`);
      }

      // 4. Delete files/folders on B
      for (const entry of deleteB) {
        const fullPath = path.posix.join(pathB, entry.relativePath);
        const percent = totalOps > 0 ? Math.round((completedOps / totalOps) * 100) : 0;
        onProgress(`Deleting on B: ${entry.relativePath}`, percent);
        await new Promise((resolve) => {
          if (entry.isDirectory) {
            sftpB.rmdir(fullPath, () => resolve());
          } else {
            sftpB.unlink(fullPath, () => resolve());
          }
        });
        incrementProgress(`Deleted on B: ${entry.relativePath}`);
      }

      // File bytes are copied directly between remotes. The terminal server only stages
      // a short-lived helper on the source host and reports progress.
      await this.runDirectRsyncCopyBatch({
        sourceSftp: sftpA,
        sourceClient: clientA,
        targetConnectionId: connectionIdB,
        sourceBasePath: pathA,
        targetBasePath: pathB,
        entries: copyAtoB,
        authOverridesTarget: authOverridesB,
        label: "Copied A to B",
        onProgress: (message) => incrementProgress(message),
      });

      await this.runDirectRsyncCopyBatch({
        sourceSftp: sftpB,
        sourceClient: clientB,
        targetConnectionId: connectionIdA,
        sourceBasePath: pathB,
        targetBasePath: pathA,
        entries: copyBtoA,
        authOverridesTarget: authOverridesA,
        label: "Copied B to A",
        onProgress: (message) => incrementProgress(message),
      });
    }, authOverridesA, authOverridesB);
  }

  async getDebugLog({ connectionId = null, limit = 100 } = {}) {
    return this.logService.readDebugTail({ connectionId, limit });
  }
}

export default SshService;


// ===== src/services/logService.js =====
import fs from "fs/promises";
import path from "path";
import stripAnsi from "strip-ansi";
import { redactSecrets } from "../security/redaction.js";

const DEFAULT_TEXT_LOG_LIMIT = 20 * 1024 * 1024;
const DEFAULT_TEXT_LOG_KEEP = 5 * 1024 * 1024;

function serializeValue(value, depth = 0) {
  if (depth > 5) return "[depth limit]";
  if (value === null || value === undefined) return value;
  if (value instanceof Error) {
    return {
      name: redactSecrets(String(value.name || "Error")).slice(0, 200),
      message: redactSecrets(String(value.message || "")).slice(0, 20_000),
      code: value.code ? redactSecrets(String(value.code)).slice(0, 500) : null,
      stack: redactSecrets(String(value.stack || "")).slice(0, 40_000),
      details: serializeValue(value.details || null, depth + 1),
    };
  }
  if (typeof value === "string") return redactSecrets(value).slice(0, 20_000);
  if (typeof value === "number" || typeof value === "boolean") return value;
  if (Buffer.isBuffer(value)) return `[Buffer ${value.length} bytes]`;
  if (Array.isArray(value)) return value.slice(0, 100).map((item) => serializeValue(item, depth + 1));
  if (typeof value === "object") {
    const output = {};
    for (const [key, item] of Object.entries(value).slice(0, 100)) {
      if (/password|passphrase|privatekey|authorization|cookie|api.?key|secret/i.test(key)) {
        output[key] = "[REDACTED]";
      } else if (/content/i.test(key) && typeof item === "string") {
        output[key] = `[content omitted: ${Buffer.byteLength(item, "utf8")} bytes]`;
      } else {
        output[key] = serializeValue(item, depth + 1);
      }
    }
    return output;
  }
  return redactSecrets(String(value)).slice(0, 20_000);
}

function formatTextEntry(entry = {}) {
  const timestamp = entry.timestamp || new Date().toISOString();
  const level = String(entry.level || "info").toUpperCase();
  const event = String(entry.event || "event");
  const message = redactSecrets(String(entry.message || "")).trim();
  const details = serializeValue(entry.details || null);
  const header = `[${timestamp}] ${level} ${event}${entry.requestId ? ` request=${entry.requestId}` : ""}${entry.operationId ? ` operation=${entry.operationId}` : ""}`;
  const lines = [header, message];
  if (details && (typeof details !== "object" || Object.keys(details).length)) {
    lines.push(JSON.stringify(details, null, 2));
  }
  return `${lines.filter(Boolean).join("\n")}\n${"-".repeat(80)}\n`;
}

class RollingLog {
  constructor({ terminalId, logDir, persist = true }) {
    this.terminalId = terminalId;
    this.logDir = logDir;
    this.persist = persist;
    this.lines = [];
    this.partial = "";
    this.flushTimer = null;
  }

  get filePath() {
    return path.join(this.logDir, `${this.terminalId}.log`);
  }

  append(chunk) {
    const cleanChunk = stripAnsi(String(chunk || ""))
      .replace(/\u0000/g, "")
      .replace(/\r\n/g, "\n")
      .replace(/\r/g, "\n");

    const joined = `${this.partial}${cleanChunk}`;
    const segments = joined.split("\n");
    this.partial = segments.pop() ?? "";
    this.lines.push(...segments);
    this.lines = this.lines.slice(-1000);
    if (this.persist) {
      this.scheduleFlush();
    }
  }

  getTail(maxLines = 200, includePartial = true) {
    const tail = this.lines.slice(-maxLines);
    if (includePartial && this.partial) {
      tail.push(this.partial);
    }
    return tail.join("\n");
  }

  scheduleFlush() {
    clearTimeout(this.flushTimer);
    this.flushTimer = setTimeout(() => {
      this.flush().catch((error) => {
        console.error(`Failed to flush terminal log ${this.terminalId}:`, error);
      });
    }, 250);
  }

  async flush(includePartial = false) {
    if (!this.persist) {
      return;
    }
    await fs.mkdir(this.logDir, { recursive: true });
    const tail = [...this.lines];
    if (includePartial && this.partial) {
      tail.push(this.partial);
    }
    await fs.writeFile(this.filePath, tail.slice(-1000).join("\n"), "utf8");
  }

  async close() {
    clearTimeout(this.flushTimer);
    if (this.persist) {
      await this.flush(true);
    }
  }
}

class LogService {
  constructor(logDir) {
    this.logDir = logDir;
    this.buffers = new Map();
    this.debugPath = path.join(this.logDir, "ssh-debug.jsonl");
    this.serverErrorPath = path.join(this.logDir, "server-errors.txt");
    this.fileSavePath = path.join(this.logDir, "file-save-debug.txt");
    this.clientDebugPath = path.join(this.logDir, "client-debug.txt");
    this.textWriteQueue = Promise.resolve();
  }

  getOrCreate(terminalId, { persist = true } = {}) {
    if (!this.buffers.has(terminalId)) {
      this.buffers.set(terminalId, new RollingLog({ terminalId, logDir: this.logDir, persist }));
    }
    return this.buffers.get(terminalId);
  }

  async close(terminalId) {
    const buffer = this.buffers.get(terminalId);
    if (!buffer) return;
    await buffer.close();
    this.buffers.delete(terminalId);
  }

  async appendDebug(entry = {}) {
    await fs.mkdir(this.logDir, { recursive: true });
    const payload = serializeValue({ timestamp: new Date().toISOString(), ...entry });
    await fs.appendFile(this.debugPath, `${JSON.stringify(payload)}\n`, "utf8");
    this.pruneDebugLog().catch((err) => console.error("Failed to prune debug log:", err));
    return payload;
  }

  appendText(filePath, entry = {}) {
    const payload = { timestamp: new Date().toISOString(), ...entry };
    this.textWriteQueue = this.textWriteQueue
      .catch(() => {})
      .then(async () => {
        await fs.mkdir(this.logDir, { recursive: true });
        await fs.appendFile(filePath, formatTextEntry(payload), "utf8");
        await this.pruneTextLog(filePath).catch((error) => {
          console.error(`Failed to prune ${path.basename(filePath)}:`, error);
        });
      });
    return this.textWriteQueue.then(() => payload);
  }

  appendServerError(error, context = {}) {
    const normalized = error instanceof Error ? error : new Error(String(error || "Unknown server error"));
    return this.appendText(this.serverErrorPath, {
      level: "error",
      event: context.event || "server-error",
      requestId: context.requestId,
      operationId: context.operationId,
      message: normalized.message,
      details: {
        ...context,
        error: normalized,
      },
    });
  }

  appendFileSave(entry = {}) {
    return this.appendText(this.fileSavePath, {
      level: entry.level || "info",
      event: entry.event || "file-save",
      requestId: entry.requestId,
      operationId: entry.operationId,
      message: entry.message || "File save event",
      details: entry.details || {},
    });
  }

  appendClientDebug(entry = {}) {
    return this.appendText(this.clientDebugPath, {
      level: entry.level || "info",
      event: entry.event || "client-debug",
      requestId: entry.requestId,
      operationId: entry.operationId,
      message: entry.message || "Client debug event",
      details: entry.details || {},
    });
  }

  async pruneTextLog(filePath) {
    try {
      const stats = await fs.stat(filePath);
      if (stats.size <= DEFAULT_TEXT_LOG_LIMIT) return;
      const fd = await fs.open(filePath, "r");
      try {
        const start = Math.max(0, stats.size - DEFAULT_TEXT_LOG_KEEP);
        const buffer = Buffer.alloc(stats.size - start);
        const { bytesRead } = await fd.read(buffer, 0, buffer.length, start);
        let text = buffer.toString("utf8", 0, bytesRead);
        const separator = text.indexOf("\n--------------------------------------------------------------------------------\n");
        if (separator >= 0) text = text.slice(separator + 82);
        await fs.writeFile(filePath, text, "utf8");
      } finally {
        await fd.close();
      }
    } catch (error) {
      if (error.code !== "ENOENT") throw error;
    }
  }

  async pruneDebugLog() {
    try {
      const limitSize = 50 * 1024 * 1024;
      const keepSize = 10 * 1024 * 1024;
      const stats = await fs.stat(this.debugPath);
      if (stats.size > limitSize) {
        const fd = await fs.open(this.debugPath, "r+");
        try {
          const buffer = Buffer.alloc(keepSize);
          const position = stats.size - keepSize;
          const { bytesRead } = await fd.read(buffer, 0, keepSize, position);
          const str = buffer.toString("utf8", 0, bytesRead);
          const firstNewline = str.indexOf("\n");
          if (firstNewline !== -1) {
            const trimmedBuffer = Buffer.from(str.substring(firstNewline + 1), "utf8");
            await fd.write(trimmedBuffer, 0, trimmedBuffer.length, 0);
            await fd.truncate(trimmedBuffer.length);
          }
        } finally {
          await fd.close();
        }
      }
    } catch (error) {
      if (error.code !== "ENOENT") console.error("Failed to prune debug log:", error);
    }
  }

  async readDebugTail({ limit = 200, connectionId = null } = {}) {
    let fd;
    try {
      const stats = await fs.stat(this.debugPath);
      const fileSize = stats.size;
      if (fileSize === 0) return [];

      fd = await fs.open(this.debugPath, "r");
      const chunkSize = 64 * 1024;
      let position = fileSize;
      let leftover = "";
      const results = [];

      while (position > 0 && results.length < limit) {
        const readLength = Math.min(position, chunkSize);
        position -= readLength;
        const buffer = Buffer.alloc(readLength);
        await fd.read(buffer, 0, readLength, position);
        const chunkStr = buffer.toString("utf8") + leftover;
        const lines = chunkStr.split("\n");
        if (position > 0) leftover = lines.shift() || "";
        else leftover = "";

        for (let i = lines.length - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
          const line = lines[i].trim();
          if (!line) continue;
          try {
            const entry = JSON.parse(line);
            if (entry && (!connectionId || entry.connectionId === connectionId)) {
              results.push(entry);
              if (results.length >= limit) break;
            }
          } catch {}
        }
      }

      if (results.length < limit && leftover.trim()) {
        try {
          const entry = JSON.parse(leftover.trim());
          if (entry && (!connectionId || entry.connectionId === connectionId)) results.push(entry);
        } catch {}
      }
      return results;
    } catch (error) {
      if (error.code === "ENOENT") return [];
      throw error;
    } finally {
      if (fd) await fd.close();
    }
  }
}

export default LogService;


// ===== src/services/userService.js =====
import { hash, verify } from "@node-rs/argon2";

class UserService {
  constructor(storageService) {
    this.storage = storageService;
  }

  async findByUsername(username) {
    const users = await this.storage.list("users");
    return users.find(u => u.username.toLowerCase() === username.toLowerCase()) || null;
  }

  async findById(id) {
    const users = await this.storage.list("users");
    return users.find(u => u.id === id) || null;
  }

  async register(username, password, { role = "user" } = {}) {
    const normalizedUsername = username.trim();
    if (!normalizedUsername || normalizedUsername.length < 2) {
      throw new Error("Username must be at least 2 characters long.");
    }
    if (!/^[a-zA-Z0-9_-]+$/.test(normalizedUsername)) {
      throw new Error("Username can only contain alphanumeric characters, underscores, or dashes.");
    }
    if (!password || password.length < 12) {
      throw new Error("Password must be at least 12 characters long.");
    }

    const existing = await this.findByUsername(normalizedUsername);
    if (existing) {
      throw new Error("Username is already taken.");
    }

    const passwordHash = await hash(password);
    const user = await this.storage.upsert("users", {
      username: normalizedUsername,
      passwordHash,
      role,
      sessionVersion: 0,
    });

    return {
      id: user.id,
      username: user.username,
      role: user.role || role,
      sessionVersion: user.sessionVersion || 0,
      createdAt: user.createdAt,
    };
  }

  async authenticate(username, password) {
    if (!username || !password) {
      return null;
    }
    const user = await this.findByUsername(username);
    if (!user) {
      return null;
    }

    const match = await verify(user.passwordHash, password);
    if (!match) {
      return null;
    }

    return {
      id: user.id,
      username: user.username,
      role: user.role || "user",
      sessionVersion: Number(user.sessionVersion || 0),
    };
  }

  async revokeSessions(userId) {
    const user = await this.storage.getById("users", userId);
    if (!user) {
      throw new Error("User not found");
    }
    const sessionVersion = Number(user.sessionVersion || 0) + 1;
    await this.storage.upsert("users", { sessionVersion }, userId);
    return { sessionVersion };
  }

  async recordLoginIp(userId, ip) {
    const user = await this.storage.getById("users", userId);
    if (!user) return null;

    const knownIps = user.knownIps || [];
    const ipHistory = user.ipHistory || [];

    const isNew = !knownIps.includes(ip);

    if (isNew) {
      knownIps.push(ip);
    }

    ipHistory.push({ ip, timestamp: new Date().toISOString() });
    if (ipHistory.length > 200) ipHistory.splice(0, ipHistory.length - 200);

    await this.storage.upsert("users", { knownIps, ipHistory }, userId);

    return { isNew, ip, knownIpCount: knownIps.length };
  }

  async listAllUsernames() {
    const users = await this.storage.list("users");
    return users.map(u => u.username);
  }
}

export default UserService;


// ===== src/services/storageService.js =====
import fs from "fs/promises";
import path from "path";
import { randomUUID } from "crypto";
import { redactSecrets } from "../security/redaction.js";

class StorageService {
  constructor(dataDir) {
    this.dataDir = dataDir;
    this.statePath = path.join(this.dataDir, "state.json");
    this.queue = Promise.resolve();
  }

  async init() {
    await fs.mkdir(this.dataDir, { recursive: true });

    try {
      await fs.access(this.statePath);
    } catch {
      await this.writeState(this.defaultState());
      return;
    }

    try {
      const state = await this.readState();
      if (!state || typeof state !== "object" || Array.isArray(state)) {
        throw new Error("State file must contain a JSON object");
      }
    } catch (error) {
      const raw = await fs.readFile(this.statePath, "utf8").catch(() => "");
      if (raw.trim()) {
        const backupPath = `${this.statePath}.corrupt-${new Date().toISOString().replaceAll(":", "-")}`;
        await fs.writeFile(backupPath, raw, "utf8");
      }
      console.error(`State file was invalid and has been reset: ${error.message}`);
      await this.writeState(this.defaultState());
    }
  }

  defaultState() {
    return {
      connections: [],
      users: [],
      sessions: [],
      quickCommands: [],
      commandHistory: [],
      uploads: [],
      llmSettings: {
        enabled: Boolean(process.env.LLM_API_KEY),
        baseUrl: process.env.LLM_BASE_URL || "https://openrouter.ai/api/v1",
        model: process.env.LLM_MODEL || "openai/gpt-5-mini",
        systemPrompt:
          process.env.LLM_SYSTEM_PROMPT ||
          "You are a concise DevOps and terminal assistant. Explain output clearly, suggest safe commands, and call out risky actions before proposing them.",
      },
    };
  }

  async withLock(task) {
    const run = this.queue.then(task, task);
    this.queue = run.then(
      () => undefined,
      () => undefined
    );
    return run;
  }

  async readState() {
    const raw = await fs.readFile(this.statePath, "utf8");
    if (!raw.trim()) {
      throw new Error("State file is empty");
    }
    return JSON.parse(raw);
  }

  async writeState(state) {
    const temporaryPath = `${this.statePath}.${process.pid}.${randomUUID()}.tmp`;
    const serialized = JSON.stringify(state, null, 2);
    await fs.writeFile(temporaryPath, serialized, { encoding: "utf8", mode: 0o600 });
    try {
      await fs.rename(temporaryPath, this.statePath);
    } catch (error) {
      if (!["EEXIST", "EPERM"].includes(error?.code)) {
        await fs.unlink(temporaryPath).catch(() => {});
        throw error;
      }
      // Windows may refuse to rename over an existing file. The temporary
      // file is already complete, so replace the destination as a fallback.
      await fs.rm(this.statePath, { force: true });
      await fs.rename(temporaryPath, this.statePath);
    }
    await fs.chmod(this.statePath, 0o600).catch(() => {});
  }

  async getState() {
    return this.withLock(() => this.readState());
  }

  async sanitizeState(state) {
    const llmSettings = { ...(state.llmSettings || {}) };
    const hasApiKey = Boolean(
      llmSettings.apiKeyEncrypted || llmSettings.apiKey || process.env.LLM_API_KEY
    );
    delete llmSettings.apiKeyEncrypted;
    delete llmSettings.apiKey;

    return {
      ...state,
      llmSettings: {
        ...llmSettings,
        apiKey: hasApiKey ? "********" : "",
        hasApiKey,
      },
      uploads: undefined,
      connections: (state.connections || []).map((item) => ({
        ...item,
        passwordEncrypted: item.passwordEncrypted ? true : false,
      })),
    };
  }

  async getClientState() {
    const state = await this.getState();
    return this.sanitizeState(state);
  }

  async list(collection) {
    const state = await this.getState();
    return state[collection] || [];
  }

  async getById(collection, id) {
    const items = await this.list(collection);
    return items.find((item) => item.id === id) || null;
  }

  async upsert(collection, payload, id = null) {
    return this.withLock(async () => {
      const state = await this.readState();
      const items = state[collection] || [];
      const now = new Date().toISOString();

      if (id) {
        const index = items.findIndex((item) => item.id === id);
        if (index === -1) {
          throw new Error(`${collection} item not found`);
        }

        items[index] = {
          ...items[index],
          ...payload,
          id,
          updatedAt: now,
        };
        state[collection] = items;
        await this.writeState(state);
        return items[index];
      }

      const created = {
        id: payload.id || randomUUID(),
        createdAt: now,
        updatedAt: now,
        ...payload,
      };

      items.unshift(created);
      state[collection] = items;
      await this.writeState(state);
      return created;
    });
  }

  async remove(collection, id) {
    return this.withLock(async () => {
      const state = await this.readState();
      const items = state[collection] || [];
      const nextItems = items.filter((item) => item.id !== id);
      state[collection] = nextItems;
      await this.writeState(state);
      return { deleted: items.length !== nextItems.length };
    });
  }

  async saveCommand(commandEntry) {
    return this.withLock(async () => {
      const state = await this.readState();
      const list = Array.isArray(state.commandHistory) ? state.commandHistory : [];
      const existingIndex = list.findIndex((item) => item.id === commandEntry.id);

      if (existingIndex >= 0) {
        list[existingIndex] = {
          ...list[existingIndex],
          ...commandEntry,
          command: redactSecrets(commandEntry.command || list[existingIndex].command || ""),
          updatedAt: new Date().toISOString(),
        };
      } else {
        list.unshift({
          id: randomUUID(),
          pinned: false,
          createdAt: new Date().toISOString(),
          updatedAt: new Date().toISOString(),
          ...commandEntry,
          command: redactSecrets(commandEntry.command || ""),
        });
      }

      state.commandHistory = list
        .sort((a, b) => new Date(b.updatedAt) - new Date(a.updatedAt))
        .slice(0, 4000);

      await this.writeState(state);
      return state.commandHistory[0];
    });
  }

  async toggleCommandPin(id) {
    return this.withLock(async () => {
      const state = await this.readState();
      const item = state.commandHistory.find((entry) => entry.id === id);
      if (!item) {
        throw new Error("Command history item not found");
      }
      item.pinned = !item.pinned;
      item.updatedAt = new Date().toISOString();
      await this.writeState(state);
      return item;
    });
  }

  async updateLlmSettings(patch) {
    return this.withLock(async () => {
      const state = await this.readState();
      const next = {
        ...(state.llmSettings || {}),
        ...patch,
        updatedAt: new Date().toISOString(),
      };
      if (Object.prototype.hasOwnProperty.call(patch, "apiKeyEncrypted")) {
        delete next.apiKey;
      }
      state.llmSettings = next;
      await this.writeState(state);
      return state.llmSettings;
    });
  }
}

export default StorageService;


// ===== src/services/terminalSessionService.js =====
class TerminalOutputBuffer {
  constructor(maxSize = 500000) {
    this.buffer = "";
    this.offset = 0;
    this.maxSize = maxSize;
  }

  append(data) {
    this.buffer += data;
    if (this.buffer.length > this.maxSize) {
      const excess = this.buffer.length - this.maxSize;
      const sliceStart = this.buffer.indexOf("\n", excess);
      if (sliceStart !== -1 && sliceStart - excess < 500) {
        this.buffer = this.buffer.slice(sliceStart + 1);
        this.offset += sliceStart + 1;
      } else {
        this.buffer = this.buffer.slice(excess);
        this.offset += excess;
      }
    }
  }

  getSince(cursor, maxLines) {
    if (cursor < this.offset) {
      return { data: "", cursor: this.offset, reset: true };
    }

    const adjusted = cursor - this.offset;
    if (adjusted >= this.buffer.length) {
      return { data: "", cursor: this.offset + this.buffer.length };
    }

    let data = this.buffer.slice(adjusted);
    let newCursor = cursor + data.length;

    if (maxLines > 0) {
      const lines = data.split("\n");
      if (lines.length > maxLines) {
        lines.length = maxLines;
        data = lines.join("\n");
        if (data.length > 0) data += "\n";
        newCursor = cursor + data.length;
      }
    }

    return { data, cursor: newCursor };
  }

  getCurrentCursor() {
    return this.offset + this.buffer.length;
  }
}

class TerminalSessionService {
  constructor(sshService) {
    this.sshService = sshService;
    this.buffers = new Map();
    this.execCallbacks = new Map();

    this._onTerminalData = this._onTerminalData.bind(this);
    this._onTerminalClosed = this._onTerminalClosed.bind(this);

    sshService.on("terminal:data", this._onTerminalData);
    sshService.on("terminal:closed", this._onTerminalClosed);
  }

  async createSession({ connectionId, cols, rows, title, authOverrides, ownerId, privateMode = false }) {
    const result = await this.sshService.createTerminal({
      connectionId,
      cols: cols || 120,
      rows: rows || 30,
      title,
      authOverrides,
      ownerId,
      privateMode,
    });

    this.buffers.set(result.terminalId, new TerminalOutputBuffer());

    return result;
  }


  requireOwnedTerminal(terminalId, ownerId) {
    const terminal = this.sshService.terminals.get(terminalId);
    if (!terminal) {
      const error = new Error("Terminal not found");
      error.statusCode = 404;
      throw error;
    }
    if (!ownerId || terminal.ownerId !== ownerId) {
      const error = new Error("Access denied to terminal");
      error.statusCode = 403;
      throw error;
    }
    return terminal;
  }

  static _keyToSequence(key) {
    const map = {
      "ctrl+space": "\x00",
      "ctrl+a": "\x01", "ctrl+b": "\x02", "ctrl+c": "\x03", "ctrl+d": "\x04",
      "ctrl+e": "\x05", "ctrl+f": "\x06", "ctrl+g": "\x07", "ctrl+h": "\x08",
      "ctrl+i": "\x09", "ctrl+j": "\x0a", "ctrl+k": "\x0b", "ctrl+l": "\x0c",
      "ctrl+m": "\x0d", "ctrl+n": "\x0e", "ctrl+o": "\x0f", "ctrl+p": "\x10",
      "ctrl+q": "\x11", "ctrl+r": "\x12", "ctrl+s": "\x13", "ctrl+t": "\x14",
      "ctrl+u": "\x15", "ctrl+v": "\x16", "ctrl+w": "\x17", "ctrl+x": "\x18",
      "ctrl+y": "\x19", "ctrl+z": "\x1a",
      "ctrl+[": "\x1b", "ctrl+\\": "\x1c", "ctrl+]": "\x1d", "ctrl+^": "\x1e",
      "ctrl+/": "\x1f",
      "enter": "\r", "return": "\r",
      "tab": "\t",
      "escape": "\x1b", "esc": "\x1b",
      "backspace": "\x7f",
      "up": "\x1b[A", "down": "\x1b[B", "right": "\x1b[C", "left": "\x1b[D",
      "home": "\x1b[H", "end": "\x1b[F",
      "delete": "\x1b[3~", "del": "\x1b[3~",
      "pageup": "\x1b[5~", "pagedown": "\x1b[6~",
      "insert": "\x1b[2~", "ins": "\x1b[2~",
    };
    return map[key.toLowerCase().replace(/\s+/g, "")] || "";
  }

  input(terminalId, data, meta = {}) {
    this.requireOwnedTerminal(terminalId, meta.ownerId);
    let payload = data || "";
    if (Array.isArray(meta.keys)) {
      for (const key of meta.keys) {
        payload += TerminalSessionService._keyToSequence(key);
      }
    }
    this.sshService.input(terminalId, payload, { source: "api", ...meta });
  }

  async exec(terminalId, command, options = {}) {
    this.requireOwnedTerminal(terminalId, options.ownerId);

    const timeout = Math.min(options.timeout || 10000, 120000);

    const existing = this.execCallbacks.get(terminalId);
    if (existing) {
      clearTimeout(existing.timer);
      if (!existing.resolved) {
        existing.resolved = true;
        existing.resolve({ output: existing.buffer, truncated: false, timedOut: false, replaced: true });
      }
    }

    this.sshService.input(terminalId, command + "\n", { source: "api:exec", ownerId: options.ownerId });

    return new Promise((resolve) => {
      const execCtx = {
        command,
        buffer: "",
        resolved: false,
        resolve,
        timer: setTimeout(() => {
          if (execCtx.resolved) return;
          execCtx.resolved = true;
          this.execCallbacks.delete(terminalId);
          resolve({ output: execCtx.buffer, truncated: false, timedOut: true });
        }, timeout),
      };

      this.execCallbacks.set(terminalId, execCtx);
    });
  }

  getOutput(terminalId, cursor = 0, maxLines = 0, ownerId = "") {
    this.requireOwnedTerminal(terminalId, ownerId);
    const buf = this.buffers.get(terminalId);
    if (!buf) {
      throw new Error("Terminal session not found");
    }
    const result = buf.getSince(cursor, maxLines);
    const terminal = this.sshService.terminals.get(terminalId);
    result.eof = !terminal;
    return result;
  }

  async closeSession(terminalId, ownerId = "") {
    this.requireOwnedTerminal(terminalId, ownerId);
    const execCtx = this.execCallbacks.get(terminalId);
    if (execCtx) {
      clearTimeout(execCtx.timer);
      if (!execCtx.resolved) {
        execCtx.resolved = true;
        execCtx.resolve({ output: execCtx.buffer, truncated: false, timedOut: false, closed: true });
      }
      this.execCallbacks.delete(terminalId);
    }

    this.buffers.delete(terminalId);
    await this.sshService.closeTerminal(terminalId, true, ownerId);
  }

  listSessions(userId) {
    return this.sshService
      .listActiveTerminals()
      .filter((t) => t.ownerId === userId)
      .map((t) => ({
        terminalId: t.terminalId,
        connectionId: t.connectionId,
        connectionName: t.connectionName,
        title: t.title,
        createdAt: t.createdAt,
        privateMode: Boolean(t.privateMode),
        cursor: this.buffers.get(t.terminalId)?.getCurrentCursor() || 0,
      }));
  }

  getSession(terminalId, userId) {
    const terminal = this.sshService.terminals.get(terminalId);
    if (!terminal || terminal.ownerId !== userId) {
      return null;
    }
    return {
      terminalId: terminal.terminalId,
      connectionId: terminal.connectionId,
      connectionName: terminal.connectionName,
      title: terminal.title,
      createdAt: terminal.createdAt,
      privateMode: Boolean(terminal.privateMode),
      cursor: this.buffers.get(terminalId)?.getCurrentCursor() || 0,
    };
  }

  _onTerminalData({ terminalId, data }) {
    const buf = this.buffers.get(terminalId);
    if (buf) {
      buf.append(data);
    }

    const execCtx = this.execCallbacks.get(terminalId);
    if (execCtx && !execCtx.resolved) {
      execCtx.buffer += data;
    }
  }

  _onTerminalClosed({ terminalId }) {
    const execCtx = this.execCallbacks.get(terminalId);
    if (execCtx && !execCtx.resolved) {
      clearTimeout(execCtx.timer);
      execCtx.resolved = true;
      this.execCallbacks.delete(terminalId);
      execCtx.resolve({ output: execCtx.buffer, truncated: false, timedOut: false, closed: true });
    }
  }
}

export default TerminalSessionService;


// ===== src/services/gitService.js =====
function shellQuote(value = "") {
  return `'${String(value).replace(/'/g, `'\\''`)}'`;
}

function toGitCommand(repoPath, command) {
  return `git -C ${shellQuote(repoPath || ".")} ${command}`;
}

function compactOutput(result = {}) {
  return [result.stderr, result.stdout].filter(Boolean).join("\n").trim();
}

function normalizeFileList(files) {
  return (Array.isArray(files) ? files : [files])
    .map((file) => String(file || "").trim())
    .filter(Boolean);
}

function fileArgs(files) {
  return normalizeFileList(files).map(shellQuote).join(" ");
}

function mapGitStatus(code) {
  const statusMap = {
    ".": null,
    " ": null,
    M: "modified",
    A: "added",
    D: "deleted",
    R: "renamed",
    C: "copied",
    T: "typechanged",
    U: "unmerged",
    "?": "untracked",
    "!": "ignored",
  };
  return Object.hasOwn(statusMap, code) ? statusMap[code] : "modified";
}

function parseBranchHeader(line = "", metadata) {
  const rest = line.slice(2);
  const firstSpace = rest.indexOf(" ");
  const key = firstSpace === -1 ? rest : rest.slice(0, firstSpace);
  const value = firstSpace === -1 ? "" : rest.slice(firstSpace + 1);

  if (key === "branch.oid") metadata.oid = value;
  if (key === "branch.head") metadata.branch = value === "(detached)" ? "detached" : value;
  if (key === "branch.upstream") metadata.upstream = value;
  if (key === "branch.ab") {
    const match = value.match(/\+(\d+)\s+-(\d+)/);
    metadata.ahead = match ? Number(match[1]) : 0;
    metadata.behind = match ? Number(match[2]) : 0;
  }
}

function parseOrdinaryRecord(record = "", type = "1") {
  const fieldCount = type === "2" ? 9 : 8;
  const fields = record.split(" ");
  const statusCode = fields[1] || "..";
  const filename = fields.slice(fieldCount).join(" ");
  return { statusCode, filename };
}

function addChange(changes, file) {
  if (!file?.filename) return;
  if (file.status === "untracked") {
    changes.untracked.push(file);
  } else if (file.staged) {
    changes.staged.push(file);
  } else {
    changes.unstaged.push(file);
  }
}

function parsePorcelainV2Status(stdout = "") {
  const records = String(stdout || "").split("\0").filter(Boolean);
  const metadata = {
    branch: "unknown",
    upstream: "",
    ahead: 0,
    behind: 0,
    oid: "",
  };
  const changes = { staged: [], unstaged: [], untracked: [] };

  for (let index = 0; index < records.length; index += 1) {
    const record = records[index];
    if (record.startsWith("# ")) {
      parseBranchHeader(record, metadata);
      continue;
    }

    if (record.startsWith("? ")) {
      addChange(changes, {
        filename: record.slice(2),
        status: "untracked",
        staged: false,
        kind: "untracked",
      });
      continue;
    }

    if (record.startsWith("! ")) {
      continue;
    }

    if (record.startsWith("1 ") || record.startsWith("2 ")) {
      const isRename = record.startsWith("2 ");
      const { statusCode, filename } = parseOrdinaryRecord(record, isRename ? "2" : "1");
      const indexCode = statusCode[0] || ".";
      const worktreeCode = statusCode[1] || ".";
      const originalFilename = isRename ? records[index + 1] || "" : "";
      if (isRename && originalFilename) {
        index += 1;
      }

      if (mapGitStatus(indexCode)) {
        addChange(changes, {
          filename,
          originalFilename,
          status: mapGitStatus(indexCode),
          staged: true,
          kind: "tracked",
        });
      }
      if (mapGitStatus(worktreeCode)) {
        addChange(changes, {
          filename,
          originalFilename,
          status: mapGitStatus(worktreeCode),
          staged: false,
          kind: "tracked",
        });
      }
      continue;
    }

    if (record.startsWith("u ")) {
      const fields = record.split(" ");
      const filename = fields.slice(10).join(" ");
      addChange(changes, {
        filename,
        status: "unmerged",
        staged: false,
        kind: "unmerged",
      });
    }
  }

  return {
    ...metadata,
    ...changes,
    totalChanges: changes.staged.length + changes.unstaged.length + changes.untracked.length,
  };
}

function parseLog(stdout = "") {
  return String(stdout || "")
    .split("\n")
    .filter(Boolean)
    .map((line) => {
      const [hash = "", subject = "", author = "", relativeDate = ""] = line.split("\x1f");
      return { hash, message: subject, author, relativeDate };
    });
}

function parseBranches(stdout = "") {
  return String(stdout || "")
    .split("\n")
    .filter(Boolean)
    .map((line) => {
      const [currentFlag = "", name = "", upstream = "", tracking = ""] = line.split("\x1f");
      const aheadMatch = tracking.match(/ahead\s+(\d+)/);
      const behindMatch = tracking.match(/behind\s+(\d+)/);
      return {
        name,
        current: currentFlag === "*",
        upstream,
        ahead: aheadMatch ? Number(aheadMatch[1]) : 0,
        behind: behindMatch ? Number(behindMatch[1]) : 0,
      };
    });
}

class GitService {
  constructor({ sshService }) {
    this.sshService = sshService;
  }

  async run(connectionId, repoPath, command, authOverrides = {}) {
    return this.sshService.executeRemoteCommand(connectionId, toGitCommand(repoPath, command), authOverrides);
  }

  async runChecked(connectionId, repoPath, command, authOverrides = {}) {
    const result = await this.run(connectionId, repoPath, command, authOverrides);
    if (result.code !== 0) {
      throw new Error(compactOutput(result) || `git command failed with code ${result.code}`);
    }
    return result;
  }

  async discover(connectionId, cwd = ".", authOverrides = {}) {
    const command = [
      `cd ${shellQuote(cwd || ".")}`,
      "git rev-parse --is-inside-work-tree",
      "printf '\\037'",
      "git rev-parse --show-toplevel",
      "printf '\\037'",
      "git rev-parse --show-prefix",
      "printf '\\037'",
      "(git symbolic-ref --quiet --short HEAD || git rev-parse --short HEAD)",
      "printf '\\037'",
      "(git rev-parse --abbrev-ref --symbolic-full-name @{u} 2>/dev/null || true)",
    ].join(" && ");

    const result = await this.sshService.executeRemoteCommand(connectionId, command, authOverrides);
    if (result.code !== 0) {
      return {
        ok: false,
        isRepo: false,
        cwd,
        repoRoot: "",
        relativePath: "",
        branch: "",
        upstream: "",
        error: compactOutput(result) || "Not inside a git repository.",
      };
    }

    const [inside = "", repoRoot = "", relativePath = "", branch = "", upstream = ""] = result.stdout.split("\x1f");
    return {
      ok: true,
      isRepo: inside.trim() === "true",
      cwd,
      repoRoot: repoRoot.trim(),
      relativePath: relativePath.trim().replace(/\/$/, ""),
      branch: branch.trim(),
      upstream: upstream.trim(),
    };
  }

  async status(connectionId, repoPath, authOverrides = {}) {
    const [discover, statusResult] = await Promise.all([
      this.discover(connectionId, repoPath, authOverrides),
      this.run(connectionId, repoPath, "status --porcelain=v2 --branch -z", authOverrides),
    ]);

    if (!discover.isRepo || statusResult.code !== 0) {
      throw new Error(discover.error || compactOutput(statusResult) || "Not inside a git repository.");
    }

    const status = parsePorcelainV2Status(statusResult.stdout || "");
    return {
      ...status,
      cwd: repoPath || ".",
      repoRoot: discover.repoRoot,
      relativePath: discover.relativePath,
      branch: status.branch === "unknown" ? discover.branch || "unknown" : status.branch,
      upstream: status.upstream || discover.upstream,
      isRepo: true,
    };
  }

  async diff(connectionId, repoPath, { staged = false, filename = "", binarySummary = true } = {}, authOverrides = {}) {
    const scope = staged ? "--cached" : "";
    const fileArg = filename ? ` -- ${shellQuote(filename)}` : "";
    const binaryFlag = binarySummary ? "--stat --summary" : "";
    const command = `diff --color=never --no-ext-diff ${scope}${fileArg}`;
    const result = await this.run(connectionId, repoPath, command, authOverrides);
    const diff = result.stdout || "";
    if (result.code !== 0 && !diff) {
      throw new Error(compactOutput(result) || `git diff failed with code ${result.code}`);
    }
    if (!diff && binarySummary) {
      const summary = await this.run(connectionId, repoPath, `diff --color=never --no-ext-diff ${binaryFlag} ${scope}${fileArg}`, authOverrides);
      return { diff: summary.stdout || "(no diff)", isBinarySummary: true };
    }
    if (/^Binary files /m.test(diff)) {
      const summary = await this.run(connectionId, repoPath, `diff --color=never --no-ext-diff ${binaryFlag} ${scope}${fileArg}`, authOverrides);
      return { diff: [diff, summary.stdout].filter(Boolean).join("\n"), isBinarySummary: true };
    }
    return { diff };
  }

  async log(connectionId, repoPath, { count = 30 } = {}, authOverrides = {}) {
    const safeCount = Math.max(1, Math.min(200, Number(count) || 30));
    const result = await this.runChecked(
      connectionId,
      repoPath,
      `log --format='%h%x1f%s%x1f%an%x1f%cr' -n ${safeCount}`,
      authOverrides
    );
    return { commits: parseLog(result.stdout) };
  }

  async stage(connectionId, repoPath, files, authOverrides = {}) {
    const args = fileArgs(files);
    if (!args) throw new Error("No files to stage");
    await this.runChecked(connectionId, repoPath, `add -- ${args}`, authOverrides);
    return { ok: true };
  }

  async unstage(connectionId, repoPath, files, authOverrides = {}) {
    const args = fileArgs(files);
    if (!args) throw new Error("No files to unstage");
    await this.runChecked(connectionId, repoPath, `restore --staged -- ${args}`, authOverrides);
    return { ok: true };
  }

  async discard(connectionId, repoPath, files, authOverrides = {}) {
    const fileList = normalizeFileList(files);
    if (fileList.length === 0) throw new Error("No files to discard");

    const status = await this.status(connectionId, repoPath, authOverrides);
    const untracked = new Set(status.untracked.map((file) => file.filename));
    const trackedFiles = fileList.filter((file) => !untracked.has(file));
    const untrackedFiles = fileList.filter((file) => untracked.has(file));

    const outputs = [];
    if (trackedFiles.length) {
      const result = await this.runChecked(connectionId, repoPath, `restore --worktree -- ${fileArgs(trackedFiles)}`, authOverrides);
      outputs.push(result.stdout || result.stderr || "");
    }
    if (untrackedFiles.length) {
      const result = await this.runChecked(connectionId, repoPath, `clean -f -- ${fileArgs(untrackedFiles)}`, authOverrides);
      outputs.push(result.stdout || result.stderr || "");
    }

    return { ok: true, output: outputs.filter(Boolean).join("\n") };
  }

  async commit(connectionId, repoPath, message, authOverrides = {}) {
    if (!message?.trim()) throw new Error("Commit message is required");
    const result = await this.runChecked(connectionId, repoPath, `commit -m ${shellQuote(message.trim())}`, authOverrides);
    return { ok: true, message: message.trim(), output: result.stdout || result.stderr || "" };
  }

  async push(connectionId, repoPath, { remote = "origin", branch = "", force = false } = {}, authOverrides = {}) {
    const branchArg = branch ? ` ${shellQuote(branch)}` : "";
    const forceFlag = force ? " --force-with-lease" : "";
    const result = await this.run(connectionId, repoPath, `push${forceFlag} ${shellQuote(remote || "origin")}${branchArg}`, authOverrides);
    return { ok: result.code === 0, output: result.stdout || "", error: result.stderr || "" };
  }

  async pull(connectionId, repoPath, { remote = "origin", branch = "" } = {}, authOverrides = {}) {
    const branchArg = branch ? ` ${shellQuote(branch)}` : "";
    const result = await this.run(connectionId, repoPath, `pull ${shellQuote(remote || "origin")}${branchArg}`, authOverrides);
    return { ok: result.code === 0, output: result.stdout || "", error: result.stderr || "" };
  }

  async fetch(connectionId, repoPath, { remote = "origin" } = {}, authOverrides = {}) {
    const result = await this.run(connectionId, repoPath, `fetch --prune ${shellQuote(remote || "origin")}`, authOverrides);
    return { ok: result.code === 0, output: result.stdout || "", error: result.stderr || "" };
  }

  async merge(connectionId, repoPath, branch, authOverrides = {}) {
    if (!branch) throw new Error("Branch is required");
    const result = await this.run(connectionId, repoPath, `merge ${shellQuote(branch)}`, authOverrides);
    return { ok: result.code === 0, output: result.stdout || "", error: result.stderr || "" };
  }

  async branches(connectionId, repoPath, authOverrides = {}) {
    const format = "%(HEAD)%x1f%(refname:short)%x1f%(upstream:short)%x1f%(upstream:track)";
    const result = await this.runChecked(connectionId, repoPath, `for-each-ref --format=${shellQuote(format)} refs/heads refs/remotes`, authOverrides);
    return { branches: parseBranches(result.stdout) };
  }

  async remoteStatus(connectionId, repoPath, authOverrides = {}) {
    const result = await this.run(connectionId, repoPath, "remote -v", authOverrides);
    const remotes = result.stdout.trim().split("\n").filter(Boolean).map((line) => {
      const parts = line.split(/\s+/);
      return { name: parts[0] || "", url: parts[1] || "", type: parts[2]?.replace(/[()]/g, "") || "" };
    });
    return { remotes };
  }

  async stashList(connectionId, repoPath, authOverrides = {}) {
    const result = await this.run(connectionId, repoPath, `stash list --format=${shellQuote("%gd%x1f%gs")}`, authOverrides);
    const stashes = result.stdout.trim().split("\n").filter(Boolean).map((line) => {
      const [ref = "", message = ""] = line.split("\x1f");
      return { ref, message };
    });
    return { stashes };
  }

  async stash(connectionId, repoPath, authOverrides = {}) {
    const result = await this.run(connectionId, repoPath, "stash push -u", authOverrides);
    return { ok: result.code === 0, output: result.stdout || result.stderr || "" };
  }

  async stashPop(connectionId, repoPath, authOverrides = {}) {
    const result = await this.run(connectionId, repoPath, "stash pop", authOverrides);
    return { ok: result.code === 0, output: result.stdout || result.stderr || "" };
  }
}

export {
  shellQuote,
  parsePorcelainV2Status,
  parseLog,
  parseBranches,
};

export default GitService;


// ===== src/security/loginRateLimiter.js =====
class LoginRateLimiter {
  constructor({ maxAttempts = 5, windowMs = 15 * 60 * 1000, lockMs = 15 * 60 * 1000 } = {}) {
    this.maxAttempts = maxAttempts;
    this.windowMs = windowMs;
    this.lockMs = lockMs;
    this.entries = new Map();
  }

  key(ip = "unknown", username = "") {
    return `${String(ip).toLowerCase()}::${String(username).trim().toLowerCase()}`;
  }

  inspect(ip, username, now = Date.now()) {
    const key = this.key(ip, username);
    const entry = this.entries.get(key);
    if (!entry) {
      return { allowed: true, retryAfterMs: 0 };
    }

    if (entry.lockedUntil > now) {
      return { allowed: false, retryAfterMs: entry.lockedUntil - now };
    }

    if (now - entry.windowStartedAt > this.windowMs) {
      this.entries.delete(key);
      return { allowed: true, retryAfterMs: 0 };
    }

    return { allowed: true, retryAfterMs: 0 };
  }

  recordFailure(ip, username, now = Date.now()) {
    const key = this.key(ip, username);
    let entry = this.entries.get(key);
    if (!entry || now - entry.windowStartedAt > this.windowMs) {
      entry = { attempts: 0, windowStartedAt: now, lockedUntil: 0 };
    }

    entry.attempts += 1;
    if (entry.attempts >= this.maxAttempts) {
      entry.lockedUntil = now + this.lockMs;
    }
    this.entries.set(key, entry);
    return this.inspect(ip, username, now);
  }

  reset(ip, username) {
    this.entries.delete(this.key(ip, username));
  }

  prune(now = Date.now()) {
    for (const [key, entry] of this.entries.entries()) {
      const expiry = Math.max(entry.lockedUntil || 0, entry.windowStartedAt + this.windowMs);
      if (expiry <= now) {
        this.entries.delete(key);
      }
    }
  }
}

export default LoginRateLimiter;


// ===== src/security/redaction.js =====
const SECRET_ASSIGNMENT_PATTERN = /\b(password|passwd|pwd|token|api[_-]?key|secret|authorization|access[_-]?token|refresh[_-]?token|client[_-]?secret)\b(\s*[:=]\s*)([^\s'";]+)/gi;
const BEARER_PATTERN = /\b(Bearer\s+)[A-Za-z0-9._~+\/-]+=*/gi;
const URL_CREDENTIAL_PATTERN = /(https?:\/\/[^\s:/]+:)([^@\s]+)(@)/gi;
const PRIVATE_KEY_PATTERN = /-----BEGIN [^-]*PRIVATE KEY-----[\s\S]*?-----END [^-]*PRIVATE KEY-----/g;
const COMMON_TOKEN_PATTERN = /\b(sk-(?:or-v1-)?[A-Za-z0-9_-]{16,}|gh[pousr]_[A-Za-z0-9_]{20,}|xox[baprs]-[A-Za-z0-9-]{20,})\b/g;

export function redactSecrets(value = "") {
  return String(value)
    .replace(PRIVATE_KEY_PATTERN, "[REDACTED PRIVATE KEY]")
    .replace(BEARER_PATTERN, "$1[REDACTED]")
    .replace(URL_CREDENTIAL_PATTERN, "$1[REDACTED]$3")
    .replace(SECRET_ASSIGNMENT_PATTERN, "$1$2[REDACTED]")
    .replace(COMMON_TOKEN_PATTERN, "[REDACTED TOKEN]");
}

export function commandContainsLikelySecret(value = "") {
  const text = String(value);
  return [
    PRIVATE_KEY_PATTERN,
    BEARER_PATTERN,
    URL_CREDENTIAL_PATTERN,
    SECRET_ASSIGNMENT_PATTERN,
    COMMON_TOKEN_PATTERN,
  ].some((pattern) => {
    pattern.lastIndex = 0;
    return pattern.test(text);
  });
}


// ===== src/server.js =====
import "dotenv/config";
import express from "express";
import http from "http";
import path from "path";
import fs from "fs/promises";
import { existsSync } from "fs";
import crypto from "crypto";
import multer from "multer";
import { Server as SocketIOServer } from "socket.io";
import { fileURLToPath } from "url";

import StorageService from "./services/storageService.js";
import CryptoService from "./services/cryptoService.js";
import KeyStoreService from "./services/keyStoreService.js";
import LogService from "./services/logService.js";
import LlmService from "./services/llmService.js";
import SshService from "./services/sshService.js";
import UserService from "./services/userService.js";
import TerminalSessionService from "./services/terminalSessionService.js";
import GitService from "./services/gitService.js";
import { sendWoL } from "./services/wolService.js";
import LoginRateLimiter from "./security/loginRateLimiter.js";
import { redactSecrets } from "./security/redaction.js";

const __filename = fileURLToPath(import.meta.url);
const __dirname = path.dirname(__filename);
const projectRoot = path.resolve(__dirname, "..");
const dataDir = path.resolve(projectRoot, process.env.APP_DATA_DIR || "./data");
const uploadDir = path.join(dataDir, "uploads");
const quickUploadDir = path.join(uploadDir, "tmp");
const keyDir = path.join(dataDir, "keys");
const logDir = path.join(dataDir, "logs");

function requireStrongSecret() {
  const value = String(process.env.UI_AUTH_SECRET || process.env.APP_SECRET || "").trim();
  if (Buffer.byteLength(value, "utf8") < 32) {
    throw new Error(
      "UI_AUTH_SECRET (or APP_SECRET) must be set to a random value of at least 32 bytes."
    );
  }
  return value;
}

function parseTrustProxy(value = "") {
  const normalized = String(value).trim().toLowerCase();
  if (!normalized || normalized === "false" || normalized === "0") return false;
  if (normalized === "true") return true;
  if (/^\d+$/.test(normalized)) return Number(normalized);
  return value;
}

const authSecret = requireStrongSecret();
const authCookieName = "rth_auth";
const authSessionMs = Number(process.env.UI_AUTH_MAX_AGE_MS || 7 * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000);
const registrationMode = String(process.env.REGISTRATION_MODE || "first-user").toLowerCase();
const quickUploadTtlMs = Math.min(
  Math.max(Number(process.env.QUICK_UPLOAD_TTL_MS || 60 * 60 * 1000), 60_000),
  24 * 60 * 60 * 1000
);

const app = express();
app.set("trust proxy", parseTrustProxy(process.env.TRUST_PROXY));
const server = http.createServer(app);
const io = new SocketIOServer(server, {
  maxHttpBufferSize: 10 * 1024 * 1024,
});

const keyUpload = multer({
  dest: uploadDir,
  limits: { fileSize: Number(process.env.MAX_PRIVATE_KEY_BYTES || 256 * 1024), files: 1 },
});

const fileUpload = multer({
  dest: uploadDir,
  limits: { fileSize: Number(process.env.MAX_UPLOAD_BYTES || 100 * 1024 * 1024), files: 1 },
});

const quickUpload = multer({
  storage: multer.diskStorage({
    destination: quickUploadDir,
    filename(_req, file, cb) {
      const id = crypto.randomUUID();
      const safeName = file.originalname.replace(/[^a-zA-Z0-9._-]/g, "-").slice(0, 100);
      cb(null, `${id}-${safeName}`);
    },
  }),
  limits: { fileSize: 50 * 1024 * 1024 },
});

const storage = new StorageService(dataDir);
const cryptoService = new CryptoService(dataDir);
const keyStore = new KeyStoreService({ keyDir, cryptoService });
const logService = new LogService(logDir);
const llmService = new LlmService({ storage, cryptoService });
const sshService = new SshService({
  storage,
  keyStore,
  cryptoService,
  logService,
  uploadDir,
});
const userService = new UserService(storage);
const terminalSessionService = new TerminalSessionService(sshService);

const loginRateLimiter = new LoginRateLimiter({
  maxAttempts: Number(process.env.LOGIN_MAX_ATTEMPTS || 5),
  windowMs: Number(process.env.LOGIN_WINDOW_MS || 15 * 60 * 1000),
  lockMs: Number(process.env.LOGIN_LOCK_MS || 15 * 60 * 1000),
});

await storage.init();
await ensureUserRoles();
await keyStore.init();
await fs.mkdir(uploadDir, { recursive: true });
await fs.mkdir(quickUploadDir, { recursive: true });
await fs.mkdir(logDir, { recursive: true });
await ensureInitialUser();

function logFatalProcessError(event, error) {
  const normalized = error instanceof Error ? error : new Error(String(error || "Unknown process error"));
  logService.appendServerError(normalized, { event }).catch((logError) => {
    console.error("Failed to persist fatal server error:", logError);
  });
  console.error(`[${event}]`, normalized);
}

process.on("unhandledRejection", (reason) => {
  logFatalProcessError("unhandled-rejection", reason);
});

process.on("uncaughtException", (error) => {
  logFatalProcessError("uncaught-exception", error);
  process.exitCode = 1;
  setTimeout(() => process.exit(1), 750).unref();
});

app.use(express.json({ limit: "5mb" }));
app.use(express.urlencoded({ extended: true, limit: "5mb" }));
app.use((req, res, next) => {
  const supplied = String(req.headers["x-request-id"] || "").trim();
  req.requestId = /^[a-zA-Z0-9._:-]{6,128}$/.test(supplied) ? supplied : crypto.randomUUID();
  req.requestStartedAt = Date.now();
  res.setHeader("X-Request-Id", req.requestId);
  next();
});
app.use((req, res, next) => {
  res.setHeader("X-Content-Type-Options", "nosniff");
  res.setHeader("X-Frame-Options", "DENY");
  res.setHeader("Referrer-Policy", "same-origin");
  res.setHeader("Permissions-Policy", "camera=(), microphone=(), geolocation=()");
  next();
});
app.use(enforceSameOrigin);

function safeEqual(a = "", b = "") {
  const left = Buffer.from(String(a));
  const right = Buffer.from(String(b));
  return left.length === right.length && crypto.timingSafeEqual(left, right);
}

function signAuthSession(userId, createdAt, sessionVersion) {
  return crypto
    .createHmac("sha256", authSecret)
    .update(`${userId}.${createdAt}.${sessionVersion}`)
    .digest("base64url");
}

function createAuthCookieValue(user) {
  const createdAt = Date.now();
  const sessionVersion = Number(user.sessionVersion || 0);
  return `${user.id}.${createdAt}.${sessionVersion}.${signAuthSession(user.id, createdAt, sessionVersion)}`;
}

function parseCookies(cookieHeader = "") {
  try {
    return Object.fromEntries(
      String(cookieHeader)
        .split(";")
        .map((item) => item.trim())
        .filter(Boolean)
        .map((item) => {
          const index = item.indexOf("=");
          if (index === -1) {
            return [item, ""];
          }
          return [decodeURIComponent(item.slice(0, index)), decodeURIComponent(item.slice(index + 1))];
        })
    );
  } catch {
    return {};
  }
}

async function getAuthenticatedUser(req) {
  const cookieValue = parseCookies(req.headers.cookie || "")[authCookieName];
  if (!cookieValue) {
    return null;
  }
  const parts = cookieValue.split(".");
  if (parts.length !== 4) {
    return null;
  }
  const [userId, createdAtRaw, sessionVersionRaw, signature] = parts;
  const createdAt = Number(createdAtRaw);
  const sessionVersion = Number(sessionVersionRaw);
  if (!Number.isFinite(createdAt) || createdAt > Date.now() + 60_000 || Date.now() - createdAt > authSessionMs) {
    return null;
  }
  if (!Number.isInteger(sessionVersion) || !safeEqual(signature || "", signAuthSession(userId, createdAt, sessionVersion))) {
    return null;
  }
  const user = await userService.findById(userId);
  if (!user || Number(user.sessionVersion || 0) !== sessionVersion) {
    return null;
  }
  return { id: user.id, username: user.username, role: user.role || "user", sessionVersion };
}

function setAuthCookie(req, res, user) {
  const secure = req.secure;
  res.cookie(authCookieName, createAuthCookieValue(user), {
    httpOnly: true,
    sameSite: "lax",
    secure,
    maxAge: authSessionMs,
    path: "/",
  });
}

function clearAuthCookie(res) {
  res.clearCookie(authCookieName, {
    httpOnly: true,
    sameSite: "lax",
    path: "/",
  });
}

async function requireUiAuth(req, res, next) {
  const user = await getAuthenticatedUser(req);
  if (user) {
    req.user = user;
    next();
    return;
  }
  if (req.path.startsWith("/api/")) {
    res.status(401).json({ error: "Authentication required" });
    return;
  }
  res.redirect(`/login?next=${encodeURIComponent(req.originalUrl || "/")}`);
}

function requireAdmin(req, res, next) {
  if (req.user?.role !== "admin") {
    res.status(403).json({ error: "Administrator access is required." });
    return;
  }
  next();
}

async function migrateUnownedData(userId) {
  try {
    const state = await storage.readState();
    let changed = false;

    const collectionsToMigrate = ["connections", "sessions", "quickCommands", "commandHistory"];
    for (const coll of collectionsToMigrate) {
      if (Array.isArray(state[coll])) {
        for (const item of state[coll]) {
          if (!item.ownerId) {
            item.ownerId = userId;
            changed = true;
          }
        }
      }
    }

    if (changed) {
      await storage.writeState(state);
      console.info(`Migrated unowned state collections to user: ${userId}`);
    }

    const keys = await keyStore.listKeys();
    for (const key of keys) {
      const filePath = keyStore.keyPath(key.id);
      try {
        const raw = await fs.readFile(filePath, "utf8");
        const parsed = JSON.parse(raw);
        if (!parsed.ownerId) {
          parsed.ownerId = userId;
          await fs.writeFile(filePath, JSON.stringify(parsed, null, 2), "utf8");
          console.info(`Migrated unowned SSH key ${key.id} to user: ${userId}`);
        }
      } catch (err) {
        console.error(`Failed to migrate key file ${key.id}:`, err);
      }
    }
  } catch (error) {
    console.error("Migration error:", error);
  }
}

async function ensureUserRoles() {
  const state = await storage.readState();
  const users = Array.isArray(state.users) ? state.users : [];
  let changed = false;
  users.forEach((user, index) => {
    if (!user.role) {
      user.role = index === users.length - 1 ? "admin" : "user";
      changed = true;
    }
    if (!Number.isInteger(user.sessionVersion)) {
      user.sessionVersion = 0;
      changed = true;
    }
  });
  if (changed) {
    state.users = users;
    await storage.writeState(state);
  }
}

async function ensureInitialUser() {
  const users = await storage.list("users");
  if (users.length > 0 || !process.env.UI_PASSWORD) {
    return;
  }

  const username = (process.env.UI_USERNAME || "admin").trim();
  const user = await userService.register(username, process.env.UI_PASSWORD, { role: "admin" });
  await migrateUnownedData(user.id);
  console.info(`Created initial UI user "${username}" from UI_PASSWORD.`);
}

async function isRegistrationAvailable() {
  if (registrationMode === "open") return true;
  if (registrationMode === "disabled") return false;
  const users = await storage.list("users");
  return users.length === 0;
}

function expectedOrigins(req) {
  const configured = String(process.env.ALLOWED_ORIGINS || "")
    .split(",")
    .map((value) => value.trim())
    .filter(Boolean);
  const protocol = req.secure ? "https" : "http";
  return new Set([...configured, `${protocol}://${req.get("host")}`]);
}

function enforceSameOrigin(req, res, next) {
  if (!["POST", "PUT", "PATCH", "DELETE"].includes(req.method)) {
    next();
    return;
  }
  if (process.env.DISABLE_ORIGIN_CHECK === "1") {
    next();
    return;
  }
  const origin = req.get("origin");
  if (!origin) {
    next();
    return;
  }
  if (!expectedOrigins(req).has(origin)) {
    res.status(403).json({ error: "Request origin was not allowed." });
    return;
  }
  next();
}

function signQuickUpload(id, expiresAt) {
  return crypto
    .createHmac("sha256", authSecret)
    .update(`${id}.${expiresAt}`)
    .digest("base64url");
}

async function removeQuickUpload(record) {
  if (!record) return;
  await fs.unlink(path.join(quickUploadDir, record.storedName)).catch(() => {});
  await storage.remove("uploads", record.id).catch(() => {});
}

async function pruneExpiredQuickUploads(now = Date.now()) {
  const uploads = await storage.list("uploads");
  await Promise.all(
    uploads
      .filter((item) => new Date(item.expiresAt).getTime() <= now)
      .map((item) => removeQuickUpload(item))
  );
}

async function checkConnectionAccess(connectionId, user) {
  const conn = await storage.getById("connections", connectionId);
  if (!conn) {
    throw new Error("Connection not found");
  }
  const hasAccess = conn.ownerId === user.id || (conn.sharedWith && conn.sharedWith.includes(user.id));
  if (!hasAccess) {
    throw new Error("Access denied to this connection");
  }
  return conn;
}

function escapeAttribute(value = "") {
  return String(value)
    .replaceAll("&", "&amp;")
    .replaceAll('"', "&quot;")
    .replaceAll("<", "&lt;")
    .replaceAll(">", "&gt;");
}

app.get("/login", async (req, res) => {
  const nextUrl =
    typeof req.query.next === "string" && req.query.next.startsWith("/") && !req.query.next.startsWith("//")
      ? req.query.next
      : "/";
  res.setHeader("Cache-Control", "no-store");
  res.type("html").send(renderLoginPage({
    error: typeof req.query.error === "string" ? req.query.error : "",
    success: typeof req.query.success === "string" ? req.query.success : "",
    nextUrl,
    registrationAvailable: await isRegistrationAvailable(),
  }));
});

function getClientIp(req) {
  return req.ip || req.socket?.remoteAddress || "unknown";
}

app.post("/login", async (req, res) => {
  const nextUrl =
    typeof req.body.next === "string" && req.body.next.startsWith("/") && !req.body.next.startsWith("//")
      ? req.body.next
      : "/";
  const ip = getClientIp(req);
  const username = String(req.body.username || "");
  const rate = loginRateLimiter.inspect(ip, username);
  if (!rate.allowed) {
    const seconds = Math.max(1, Math.ceil(rate.retryAfterMs / 1000));
    res.setHeader("Retry-After", String(seconds));
    res.redirect(`/login?error=${encodeURIComponent(`Too many attempts. Try again in ${seconds} seconds.`)}&next=${encodeURIComponent(nextUrl)}`);
    return;
  }

  try {
    const user = await userService.authenticate(username, req.body.password);
    if (!user) {
      loginRateLimiter.recordFailure(ip, username);
      res.redirect(`/login?error=Invalid username or password&next=${encodeURIComponent(nextUrl)}`);
      return;
    }
    loginRateLimiter.reset(ip, username);
    setAuthCookie(req, res, user);

    const ipResult = await userService.recordLoginIp(user.id, ip);
    if (ipResult?.isNew) {
      const separator = nextUrl.includes("?") ? "&" : "?";
      res.redirect(`${nextUrl}${separator}newIp=${encodeURIComponent(ip)}`);
    } else {
      res.redirect(nextUrl);
    }
  } catch (err) {
    res.redirect(`/login?error=${encodeURIComponent(err.message)}&next=${encodeURIComponent(nextUrl)}`);
  }
});

app.get("/register", async (req, res) => {
  if (!(await isRegistrationAvailable())) {
    res.status(404).type("text").send("Registration is disabled.");
    return;
  }
  const nextUrl =
    typeof req.query.next === "string" && req.query.next.startsWith("/") && !req.query.next.startsWith("//")
      ? req.query.next
      : "/";
  res.setHeader("Cache-Control", "no-store");
  res.type("html").send(renderRegisterPage({
    error: typeof req.query.error === "string" ? req.query.error : "",
    nextUrl
  }));
});

app.post("/register", async (req, res) => {
  const nextUrl =
    typeof req.body.next === "string" && req.body.next.startsWith("/") && !req.body.next.startsWith("//")
      ? req.body.next
      : "/";
  try {
    if (!(await isRegistrationAvailable())) {
      res.status(403).type("text").send("Registration is disabled.");
      return;
    }
    const existingUsers = await storage.list("users");
    const user = await userService.register(req.body.username, req.body.password, {
      role: existingUsers.length === 0 ? "admin" : "user",
    });

    if (existingUsers.length === 0) {
      await migrateUnownedData(user.id);
    }

    setAuthCookie(req, res, user);
    res.redirect(nextUrl);
  } catch (error) {
    res.redirect(`/register?error=${encodeURIComponent(error.message)}&next=${encodeURIComponent(nextUrl)}`);
  }
});

app.post("/logout", (req, res) => {
  clearAuthCookie(res);
  res.redirect("/login");
});

  res.type("application/manifest+json").sendFile(path.join(projectRoot, "public", "manifest.webmanifest"));

  res.setHeader("Service-Worker-Allowed", "/");
  res.type("application/javascript").sendFile(path.join(projectRoot, "public", "service-worker.js"));
});

  maxAge: "7d",
  immutable: true,
}));

app.get("/download/quick/:id", async (req, res) => {
  try {
    const record = await storage.getById("uploads", req.params.id);
    const expiresAt = Number(req.query.expires || 0);
    const token = String(req.query.token || "");
    const expectedToken = signQuickUpload(req.params.id, expiresAt);
    if (
      !record ||
      !Number.isFinite(expiresAt) ||
      expiresAt <= Date.now() ||
      new Date(record.expiresAt).getTime() !== expiresAt ||
      !safeEqual(token, expectedToken)
    ) {
      if (record && new Date(record.expiresAt).getTime() <= Date.now()) {
        await removeQuickUpload(record);
      }
      res.status(404).type("text").send("This upload link is invalid or expired.");
      return;
    }

    const filePath = path.join(quickUploadDir, record.storedName);
    res.setHeader("Cache-Control", "private, no-store");
    res.type(record.mimeType || "application/octet-stream");
    res.download(filePath, record.originalName);
  } catch (error) {
    sendError(res, error, 500);
  }
});

app.post("/api/auth/logout-all", async (req, res) => {
  try {
    await userService.revokeSessions(req.user.id);
    clearAuthCookie(res);
    res.json({ ok: true });
  } catch (error) {
    sendError(res, error, 500);
  }
});
app.post("/api/client-debug", async (req, res) => {
  try {
    const body = req.body && typeof req.body === "object" ? req.body : {};
    await logService.appendClientDebug({
      level: ["debug", "info", "warn", "error"].includes(body.level) ? body.level : "info",
      event: String(body.event || "client-debug").slice(0, 120),
      requestId: req.requestId,
      operationId: String(body.details?.operationId || body.operationId || "").slice(0, 128) || undefined,
      message: String(body.message || "Client debug event").slice(0, 2_000),
      details: {
        userId: req.user.id,
        page: String(body.page || "").slice(0, 500),
        userAgent: String(body.userAgent || req.headers["user-agent"] || "").slice(0, 1_000),
        clientTimestamp: String(body.timestamp || "").slice(0, 100),
        clientDetails: body.details || {},
      },
    });
    res.status(204).end();
  } catch (error) {
    sendError(res, error, 500);
  }
});
