  setHeaders(res, filePath) {
    if (/\.(?:js|css|html)$/i.test(filePath)) {
      res.setHeader("Cache-Control", "no-store");
    }
  },
}));

function summarizeRequestForLog(req) {
  const body = req?.body && typeof req.body === "object" ? req.body : {};
  return {
    method: req?.method || "",
    path: req?.originalUrl || req?.url || "",
    userId: req?.user?.id || null,
    ip: req?.ip || req?.socket?.remoteAddress || null,
    connectionId: body.connectionId || null,
    remotePath: body.remotePath || null,
    operationId: body.operationId || null,
    contentByteLength: typeof body.content === "string" ? Buffer.byteLength(body.content, "utf8") : null,
    elapsedMs: req?.requestStartedAt ? Date.now() - req.requestStartedAt : null,
  };
}

function sendError(res, error, statusCode = error?.statusCode || 400) {
  const request = summarizeRequestForLog(res.req);
  const payload = {
    statusCode,
    requestId: res.req?.requestId || null,
    message: error?.message || "Unknown error",
    details: error?.details || null,
    request,
  };
  console.error("[api error]", payload);
  logService.appendServerError(error, {
    event: "api-error",
    requestId: res.req?.requestId,
    operationId: request.operationId,
    statusCode,
    request,
  }).catch((logError) => console.error("Failed to persist API error:", logError));
  if (!res.headersSent) {
    res.status(statusCode).json({
      error: error?.message || "Unknown error",
      details: error?.details || null,
      requestId: res.req?.requestId || null,
    });
  }
}

function readAuthOverrides(source = {}) {
  const authOverrides = source?.authOverrides && typeof source.authOverrides === "object"
    ? source.authOverrides
    : source;

  return {
    usernameOverride:
      typeof authOverrides?.usernameOverride === "string" && authOverrides.usernameOverride.trim()
        ? authOverrides.usernameOverride.trim()
        : "",
    passwordOverride:
      typeof authOverrides?.passwordOverride === "string" && authOverrides.passwordOverride.length
        ? authOverrides.passwordOverride
        : "",
  };
}

function summarizeTerminalPayload(value = "") {
  const text = String(value || "");
  const preview = redactSecrets(text)
    .replace(/\x1b/g, "\\x1b")
    .replace(/\r/g, "\\r")
    .replace(/\n/g, "\\n")
    .replace(/\t/g, "\\t")
    .slice(0, 180);

  return {
    bytes: Buffer.byteLength(text),
    chars: text.length,
    hasBracketedPasteStart: text.includes("\x1b[200~"),
    hasBracketedPasteEnd: text.includes("\x1b[201~"),
    hasNewline: /[\r\n]/.test(text),
    preview,
  };
}

async function sanitizeConnection(connection, currentUserId, userService) {
  if (!connection) {
    return null;
  }

  const isOwner = connection.ownerId === currentUserId;

  let sharedWithUsernames = [];
  if (isOwner && Array.isArray(connection.sharedWith) && userService) {
    for (const uid of connection.sharedWith) {
      const u = await userService.findById(uid);
      if (u) {
        sharedWithUsernames.push(u.username);
      }
    }
  }

  return {
    id: connection.id,
    name: connection.name,
    host: connection.host,
    port: connection.port,
    username: connection.username,
    authType: connection.authType,
    privateKeyId: connection.privateKeyId,
    macAddress: connection.macAddress || "",
    defaultPath: connection.defaultPath,
    notes: connection.notes,
    createdAt: connection.createdAt,
    updatedAt: connection.updatedAt,
    passwordEncrypted: Boolean(connection.passwordEncrypted),
    passphraseEncrypted: Boolean(connection.passphraseEncrypted),
    ownerId: connection.ownerId,
    sharedWith: connection.sharedWith || [],
    isShared: !isOwner,
    ownerName: !isOwner && userService ? (await userService.findById(connection.ownerId))?.username || "unknown" : undefined,
    sharedWithUsernames: isOwner ? sharedWithUsernames : undefined,
  };
}

async function buildConnectionPayload(body, existing = null) {
  const authType = body.authType || existing?.authType || "privateKey";
  const payload = {
    name: body.name?.trim(),
    host: body.host?.trim(),
    port: Number(body.port || existing?.port || 22),
    username: body.username?.trim(),
    authType,
    privateKeyId: body.privateKeyId || null,
    defaultPath: body.defaultPath?.trim() || "",
    macAddress: body.macAddress?.trim() || "",
    notes: body.notes?.trim() || "",
  };

  if (!payload.name || !payload.host || !payload.username) {
    throw new Error("Name, host, and username are required");
  }

  const hasIncomingPassword = typeof body.password === "string" && body.password.length > 0;
  const preservedPassword = existing?.passwordEncrypted || null;
  const resolvedPasswordEncrypted = hasIncomingPassword
    ? await cryptoService.encryptText(body.password)
    : preservedPassword;

  if (authType === "password") {
    if (!resolvedPasswordEncrypted) {
      throw new Error("Password is required for password auth");
    }
    payload.passwordEncrypted = resolvedPasswordEncrypted;
    payload.privateKeyId = null;
    payload.passphraseEncrypted = null;
  } else {
    if (!payload.privateKeyId && !existing?.privateKeyId) {
      throw new Error("Private key is required for key-based auth");
    }
    payload.privateKeyId = payload.privateKeyId || existing?.privateKeyId;
    payload.passwordEncrypted = resolvedPasswordEncrypted;

    if (body.passphrase) {
      payload.passphraseEncrypted = await cryptoService.encryptText(body.passphrase);
    } else if (existing?.passphraseEncrypted) {
      payload.passphraseEncrypted = existing.passphraseEncrypted;
    } else {
      payload.passphraseEncrypted = null;
    }
  }

  return payload;
}

app.get("/api/state", async (req, res) => {
  const state = await storage.getClientState();
  const keys = await keyStore.listKeys();

  const filteredConnections = [];
  for (const conn of (state.connections || [])) {
    if (conn.ownerId === req.user.id || (conn.sharedWith && conn.sharedWith.includes(req.user.id))) {
      filteredConnections.push(await sanitizeConnection(conn, req.user.id, userService));
    }
  }

  const filteredSessions = (state.sessions || []).filter(item => item.ownerId === req.user.id);
  const filteredQuickCommands = (state.quickCommands || []).filter(item => item.ownerId === req.user.id);
  const filteredCommandHistory = (state.commandHistory || []).filter(item => item.ownerId === req.user.id);
  const filteredKeys = keys.filter(item => item.ownerId === req.user.id);

  res.json({
    connections: filteredConnections,
    sessions: filteredSessions,
    quickCommands: filteredQuickCommands,
    commandHistory: filteredCommandHistory,
    keys: filteredKeys,
    llmSettings: state.llmSettings,
    activeTerminals: sshService.listActiveTerminals().filter(t => t.ownerId === req.user.id),
    currentUser: { id: req.user.id, username: req.user.username, role: req.user.role || "user" },
  });
});

app.get("/api/keys", async (req, res) => {
  const keys = await keyStore.listKeys();
  res.json(keys.filter(k => k.ownerId === req.user.id));
});

app.post("/api/keys", async (req, res) => {
  try {
    const key = await keyStore.createKey({
      name: req.body.name,
      privateKeyText: req.body.privateKeyText,
      ownerId: req.user.id,
    });
    res.json(key);
  } catch (error) {
    sendError(res, error);
  }
});

app.post("/api/keys/upload", keyUpload.single("privateKey"), async (req, res) => {
  try {
    if (!req.file) {
      res.status(400).json({ error: "Private key file is required" });
      return;
    }
    const fileContent = await fs.readFile(req.file.path, "utf8");
    const key = await keyStore.createKey({
      name: req.body.name || req.file.originalname,
      privateKeyText: fileContent,
      ownerId: req.user.id,
    });
    res.json(key);
  } catch (error) {
    sendError(res, error);
  } finally {
    if (req.file?.path) {
      await fs.unlink(req.file.path).catch(() => {});
    }
  }
});

app.delete("/api/keys/:id", async (req, res) => {
  try {
    const keys = await keyStore.listKeys();
    const key = keys.find(k => k.id === req.params.id);
    if (!key) {
      return res.status(404).json({ error: "Key not found" });
    }
    if (key.ownerId !== req.user.id) {
      return res.status(403).json({ error: "Forbidden: You do not own this key" });
    }

    const connections = await storage.list("connections");
    if (connections.some((item) => item.ownerId === req.user.id && item.privateKeyId === req.params.id)) {
      throw new Error("This key is still used by one or more saved connections.");
    }
    res.json(await keyStore.removeKey(req.params.id));
  } catch (error) {
    sendError(res, error);
  }
});

app.get("/api/connections", async (req, res) => {
  const items = await storage.list("connections");
  const filtered = items.filter(conn => conn.ownerId === req.user.id || (conn.sharedWith && conn.sharedWith.includes(req.user.id)));
  const sanitized = [];
  for (const item of filtered) {
    sanitized.push(await sanitizeConnection(item, req.user.id, userService));
  }
  res.json(sanitized);
});

app.post("/api/connections", async (req, res) => {
  try {
    const payload = await buildConnectionPayload(req.body);
    payload.ownerId = req.user.id;
    payload.sharedWith = [];
    const created = await storage.upsert("connections", payload);
    res.json(await sanitizeConnection(created, req.user.id, userService));
  } catch (error) {
    sendError(res, error);
  }
});

app.post("/api/connections/:id/duplicate", async (req, res) => {
  try {
    const existing = await storage.getById("connections", req.params.id);
    if (!existing) {
      throw new Error("Connection not found");
    }

    const hasAccess = existing.ownerId === req.user.id || (existing.sharedWith && existing.sharedWith.includes(req.user.id));
    if (!hasAccess) {
      return res.status(403).json({ error: "Forbidden" });
    }

    const requestedName =
      typeof req.body?.name === "string" && req.body.name.trim()
        ? req.body.name.trim()
        : `${existing.name} copy`;

    const {
      id: _id,
      createdAt: _createdAt,
      updatedAt: _updatedAt,
      ...copyable
    } = existing;

    const duplicated = await storage.upsert("connections", {
      ...copyable,
      name: requestedName,
      ownerId: req.user.id,
      sharedWith: [],
    });

    res.json(await sanitizeConnection(duplicated, req.user.id, userService));
  } catch (error) {
    sendError(res, error);
  }
});

app.put("/api/connections/:id", async (req, res) => {
  try {
    const existing = await storage.getById("connections", req.params.id);
    if (!existing) {
      throw new Error("Connection not found");
    }
    if (existing.ownerId !== req.user.id) {
      return res.status(403).json({ error: "Forbidden: You do not own this connection" });
    }
    const payload = await buildConnectionPayload(req.body, existing);
    payload.ownerId = existing.ownerId;
    payload.sharedWith = existing.sharedWith || [];
    const updated = await storage.upsert("connections", payload, req.params.id);
    res.json(await sanitizeConnection(updated, req.user.id, userService));
  } catch (error) {
    sendError(res, error);
  }
});

app.post("/api/connections/:id/share", async (req, res) => {
  try {
    const existing = await storage.getById("connections", req.params.id);
    if (!existing) {
      return res.status(404).json({ error: "Connection not found" });
    }
    if (existing.ownerId !== req.user.id) {
      return res.status(403).json({ error: "Forbidden: Only the owner can share" });
    }
    const targetUsername = req.body.username?.trim();
    if (!targetUsername) {
      return res.status(400).json({ error: "Username is required" });
    }
    const targetUser = await userService.findByUsername(targetUsername);
    if (!targetUser) {
      return res.status(404).json({ error: `User "${targetUsername}" not found` });
    }
    if (targetUser.id === req.user.id) {
      return res.status(400).json({ error: "You cannot share with yourself" });
    }
    const sharedWith = existing.sharedWith || [];
    if (!sharedWith.includes(targetUser.id)) {
      sharedWith.push(targetUser.id);
    }
    existing.sharedWith = sharedWith;
    await storage.upsert("connections", existing, req.params.id);
    const usernames = [];
    for (const uid of sharedWith) {
      const u = await userService.findById(uid);
      if (u) usernames.push(u.username);
    }
    res.json({ success: true, sharedWithUsernames: usernames });
  } catch (error) {
    sendError(res, error);
  }
});

app.post("/api/connections/:id/unshare", async (req, res) => {
  try {
    const existing = await storage.getById("connections", req.params.id);
    if (!existing) {
      return res.status(404).json({ error: "Connection not found" });
    }
    if (existing.ownerId !== req.user.id) {
      return res.status(403).json({ error: "Forbidden: Only the owner can unshare" });
    }
    const targetUsername = req.body.username?.trim();
    if (!targetUsername) {
      return res.status(400).json({ error: "Username is required" });
    }
    const targetUser = await userService.findByUsername(targetUsername);
    if (!targetUser) {
      return res.status(404).json({ error: `User "${targetUsername}" not found` });
    }
    let sharedWith = existing.sharedWith || [];
    sharedWith = sharedWith.filter(id => id !== targetUser.id);
    existing.sharedWith = sharedWith;
    await storage.upsert("connections", existing, req.params.id);
    const usernames = [];
    for (const uid of sharedWith) {
      const u = await userService.findById(uid);
      if (u) usernames.push(u.username);
    }
    res.json({ success: true, sharedWithUsernames: usernames });
  } catch (error) {
    sendError(res, error);
  }
});

app.post("/api/connections/:id/test", async (req, res) => {
  try {
    await checkConnectionAccess(req.params.id, req.user);
    res.json(await sshService.testConnection(req.params.id, readAuthOverrides(req.body)));
  } catch (error) {
    sendError(res, error, 500);
  }
});

app.get("/api/connections/export", async (req, res) => {
  try {
    const items = await storage.list("connections");
    const own = items.filter(conn => conn.ownerId === req.user.id);
    const exported = [];

    for (const conn of own) {
      const password = conn.passwordEncrypted ? await cryptoService.decryptPayload(conn.passwordEncrypted) : null;
      const passphrase = conn.passphraseEncrypted ? await cryptoService.decryptPayload(conn.passphraseEncrypted) : null;

      let privateKey = null;
      let privateKeyName = null;
      if (conn.authType === "privateKey" && conn.privateKeyId) {
        try {
          privateKey = await keyStore.readKey(conn.privateKeyId);
          const keys = await keyStore.listKeys();
          const keyMeta = keys.find(k => k.id === conn.privateKeyId);
          privateKeyName = keyMeta?.name || null;
        } catch {}
      }

      exported.push({
        name: conn.name,
        host: conn.host,
        port: conn.port,
        username: conn.username,
        authType: conn.authType,
        password,
        passphrase,
        privateKey,
        privateKeyName,
        defaultPath: conn.defaultPath || "",
        macAddress: conn.macAddress || "",
        notes: conn.notes || "",
      });
    }

    res.json({ version: 1, connections: exported });
  } catch (error) {
    sendError(res, error, 500);
  }
});

app.post("/api/connections/import", async (req, res) => {
  try {
    const { connections } = req.body;
    if (!Array.isArray(connections)) {
      return res.status(400).json({ error: "Invalid import format: connections array required" });
    }

    const created = [];

    for (const conn of connections) {
      if (!conn.name || !conn.host || !conn.username) {
        continue;
      }

      let privateKeyId = null;
      if (conn.authType === "privateKey" && conn.privateKey) {
        try {
          const key = await keyStore.createKey({
            name: conn.privateKeyName || `${conn.name} key`,
            privateKeyText: conn.privateKey,
            ownerId: req.user.id,
          });
          privateKeyId = key.id;
        } catch (error) {
          console.error(`[import] Failed to import key for "${conn.name}":`, error.message);
        }
      }

      const payload = {
        name: conn.name.trim(),
        host: conn.host.trim(),
        port: Number(conn.port || 22),
        username: conn.username.trim(),
        authType: conn.authType || "privateKey",
        privateKeyId,
        defaultPath: conn.defaultPath?.trim() || "",
        macAddress: conn.macAddress?.trim() || "",
        notes: conn.notes?.trim() || "",
      };

      if (conn.password) {
        payload.passwordEncrypted = await cryptoService.encryptText(conn.password);
      } else {
        payload.passwordEncrypted = null;
      }

      if (conn.passphrase) {
        payload.passphraseEncrypted = await cryptoService.encryptText(conn.passphrase);
      } else {
        payload.passphraseEncrypted = null;
      }

      payload.ownerId = req.user.id;
      payload.sharedWith = [];

      const result = await storage.upsert("connections", payload);
      created.push(await sanitizeConnection(result, req.user.id, userService));
    }

    res.json({ imported: created.length, connections: created });
  } catch (error) {
    sendError(res, error, 500);
  }
});

app.post("/api/wake/:connectionId", async (req, res) => {
  try {
    const conn = await checkConnectionAccess(req.params.connectionId, req.user);
    if (!conn.macAddress) {
      return res.status(400).json({ error: "No MAC address configured for this connection." });
    }
    const target = req.body.address || conn.host || "255.255.255.255";
    const port = Number(req.body.port) || 9;
    const result = await sendWoL(conn.macAddress, { address: target, port });
    res.json(result);
  } catch (error) {
    sendError(res, error, 500);
  }
});

  let filtered = history.filter(item => item.ownerId === req.user.id);
  if (connectionId) {
    filtered = filtered.filter((item) => item.connectionId === connectionId);
  }
  res.json(filtered.sort((a, b) => new Date(b.updatedAt) - new Date(a.updatedAt)));
});

app.post("/api/sync/remote-to-remote/preview", async (req, res) => {
  try {
    const {
      connectionIdA,
      pathA,
      connectionIdB,
      pathB,
      direction,
      conflictPolicy,
      includeDeletes,
      mode = "folder",
      ignorePatterns = [],
      authOverridesA = {},
      authOverridesB = {}
    } = req.body;

    await checkConnectionAccess(connectionIdA, req.user);
    await checkConnectionAccess(connectionIdB, req.user);

    let plan;
    if (mode === "file") {
      const [fileA, fileB] = await Promise.all([
        sshService.sftpFileEntry(connectionIdA, pathA, authOverridesA),
        sshService.sftpFileEntry(connectionIdB, pathB, authOverridesB),
      ]);
      plan = sshService.buildRemoteFileSyncPlan({
        direction,
        fileA,
        fileB,
        pathA,
        pathB,
        connectionIdA,
        connectionIdB,
        includeDeletes: Boolean(includeDeletes),
        conflictPolicy,
      });
    } else {
      const [entriesA, entriesB] = await Promise.all([
        sshService.sftpListTree(connectionIdA, pathA, authOverridesA),
        sshService.sftpListTree(connectionIdB, pathB, authOverridesB),
      ]);

      plan = sshService.buildRemoteSyncPlan({
        direction,
        entriesA,
        entriesB,
        pathA,
        pathB,
        connectionIdA,
        connectionIdB,
        includeDeletes: Boolean(includeDeletes),
        conflictPolicy,
        ignorePatterns
      });
    }

    res.json({ ok: true, plan });
  } catch (error) {
    sendError(res, error, 500);
  }
});

app.post("/api/sync/remote-to-remote/execute", async (req, res) => {
  try {
    const { plan, socketId, authOverridesA = {}, authOverridesB = {} } = req.body;
    
    await checkConnectionAccess(plan.connectionIdA, req.user);
    await checkConnectionAccess(plan.connectionIdB, req.user);

    res.json({ ok: true, status: "started" });

    const onProgress = (message, percent) => {
      if (socketId) {
        io.to(socketId).emit("remote-sync:progress", { message, percent });
      }
    };

    sshService.executeRemoteSync(plan, onProgress, authOverridesA, authOverridesB)
      .then(() => {
        if (socketId) {
          io.to(socketId).emit("remote-sync:complete", { plan });
        }
      })
      .catch((error) => {
        console.error("Remote-to-remote sync error:", error);
        if (socketId) {
          io.to(socketId).emit("remote-sync:error", { error: error.message });
        }
      });
  } catch (error) {
    console.error("Failed to start remote sync:", error);
  }
});

app.post("/api/files/write", async (req, res) => {
  const operationId = /^[a-zA-Z0-9._:-]{6,128}$/.test(String(req.body.operationId || ""))
    ? String(req.body.operationId)
    : req.requestId;
  const connectionId = String(req.body.connectionId || "").trim();
  const remotePath = String(req.body.remotePath || "").trim();
  const content = typeof req.body.content === "string" ? req.body.content : "";
  const byteLength = Buffer.byteLength(content, "utf8");

  await logService.appendFileSave({
    level: "info",
    event: "file-save-request",
    requestId: req.requestId,
    operationId,
    message: `Received remote file save request for ${remotePath || "[missing path]"}.`,
    details: { userId: req.user.id, connectionId, remotePath, byteLength },
  }).catch(() => {});

  try {
    if (!connectionId) {
      const error = new Error("connectionId is required to save a remote file.");
      error.statusCode = 400;
      throw error;
    }
    if (!remotePath || remotePath.includes("\0")) {
      const error = new Error("A valid remotePath is required to save a remote file.");
      error.statusCode = 400;
      throw error;
    }
    const maxBytes = Number(process.env.MAX_EDITOR_SAVE_BYTES || 20 * 1024 * 1024);
    if (byteLength > maxBytes) {
      const error = new Error(`File is too large for the text editor (${byteLength} bytes; maximum ${maxBytes}).`);
      error.statusCode = 413;
      throw error;
    }

    await checkConnectionAccess(connectionId, req.user);
    const result = await sshService.sftpWriteText(
      connectionId,
      remotePath,
      content,
      readAuthOverrides(req.body),
      { operationId, requestId: req.requestId, userId: req.user.id }
    );

    await logService.appendFileSave({
      level: "info",
      event: "file-save-response",
      requestId: req.requestId,
      operationId,
      message: `Remote file save completed and verified for ${remotePath}.`,
      details: { userId: req.user.id, connectionId, remotePath, ...result },
    });
    res.json({ ...result, requestId: req.requestId });
  } catch (error) {
    await logService.appendFileSave({
      level: "error",
      event: "file-save-error",
      requestId: req.requestId,
      operationId,
      message: error?.message || "Remote file save failed.",
      details: {
        userId: req.user.id,
        connectionId,
        remotePath,
        byteLength,
        code: error?.code || null,
        stack: error?.stack || "",
      },
    }).catch(() => {});
    sendError(res, error, error?.statusCode || 500);
  }
});

app.post("/api/files/upload", fileUpload.single("file"), async (req, res) => {
  try {
    if (!req.file) {
      res.status(400).json({ error: "File is required" });
      return;
    }
    await checkConnectionAccess(req.body.connectionId, req.user);
    const result = await sshService.sftpUploadLocalFile(
      req.body.connectionId,
      req.file.path,
      req.body.remotePath,
      readAuthOverrides(req.body)
    );
    res.json(result);
  } catch (error) {
    sendError(res, error, 500);
  } finally {
    if (req.file?.path) {
      await fs.unlink(req.file.path).catch(() => {});
    }
  }
});

app.post("/api/files/download", async (req, res) => {
  try {
    await checkConnectionAccess(req.body.connectionId, req.user);
    const { localPath, filename, contentType } = await sshService.sftpDownloadToTemp(
      req.body.connectionId,
      req.body.remotePath,
      readAuthOverrides(req.body)
    );

    res.setHeader("Content-Type", contentType);
    res.download(localPath, filename, async () => {
      if (existsSync(localPath)) {
        await fs.unlink(localPath).catch(() => {});
      }
    });
  } catch (error) {
    sendError(res, error, 500);
  }
});

app.post("/api/files/compress-download", async (req, res) => {
  try {
    await checkConnectionAccess(req.body.connectionId, req.user);
    const { connectionId, remotePath } = req.body;
    const authOverrides = readAuthOverrides(req.body);

    const parentPath = path.posix.dirname(remotePath);
    const folderName = path.posix.basename(remotePath);
    const zipName = `${folderName}.zip`;
    const tarName = `${folderName}.tar.gz`;
    const zipRemotePath = path.posix.join(parentPath, zipName);
    const tarRemotePath = path.posix.join(parentPath, tarName);

    const parentEscaped = parentPath.replace(/"/g, '\\"');
    const folderEscaped = folderName.replace(/"/g, '\\"');
    const zipEscaped = zipName.replace(/"/g, '\\"');
    const tarEscaped = tarName.replace(/"/g, '\\"');
    const command = `cd "${parentEscaped}" && (zip -q -r "${zipEscaped}" "${folderEscaped}" || tar -czf "${tarEscaped}" "${folderEscaped}")`;

    await sshService.executeRemoteCommand(connectionId, command, authOverrides);

    const { localPath, filename, contentType } = await sshService.downloadAndCleanupArchive(
      connectionId,
      zipRemotePath,
      tarRemotePath,
      authOverrides
    );

    res.setHeader("Content-Type", contentType);
    res.download(localPath, filename, async () => {
      if (existsSync(localPath)) {
        await fs.unlink(localPath).catch(() => {});
      }
    });
  } catch (error) {
    sendError(res, error, 500);
  }
});

app.get("/api/active-terminals", async (req, res) => {
  res.json(sshService.listActiveTerminals().filter(t => t.ownerId === req.user.id));
});

app.post("/api/quick-upload", quickUpload.single("file"), async (req, res) => {
  let record = null;
  try {
    if (!req.file) {
      res.status(400).json({ error: "No file provided" });
      return;
    }
    await pruneExpiredQuickUploads();
    const expiresAt = Date.now() + quickUploadTtlMs;
    record = await storage.upsert("uploads", {
      ownerId: req.user.id,
      storedName: req.file.filename,
      originalName: req.file.originalname,
      size: req.file.size,
      mimeType: req.file.mimetype || "application/octet-stream",
      expiresAt: new Date(expiresAt).toISOString(),
    });
    const token = signQuickUpload(record.id, expiresAt);
    const url = `${req.protocol}://${req.get("host")}/download/quick/${encodeURIComponent(record.id)}?expires=${expiresAt}&token=${encodeURIComponent(token)}`;
    res.json({
      ok: true,
      url,
      filename: record.originalName,
      size: record.size,
      mimeType: record.mimeType,
      expiresAt: record.expiresAt,
    });
  } catch (error) {
    if (record) {
      await removeQuickUpload(record);
    } else if (req.file?.path) {
      await fs.unlink(req.file.path).catch(() => {});
    }
    sendError(res, error, 500);
  }
});

app.post("/api/git/llm-commit-message", async (req, res) => {
  try {
    await checkConnectionAccess(req.body.connectionId, req.user);
    const statusResult = await gitService.status(
      req.body.connectionId,
      req.body.repoPath || ".",
      readAuthOverrides(req.body)
    );

    const stagedFiles = statusResult.staged || [];
    const unstagedFiles = statusResult.unstaged || [];
    const untrackedFiles = statusResult.untracked || [];
    const allFiles = [...stagedFiles, ...unstagedFiles, ...untrackedFiles];

    if (allFiles.length === 0) {
      return res.json({ message: "No changes to commit" });
    }

    let diffContent = "";
    try {
      if (stagedFiles.length > 0) {
        const stagedDiff = await gitService.diff(
          req.body.connectionId,
          req.body.repoPath || ".",
          { staged: true },
          readAuthOverrides(req.body)
        );
        diffContent = (stagedDiff.diff || "").slice(0, 8000);
      }
      if (!diffContent && unstagedFiles.length > 0) {
        const unstagedDiff = await gitService.diff(
          req.body.connectionId,
          req.body.repoPath || ".",
          { staged: false },
          readAuthOverrides(req.body)
        );
        diffContent = (unstagedDiff.diff || "").slice(0, 8000);
      }
    } catch {}

    const fileSummary = allFiles.map((f) => `  ${f.status} ${f.filename}`).join("\n");
    const prompt = [
      `Write a concise, conventional commit message for the following changes in repo at path "${req.body.repoPath || "."}":`,
      `Branch: ${statusResult.branch}`,
      `Changed files:\n${fileSummary}`,
      diffContent ? `Diff summary:\n${diffContent}` : "",
      "Return ONLY the commit message, nothing else. Use conventional commits format (feat:, fix:, chore:, refactor:, etc). Keep it under 72 chars for the first line.",
    ].filter(Boolean).join("\n\n");

    const result = await llmService.assist({
      mode: "suggest",
      outputSnippet: prompt,
      userMessage: "Generate a commit message",
      connectionName: "",
      recentCommands: [],
    });

    const message = (result.content || "").trim().replace(/^```.*?\n?/, "").replace(/\n?```$/, "").trim();
    res.json({ message: message || "Update files" });
  } catch (error) {
    sendError(res, error, 500);
  }
});

app.get("*", (_req, res) => {
  res.sendFile(path.join(projectRoot, "public", "index.html"));
});

function emitOwnedTerminalEvent(eventName, payload = {}) {
  if (!payload.ownerId) {
    console.warn(`[terminal event dropped] ${eventName} did not include an ownerId`, {
      terminalId: payload.terminalId || null,
    });
    return;
  }
  const { ownerId, ...clientPayload } = payload;
  io.to(`user_${ownerId}`).emit(eventName, clientPayload);
}

sshService.on("terminal:data", (payload) => emitOwnedTerminalEvent("terminal:data", payload));
sshService.on("terminal:error", (payload) => emitOwnedTerminalEvent("terminal:error", payload));
sshService.on("terminal:status", (payload) => emitOwnedTerminalEvent("terminal:status", payload));
sshService.on("terminal:closed", (payload) => emitOwnedTerminalEvent("terminal:closed", payload));


app.use((error, req, res, _next) => {
  sendError(res, error, error?.statusCode || (error?.name === "MulterError" ? 400 : 500));
});

io.use(async (socket, next) => {
  const user = await getAuthenticatedUser(socket.request);
  if (user) {
    socket.user = user;
    next();
    return;
  }
  next(new Error("Authentication required"));
});

io.on("connection", (socket) => {
  socket.join(`user_${socket.user.id}`);

  socket.on("terminal:create", async (payload, callback = () => {}) => {
    try {
      await checkConnectionAccess(payload.connectionId, socket.user);
      const terminal = await sshService.createTerminal({
        ...payload,
        ownerId: socket.user.id,
      });
      callback({ ok: true, terminal });
    } catch (error) {
      callback({ ok: false, error: error.message, details: error.details || null });
    }
  });

  socket.on("terminal:input", async (payload = {}) => {
    try {
      const terminal = sshService.terminals.get(payload.terminalId);
      if (!terminal || terminal.ownerId !== socket.user.id) {
        throw new Error("Access denied or terminal not found");
      }

      if (process.env.DEBUG_TERMINAL_INPUT === "1") {
        const summary = summarizeTerminalPayload(payload.data);
        console.info("[socket terminal:input]", {
          socketId: socket.id,
          terminalId: payload.terminalId || null,
          source: payload.source || "unknown",
          ...summary,
        });
      }

      await sshService.input(payload.terminalId, payload.data, {
        source: payload.source || "socket",
        socketId: socket.id,
        ownerId: socket.user.id,
      });
    } catch (error) {
      console.error("[socket terminal:input:error]", {
        socketId: socket.id,
        terminalId: payload.terminalId || null,
        message: error.message,
      });
      socket.emit("terminal:error", {
        terminalId: payload.terminalId,
        message: error.message,
      });
    }
  });

  socket.on("terminal:resize", (payload) => {
    try {
      const terminal = sshService.terminals.get(payload.terminalId);
      if (!terminal || terminal.ownerId !== socket.user.id) {
        return;
      }
      sshService.resize(payload.terminalId, payload.cols, payload.rows, { ownerId: socket.user.id });
    } catch {}
  });

  socket.on("terminal:sendBatch", async (payload = {}) => {
    try {
      const terminal = sshService.terminals.get(payload.terminalId);
      if (!terminal || terminal.ownerId !== socket.user.id) {
        throw new Error("Access denied or terminal not found");
      }

      const summary = summarizeTerminalPayload(payload.commands);
      console.info("[socket terminal:sendBatch]", {
        socketId: socket.id,
        terminalId: payload.terminalId || null,
        source: payload.source || "batch",
        ...summary,
      });

      await sshService.sendBatch(payload.terminalId, payload.commands, {
        source: payload.source || "batch",
        socketId: socket.id,
        ownerId: socket.user.id,
      });
    } catch (error) {
      console.error("[socket terminal:sendBatch:error]", {
        socketId: socket.id,
        terminalId: payload.terminalId || null,
        message: error.message,
      });
      socket.emit("terminal:error", {
        terminalId: payload.terminalId,
        message: error.message,
      });
    }
  });

  socket.on("terminal:command", async (payload) => {
    try {
      const terminal = sshService.terminals.get(payload.terminalId);
      if (!terminal || terminal.ownerId !== socket.user.id) {
        throw new Error("Access denied or terminal not found");
      }

      await storage.saveCommand({
        command: payload.command,
        connectionId: payload.connectionId,
        connectionName: payload.connectionName,
        terminalId: payload.terminalId,
        source: payload.source || "terminal",
        ownerId: socket.user.id,
      });
      io.to(`user_${socket.user.id}`).emit("command:updated");
    } catch (error) {
      socket.emit("terminal:error", {
        terminalId: payload.terminalId,
        message: error.message,
      });
    }
  });

  socket.on("terminal:close", async (payload) => {
    try {
      const terminal = sshService.terminals.get(payload.terminalId);
      if (!terminal || terminal.ownerId !== socket.user.id) {
        return;
      }
      await sshService.closeTerminal(payload.terminalId);
    } catch {}
  });
});

server.on("clientError", (error, socket) => {
  logService.appendServerError(error, {
    event: "http-client-error",
    remoteAddress: socket?.remoteAddress || null,
  }).catch(() => {});
  if (socket?.writable) {
    socket.end("HTTP/1.1 400 Bad Request\r\nConnection: close\r\n\r\n");
  }
});

const port = Number(process.env.PORT || 3015);
server.listen(port, () => {
  console.log(`Remote Terminal Hub listening on http://localhost:${port}`);
});
