// ===== scripts/check-secrets.mjs =====
import fs from "node:fs/promises";
import path from "node:path";
import process from "node:process";

const root = process.cwd();
const excluded = new Set([".git", "node_modules", "data", "build", "coverage"]);
const findings = [];
const patterns = [
  { name: "private key", regex: /-----BEGIN [^-\n]*PRIVATE KEY-----\s+[A-Za-z0-9+/=\r\n]{80,}-----END [^-\n]*PRIVATE KEY-----/ },
  { name: "OpenRouter API key", regex: /\bsk-or-v1-[A-Za-z0-9_-]{32,}\b/ },
  { name: "GitHub token", regex: /\bgh[pousr]_[A-Za-z0-9_]{30,}\b/ },
  { name: "Slack token", regex: /\bxox[baprs]-[A-Za-z0-9-]{20,}\b/ },
];

async function walk(directory = ".") {
  const absolute = path.join(root, directory);
  const entries = await fs.readdir(absolute, { withFileTypes: true });
  for (const entry of entries) {
    if (excluded.has(entry.name)) continue;
    const relative = path.join(directory, entry.name);
    if (entry.isDirectory()) {
      await walk(relative);
      continue;
    }
    if (!entry.isFile() || /\.(?:png|jpe?g|gif|webp|ico|woff2?|zip|gz|pdf)$/i.test(entry.name)) continue;
    const content = await fs.readFile(path.join(root, relative), "utf8").catch(() => "");
    for (const pattern of patterns) {
      if (pattern.regex.test(content)) {
        findings.push(`${relative}: possible ${pattern.name}`);
      }
    }
  }
}

await walk();
if (findings.length) {
  console.error("Potential secrets detected:\n" + findings.map((item) => `- ${item}`).join("\n"));
  process.exitCode = 1;
} else {
  console.log("No high-confidence secrets detected.");
}


// ===== scripts/export-source.mjs =====
import fs from "node:fs/promises";
import path from "node:path";
import process from "node:process";

const root = path.resolve(process.cwd());
const outputPath = path.resolve(root, process.argv[2] || "combined-source.txt");
const roots = ["src", "public", "frontend", "scripts", "test", ".github"];
const rootFiles = [
  "package.json",
  "package-lock.json",
  "vite.config.js",
  ".gitignore",
  ".env.example",
];
const excludedParts = new Set([
  ".git",
  "node_modules",
  "data",
  "build",
  "uploads",
  "logs",
  "backups",
]);
const excludedNames = new Set([".env", ".app-secret"]);

function shouldExclude(relativePath) {
  const parts = relativePath.split(path.sep);
  return parts.some((part) => excludedParts.has(part)) || excludedNames.has(path.basename(relativePath));
}

async function collect(directory, results = []) {
  const absolute = path.join(root, directory);
  const entries = await fs.readdir(absolute, { withFileTypes: true }).catch(() => []);
  for (const entry of entries) {
    const relative = path.join(directory, entry.name);
    if (shouldExclude(relative)) continue;
    if (entry.isDirectory()) {
      await collect(relative, results);
    } else if (entry.isFile()) {
      results.push(relative);
    }
  }
  return results;
}

const files = [];
for (const directory of roots) {
  await collect(directory, files);
}
for (const file of rootFiles) {
  if (!shouldExclude(file)) {
    await fs.access(path.join(root, file)).then(() => files.push(file)).catch(() => {});
  }
}

files.sort((a, b) => a.localeCompare(b));
const chunks = [];
for (const relative of files) {
  const body = await fs.readFile(path.join(root, relative), "utf8");
  chunks.push(`// ===== ${relative.replaceAll(path.sep, "/")} =====\n${body.trimEnd()}\n`);
}
await fs.writeFile(outputPath, `${chunks.join("\n")}\n`, { encoding: "utf8", mode: 0o600 });
console.log(`Exported ${files.length} source files to ${outputPath}`);


// ===== test/fileSave.test.js =====
import test from "node:test";
import assert from "node:assert/strict";
import fs from "node:fs/promises";
import os from "node:os";
import path from "node:path";
import { Readable, Writable } from "node:stream";

import { writeAndVerifySftpText } from "../src/services/sshService.js";
import LogService from "../src/services/logService.js";
import { canDismissUnsavedPrompt } from "../frontend/modules/fileSaveController.js";

function createMemorySftp({ corruptRead = false } = {}) {
  const files = new Map();
  return {
    files,
    createWriteStream(remotePath) {
      const chunks = [];
      return new Writable({
        write(chunk, _encoding, callback) {
          chunks.push(Buffer.from(chunk));
          callback();
        },
        final(callback) {
          files.set(remotePath, Buffer.concat(chunks));
          callback();
        },
      });
    },
    createReadStream(remotePath) {
      const stored = files.get(remotePath) || Buffer.alloc(0);
      const value = corruptRead ? Buffer.concat([stored, Buffer.from("corrupt")]) : stored;
      return Readable.from([value]);
    },
  };
}

function createCallbackMemorySftp() {
  const files = new Map();
  const handles = new Map();
  let nextHandleId = 1;
  return {
    files,
    open(remotePath, flags, _attrs, callback) {
      const handle = nextHandleId++;
      handles.set(handle, { remotePath, buffer: Buffer.alloc(0) });
      if (String(flags).includes("w")) {
        files.set(remotePath, Buffer.alloc(0));
      }
      callback(null, handle);
    },
    write(handle, buffer, offset, length, position, callback) {
      const entry = handles.get(handle);
      if (!entry) {
        callback(new Error("Invalid handle"));
        return;
      }
      const chunk = Buffer.from(buffer.subarray(offset, offset + length));
      const requiredLength = position + chunk.length;
      if (entry.buffer.length < requiredLength) {
        const expanded = Buffer.alloc(requiredLength);
        entry.buffer.copy(expanded);
        entry.buffer = expanded;
      }
      chunk.copy(entry.buffer, position);
      callback(null);
    },
    close(handle, callback) {
      const entry = handles.get(handle);
      if (!entry) {
        callback(new Error("Invalid handle"));
        return;
      }
      files.set(entry.remotePath, entry.buffer);
      handles.delete(handle);
      callback(null);
    },
    createReadStream(remotePath) {
      return Readable.from([files.get(remotePath) || Buffer.alloc(0)]);
    },
  };
}

test("file save writes Unicode and verifies the exact remote bytes", async () => {
  const sftp = createMemorySftp();
  const content = "hello 🌮\nsecond line\n";
  const stages = [];
  const result = await writeAndVerifySftpText(sftp, "/tmp/test.txt", content, {
    operationId: "save-test-1",
    onStage(entry) { stages.push(entry.event); },
  });

  assert.equal(result.ok, true);
  assert.equal(result.verified, true);
  assert.equal(result.byteLength, Buffer.byteLength(content));
  assert.equal(sftp.files.get("/tmp/test.txt").toString("utf8"), content);
  assert.deepEqual(stages, [
    "sftp-write-start",
    "sftp-write-finished",
    "sftp-write-verify-start",
    "sftp-write-verified",
  ]);
});

test("file save can write through callback-based SFTP methods", async () => {
  const sftp = createCallbackMemorySftp();
  const content = "direct write\nsecond line\n";
  const result = await writeAndVerifySftpText(sftp, "/tmp/direct.txt", content, {
    operationId: "save-test-direct",
  });

  assert.equal(result.verified, true);
  assert.equal(sftp.files.get("/tmp/direct.txt").toString("utf8"), content);
});

test("file save correctly truncates a remote file to empty content", async () => {
  const sftp = createMemorySftp();
  sftp.files.set("/tmp/empty.txt", Buffer.from("old content"));
  const result = await writeAndVerifySftpText(sftp, "/tmp/empty.txt", "", {
    operationId: "save-test-empty",
  });
  assert.equal(result.verified, true);
  assert.equal(result.byteLength, 0);
  assert.equal(sftp.files.get("/tmp/empty.txt").length, 0);
});

test("file save rejects a mismatched read-back", async () => {
  const sftp = createMemorySftp({ corruptRead: true });
  await assert.rejects(
    writeAndVerifySftpText(sftp, "/tmp/test.txt", "expected", { operationId: "save-test-bad" }),
    (error) => error.code === "SFTP_SAVE_VERIFY_FAILED"
  );
});

test("false unsaved warning is bypassed only for exact verified content", () => {
  assert.equal(canDismissUnsavedPrompt("You have unsaved changes. Discard them?", "saved", "saved"), true);
  assert.equal(canDismissUnsavedPrompt("You have unsaved changes. Discard them?", "changed", "saved"), false);
  assert.equal(canDismissUnsavedPrompt("Delete this file?", "saved", "saved"), false);
});

test("text debug logs redact secrets and include operation IDs", async () => {
  const directory = await fs.mkdtemp(path.join(os.tmpdir(), "rth-save-log-"));
  try {
    const logs = new LogService(directory);
    await logs.appendFileSave({
      level: "error",
      event: "file-save-test",
      operationId: "operation-123",
      message: "password=supersecret failed",
      details: { authorization: "Bearer abcdefghijklmnop", byteLength: 12 },
    });
    const text = await fs.readFile(path.join(directory, "file-save-debug.txt"), "utf8");
    assert.match(text, /operation-123/);
    assert.match(text, /file-save-test/);
    assert.doesNotMatch(text, /supersecret/);
    assert.doesNotMatch(text, /abcdefghijklmnop/);
    assert.match(text, /REDACTED/);
  } finally {
    await fs.rm(directory, { recursive: true, force: true });
  }
});


// ===== test/security.test.js =====
import test from "node:test";
import assert from "node:assert/strict";
import { EventEmitter } from "node:events";
import fs from "node:fs/promises";
import os from "node:os";
import path from "node:path";

import TerminalSessionService from "../src/services/terminalSessionService.js";
import LogService from "../src/services/logService.js";
import LoginRateLimiter from "../src/security/loginRateLimiter.js";
import { redactSecrets } from "../src/security/redaction.js";
import CryptoService from "../src/services/cryptoService.js";
import SshService from "../src/services/sshService.js";

class FakeSshService extends EventEmitter {
  constructor() {
    super();
    this.terminals = new Map();
    this.writes = [];
  }

  input(terminalId, data, meta) {
    this.writes.push({ terminalId, data, meta });
  }

  async closeTerminal(terminalId) {
    this.terminals.delete(terminalId);
  }

  listActiveTerminals() {
    return [...this.terminals.values()];
  }
}

test("terminal session methods reject a different owner", async () => {
  const ssh = new FakeSshService();
  ssh.terminals.set("terminal-1", {
    terminalId: "terminal-1",
    ownerId: "owner-a",
    connectionId: "connection-1",
    connectionName: "Server",
    title: "Server",
    createdAt: new Date().toISOString(),
  });
  const sessions = new TerminalSessionService(ssh);

  assert.throws(
    () => sessions.input("terminal-1", "whoami", { ownerId: "owner-b" }),
    (error) => error.statusCode === 403
  );
  assert.throws(
    () => sessions.getOutput("terminal-1", 0, 0, "owner-b"),
    (error) => error.statusCode === 403
  );
  await assert.rejects(
    () => sessions.closeSession("terminal-1", "owner-b"),
    (error) => error.statusCode === 403
  );
  assert.equal(ssh.writes.length, 0);

  sessions.input("terminal-1", "whoami", { ownerId: "owner-a" });
  assert.equal(ssh.writes.length, 1);
});

test("secret redaction masks common command credentials", () => {
  const input = "curl -H 'Authorization: Bearer abc.def.ghi' https://user:pass@example.com API_KEY=sk-test-12345678901234567890";
  const output = redactSecrets(input);
  assert.doesNotMatch(output, /abc\.def\.ghi/);
  assert.doesNotMatch(output, /user:pass/);
  assert.doesNotMatch(output, /sk-test/);
  assert.match(output, /REDACTED/);
});

test("login limiter locks a username and IP after repeated failures", () => {
  const limiter = new LoginRateLimiter({ maxAttempts: 2, windowMs: 1_000, lockMs: 5_000 });
  assert.equal(limiter.inspect("127.0.0.1", "admin", 0).allowed, true);
  limiter.recordFailure("127.0.0.1", "admin", 0);
  assert.equal(limiter.inspect("127.0.0.1", "admin", 1).allowed, true);
  limiter.recordFailure("127.0.0.1", "admin", 2);
  const locked = limiter.inspect("127.0.0.1", "admin", 3);
  assert.equal(locked.allowed, false);
  assert.equal(locked.retryAfterMs, 4_999);
  limiter.reset("127.0.0.1", "admin");
  assert.equal(limiter.inspect("127.0.0.1", "admin", 4).allowed, true);
});

test("private terminal logs remain in memory and are not written to disk", async () => {
  const directory = await fs.mkdtemp(path.join(os.tmpdir(), "rth-private-log-"));
  try {
    const logs = new LogService(directory);
    const log = logs.getOrCreate("private-terminal", { persist: false });
    log.append("secret output\n");
    assert.match(log.getTail(), /secret output/);
    await logs.close("private-terminal");
    await assert.rejects(() => fs.access(path.join(directory, "private-terminal.log")));
  } finally {
    await fs.rm(directory, { recursive: true, force: true });
  }
});

test("crypto decrypt failures do not expose the AES-GCM error", async () => {
  const directory = await fs.mkdtemp(path.join(os.tmpdir(), "rth-crypto-"));
  const originalSecret = process.env.APP_SECRET;
  try {
    process.env.APP_SECRET = "original-test-secret-value-with-32-bytes";
    const first = new CryptoService(directory);
    const encrypted = await first.encryptText("secret");
    const second = new CryptoService(directory);
    process.env.APP_SECRET = "different-test-secret-value-with-32-bytes";
    await assert.rejects(
      () => second.decryptPayload(encrypted),
      (error) => {
        assert.equal(error.code, "DECRYPT_FAILED");
        assert.match(error.message, /application secret may have changed/i);
        assert.doesNotMatch(error.message, /Unsupported state|authenticate data/i);
        return true;
      }
    );
  } finally {
    if (originalSecret === undefined) {
      delete process.env.APP_SECRET;
    } else {
      process.env.APP_SECRET = originalSecret;
    }
    await fs.rm(directory, { recursive: true, force: true });
  }
});

test("SSH connection config reports saved password decrypt recovery message", async () => {
  const directory = await fs.mkdtemp(path.join(os.tmpdir(), "rth-ssh-decrypt-"));
  const originalSecret = process.env.APP_SECRET;
  try {
    process.env.APP_SECRET = "original-test-secret-value-with-32-bytes";
    const cryptoService = new CryptoService(directory);
    const passwordEncrypted = await cryptoService.encryptText("secret");
    process.env.APP_SECRET = "different-test-secret-value-with-32-bytes";

    const ssh = new SshService({
      storage: {
        async getById(collection, id) {
          assert.equal(collection, "connections");
          assert.equal(id, "connection-1");
          return {
            id,
            name: "Server",
            host: "example.test",
            port: 22,
            username: "deploy",
            authType: "password",
            passwordEncrypted,
          };
        },
      },
      keyStore: { async readKey() {} },
      cryptoService: new CryptoService(directory),
      logService: { async appendDebug() {} },
      uploadDir: directory,
    });

    await assert.rejects(
      () => ssh.connectionConfigFromSaved("connection-1"),
      (error) => {
        assert.equal(error.code, "DECRYPT_FAILED");
        assert.match(error.message, /Stored password cannot be decrypted/i);
        assert.doesNotMatch(error.message, /Unsupported state|authenticate data/i);
        return true;
      }
    );
  } finally {
    if (originalSecret === undefined) {
      delete process.env.APP_SECRET;
    } else {
      process.env.APP_SECRET = originalSecret;
    }
    await fs.rm(directory, { recursive: true, force: true });
  }
});

test("SSH password override bypasses stale saved encrypted password", async () => {
  const directory = await fs.mkdtemp(path.join(os.tmpdir(), "rth-ssh-override-"));
  const originalSecret = process.env.APP_SECRET;
  try {
    process.env.APP_SECRET = "original-test-secret-value-with-32-bytes";
    const cryptoService = new CryptoService(directory);
    const passwordEncrypted = await cryptoService.encryptText("stale-secret");
    process.env.APP_SECRET = "different-test-secret-value-with-32-bytes";

    const ssh = new SshService({
      storage: {
        async getById() {
          return {
            id: "connection-1",
            name: "Server",
            host: "example.test",
            port: 22,
            username: "deploy",
            authType: "password",
            passwordEncrypted,
          };
        },
      },
      keyStore: { async readKey() {} },
      cryptoService: new CryptoService(directory),
      logService: { async appendDebug() {} },
      uploadDir: directory,
    });

    const { config, debugMeta } = await ssh.connectionConfigFromSaved("connection-1", {
      passwordOverride: "fresh-secret",
    });
    assert.equal(config.password, "fresh-secret");
    assert.equal(config.tryKeyboard, true);
    assert.equal(debugMeta.usingPasswordOverride, true);
  } finally {
    if (originalSecret === undefined) {
      delete process.env.APP_SECRET;
    } else {
      process.env.APP_SECRET = originalSecret;
    }
    await fs.rm(directory, { recursive: true, force: true });
  }
});


// ===== test/gitService.test.js =====
import test from "node:test";
import assert from "node:assert/strict";

import {
  default as GitService,
  parseBranches,
  parseLog,
  parsePorcelainV2Status,
  shellQuote,
} from "../src/services/gitService.js";

test("shellQuote single-quotes shell arguments safely", () => {
  assert.equal(shellQuote("plain"), "'plain'");
  assert.equal(shellQuote("has spaces"), "'has spaces'");
  assert.equal(shellQuote("x'$(touch nope)'y"), "'x'\\''$(touch nope)'\\''y'");
});

test("parsePorcelainV2Status parses branch metadata and file states", () => {
  const stdout = [
    "# branch.oid abc123",
    "# branch.head main",
    "# branch.upstream origin/main",
    "# branch.ab +2 -1",
    "1 .M N... 100644 100644 100644 abc abc src/app.js",
    "1 M. N... 100644 100644 100644 abc def README.md",
    "? new file.txt",
    "2 R. N... 100644 100644 100644 abc def R100 src/new.js",
    "src/old.js",
    "",
  ].join("\0");

  const status = parsePorcelainV2Status(stdout);

  assert.equal(status.branch, "main");
  assert.equal(status.upstream, "origin/main");
  assert.equal(status.ahead, 2);
  assert.equal(status.behind, 1);
  assert.deepEqual(status.unstaged.map((file) => [file.status, file.filename]), [
    ["modified", "src/app.js"],
  ]);
  assert.deepEqual(status.staged.map((file) => [file.status, file.filename, file.originalFilename]), [
    ["modified", "README.md", ""],
    ["renamed", "src/new.js", "src/old.js"],
  ]);
  assert.deepEqual(status.untracked.map((file) => file.filename), ["new file.txt"]);
  assert.equal(status.totalChanges, 4);
});

test("parseLog handles stable field-separated git log output", () => {
  assert.deepEqual(parseLog("abc\x1ffix bug\x1fAda\x1f2 hours ago\n"), [
    { hash: "abc", message: "fix bug", author: "Ada", relativeDate: "2 hours ago" },
  ]);
});

test("parseBranches reads current marker and upstream tracking text", () => {
  const branches = parseBranches("*\x1fmain\x1forigin/main\x1f[ahead 3, behind 1]\n \x1ffeature\x1f\x1f");
  assert.deepEqual(branches, [
    { name: "main", current: true, upstream: "origin/main", ahead: 3, behind: 1 },
    { name: "feature", current: false, upstream: "", ahead: 0, behind: 0 },
  ]);
});

test("GitService constructs git -C commands with quoted repo and file args", async () => {
  const calls = [];
  const service = new GitService({
    sshService: {
      async executeRemoteCommand(connectionId, command, authOverrides) {
        calls.push({ connectionId, command, authOverrides });
        return { code: 0, stdout: "", stderr: "" };
      },
    },
  });

  await service.stage("conn-1", "/repo path", ["src/a file.js", "x'$(touch nope).js"], { usernameOverride: "ada" });

  assert.equal(calls.length, 1);
  assert.equal(calls[0].connectionId, "conn-1");
  assert.equal(calls[0].authOverrides.usernameOverride, "ada");
  assert.equal(
    calls[0].command,
    "git -C '/repo path' add -- 'src/a file.js' 'x'\\''$(touch nope).js'"
  );
});


// ===== frontend/modules/socketGuard.js =====
const DANGEROUS_COMMAND_PATTERN = /(^|[;&|]\s*)(sudo\s+)?(rm\s+-rf\s+\/?(?:\s|$)|mkfs(?:\.|\s)|dd\s+if=|shutdown(?:\s|$)|reboot(?:\s|$)|poweroff(?:\s|$)|:.*\{.*:\|:.*&)/im;

function normalizePastedText(value = "") {
  return String(value)
    .replace(/^\u001b\[200~/, "")
    .replace(/\u001b\[201~$/, "");
}

function shouldConfirmPaste(value = "") {
  const text = normalizePastedText(value);
  const lineCount = text.split(/\r?\n/).filter((line) => line.trim()).length;
  return lineCount > 1 || DANGEROUS_COMMAND_PATTERN.test(text);
}

function confirmPaste(value = "") {
  const text = normalizePastedText(value);
  const lines = text.split(/\r?\n/).filter((line) => line.trim());
  const dangerous = DANGEROUS_COMMAND_PATTERN.test(text);
  const summary = dangerous
    ? "This paste appears to contain a destructive or system-level command."
    : `This paste contains ${lines.length} non-empty lines.`;
  return window.confirm(`${summary}\n\nReview it carefully before sending it to the remote terminal. Continue?`);
}

export function createGuardedSocketFactory(createSocket, privacyController) {
  return (...args) => {
    const socket = createSocket(...args);
    const originalEmit = socket.emit.bind(socket);

    socket.emit = (eventName, payload, ...rest) => {
      let nextPayload = payload;
      if (eventName === "terminal:create" && payload && typeof payload === "object") {
        nextPayload = { ...payload, privateMode: privacyController.isEnabled() };
      }
      if (eventName === "terminal:command" && payload && typeof payload === "object") {
        nextPayload = { ...payload, privateMode: privacyController.isEnabled() };
      }
      if (
        eventName === "terminal:input" &&
        payload &&
        typeof payload === "object" &&
        shouldConfirmPaste(payload.data) &&
        !confirmPaste(payload.data)
      ) {
        return socket;
      }
      return originalEmit(eventName, nextPayload, ...rest);
    };

    window.__rthSocket = socket;
    return socket;
  };
}


// ===== frontend/modules/fileSaveController.js =====
const CLIENT_LOG_ENDPOINT = "/api/client-debug";
const READ_ENDPOINT = "/api/files/read";
const WRITE_ENDPOINT = "/api/files/write";
const SAVE_WATCHDOG_MS = 1_500;
const SAVE_TIMEOUT_MS = 90_000;
const UNSAVED_PROMPT_PATTERN = /you have unsaved changes\.\s*discard them\?/i;

function createId() {
  return globalThis.crypto?.randomUUID?.() || `${Date.now()}-${Math.random().toString(36).slice(2, 10)}`;
}

function safeJson(value) {
  if (typeof value !== "string" || !value.trim()) return null;
  try {
    return JSON.parse(value);
  } catch {
    return null;
  }
}

function pathOf(input) {
  const value = typeof input === "string" ? input : input instanceof URL ? input.href : input?.url || "";
  try {
    return new URL(value, location.href).pathname;
  } catch {
    return String(value || "");
  }
}

function bodyOf(input, init = {}) {
  if (typeof init.body === "string") return safeJson(init.body);
  if (input instanceof Request && typeof input.clone === "function") return null;
  return null;
}

function byteLength(value) {
  return new TextEncoder().encode(String(value ?? "")).length;
}

function editorValue() {
  return document.getElementById("fileEditor")?.value ?? "";
}

function setStatus(state, message) {
  const status = document.getElementById("editorSaveStatus");
  const button = document.getElementById("saveFileBtn");
  if (status) {
    status.textContent = message;
    status.dataset.state = state;
    status.title = message;
  }
  if (button) {
    button.dataset.saveState = state;
    button.setAttribute("aria-busy", String(state === "saving"));
  }
}

function showNotice(message, kind = "info") {
  let notice = document.getElementById("rthFileSaveNotice");
  if (!notice) {
    notice = document.createElement("div");
    notice.id = "rthFileSaveNotice";
    notice.className = "rth-file-save-notice";
    notice.setAttribute("role", "status");
    notice.setAttribute("aria-live", "polite");
    document.body.appendChild(notice);
  }
  notice.dataset.kind = kind;
  notice.textContent = message;
  notice.classList.add("is-visible");
  clearTimeout(showNotice.timer);
  showNotice.timer = setTimeout(
    () => notice.classList.remove("is-visible"),
    kind === "error" ? 12_000 : 4_000
  );
}

function cleanDetails(value) {
  if (!value || typeof value !== "object") return {};
  return Object.fromEntries(
    Object.entries(value)
      .filter(([key]) => !/password|passphrase|privatekey|authorization|cookie|content/i.test(key))
      .slice(0, 40)
      .map(([key, item]) => {
        if (typeof item === "string") return [key, item.slice(0, 2_000)];
        if (typeof item === "number" || typeof item === "boolean" || item == null) return [key, item];
        return [key, String(item).slice(0, 2_000)];
      })
  );
}

export function canDismissUnsavedPrompt(message, currentContent, verifiedContent) {
  return UNSAVED_PROMPT_PATTERN.test(String(message || ""))
    && typeof verifiedContent === "string"
    && String(currentContent ?? "") === verifiedContent;
}

export function initFileSaveController() {
  if (window.__rthFileSaveControllerInitialized) return;
  window.__rthFileSaveControllerInitialized = true;

  const nativeFetch = window.fetch.bind(window);
  const nativeConfirm = window.confirm.bind(window);
  const state = {
    context: null,
    verifiedContent: null,
    verifiedAt: 0,
    writeSequence: 0,
    pendingWrites: 0,
    watchdog: null,
    fallbackInFlight: false,
  };

  const log = (entry = {}) => {
    const payload = {
      level: entry.level || "info",
      event: entry.event || "file-save-client",
      message: entry.message || "",
      operationId: entry.operationId || "",
      remotePath: entry.remotePath || state.context?.remotePath || "",
      details: cleanDetails(entry.details || {}),
    };
    nativeFetch(CLIENT_LOG_ENDPOINT, {
      method: "POST",
      headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },
      body: JSON.stringify(payload),
      keepalive: true,
    }).catch(() => {});
  };

  const markVerified = ({ body, result, operationId, source }) => {
    if (typeof body?.content !== "string") return;
    state.context = {
      connectionId: body.connectionId,
      remotePath: body.remotePath,
      authOverrides: body.authOverrides || {},
    };
    state.verifiedContent = body.content;
    state.verifiedAt = Date.now();
    setStatus("saved", `Saved ${new Date().toLocaleTimeString()}`);
    showNotice(`Saved and verified: ${body.remotePath}`, "success");
    log({
      event: "file-save-verified-client",
      message: "The browser received a verified save response.",
      operationId,
      remotePath: body.remotePath,
      details: {
        source,
        byteLength: result.byteLength,
        sha256: result.sha256,
        requestId: result.requestId,
      },
    });
    window.dispatchEvent(new CustomEvent("rth:file-saved", {
      detail: { ...result, operationId, remotePath: body.remotePath, content: body.content },
    }));
  };

  window.fetch = async (input, init = {}) => {
    const pathname = pathOf(input);
    const parsedBody = bodyOf(input, init);
    let effectiveInit = init;
    let operationId = "";

    if (pathname === WRITE_ENDPOINT && parsedBody) {
      operationId = String(parsedBody.operationId || createId());
      const headers = new Headers(init.headers || (input instanceof Request ? input.headers : undefined));
      headers.set("Content-Type", "application/json");
      headers.set("X-Request-Id", operationId);
      effectiveInit = {
        ...init,
        headers,
        body: JSON.stringify({ ...parsedBody, operationId }),
      };
      state.writeSequence += 1;
      state.pendingWrites += 1;
      clearTimeout(state.watchdog);
      state.watchdog = null;
      setStatus("saving", "Saving…");
      log({
        event: "file-save-request-client",
        message: "A file write request is leaving the browser.",
        operationId,
        remotePath: parsedBody.remotePath,
        details: {
          connectionId: parsedBody.connectionId,
          byteLength: byteLength(parsedBody.content),
        },
      });
    }

    const startedAt = performance.now();
    try {
      const response = await nativeFetch(input, effectiveInit);
      const durationMs = Math.round(performance.now() - startedAt);

      if (pathname === READ_ENDPOINT && response.ok && parsedBody?.connectionId && parsedBody?.remotePath) {
        const result = await response.clone().json().catch(() => null);
        if (result && typeof result.content === "string") {
          state.context = {
            connectionId: parsedBody.connectionId,
            remotePath: parsedBody.remotePath,
            authOverrides: parsedBody.authOverrides || {},
          };
          state.verifiedContent = result.content;
          state.verifiedAt = Date.now();
          log({
            event: "file-read-context-captured",
            message: "Captured the exact connection and path used to open the editor.",
            remotePath: parsedBody.remotePath,
            details: { connectionId: parsedBody.connectionId, byteLength: byteLength(result.content), durationMs },
          });
        }
      }

      if (pathname === WRITE_ENDPOINT) {
        const raw = await response.clone().text().catch(() => "");
        const result = safeJson(raw) || {};
        if (response.ok && result.ok === true && result.verified === true) {
          markVerified({ body: { ...parsedBody, operationId }, result, operationId, source: parsedBody?.source || "native" });
        } else {
          const message = result.error || raw || `Save failed with HTTP ${response.status}.`;
          setStatus("error", `Save failed · ${operationId.slice(0, 8)}`);
          showNotice(`${message} · Log ID ${operationId}`, "error");
          log({
            level: "error",
            event: "file-save-response-error-client",
            message,
            operationId,
            remotePath: parsedBody?.remotePath,
            details: { status: response.status, requestId: result.requestId, durationMs, code: result.code },
          });
        }
      }
      return response;
    } catch (error) {
      if (pathname === WRITE_ENDPOINT) {
        setStatus("error", `Save failed · ${operationId.slice(0, 8)}`);
        showNotice(`${error?.message || "Save request failed"} · Log ID ${operationId}`, "error");
      }
      log({
        level: "error",
        event: "file-api-network-error-client",
        message: error?.message || "The browser request failed before receiving a response.",
        operationId,
        remotePath: parsedBody?.remotePath,
        details: { pathname, name: error?.name, stack: error?.stack || "" },
      });
      throw error;
    } finally {
      if (pathname === WRITE_ENDPOINT && parsedBody) {
        state.pendingWrites = Math.max(0, state.pendingWrites - 1);
      }
    }
  };

  const fallbackSave = async (clickId) => {
    if (state.fallbackInFlight) return;
    const context = state.context;
    if (!context?.connectionId || !context?.remotePath) {
      const message = "No exact remote file context is available. Reopen the file and try Save again.";
      setStatus("error", "Save not sent");
      showNotice(`${message} · Log ID ${clickId}`, "error");
      log({ level: "error", event: "file-save-context-missing", message, operationId: clickId });
      return;
    }

    state.fallbackInFlight = true;
    log({
      level: "warn",
      event: "file-save-native-handler-missed",
      message: "The app did not send a write request after the Save click; using the verified fallback controller.",
      operationId: clickId,
      remotePath: context.remotePath,
    });

    const controller = new AbortController();
    const timeout = setTimeout(() => controller.abort(new DOMException("Save timed out", "TimeoutError")), SAVE_TIMEOUT_MS);
    try {
      const response = await window.fetch(WRITE_ENDPOINT, {
        method: "POST",
        headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },
        body: JSON.stringify({
          operationId: clickId,
          source: "fallback",
          connectionId: context.connectionId,
          remotePath: context.remotePath,
          authOverrides: context.authOverrides || {},
          content: editorValue(),
        }),
        signal: controller.signal,
      });
      if (!response.ok) {
        const result = await response.json().catch(() => ({}));
        throw new Error(result.error || `Save failed with HTTP ${response.status}.`);
      }
    } catch (error) {
      log({
        level: "error",
        event: "file-save-fallback-error",
        message: error?.message || "Fallback save failed.",
        operationId: clickId,
        remotePath: context.remotePath,
        details: { stack: error?.stack || "" },
      });
    } finally {
      clearTimeout(timeout);
      state.fallbackInFlight = false;
    }
  };

  document.addEventListener("click", (event) => {
    const button = event.target?.closest?.("#saveFileBtn");
    if (!button) return;
    const clickId = createId();
    const writeSequenceAtClick = state.writeSequence;
    clearTimeout(state.watchdog);
    setStatus("saving", "Saving…");
    log({
      event: "file-save-click-client",
      message: "Save changes was clicked. Waiting for the app's native save handler.",
      operationId: clickId,
      remotePath: state.context?.remotePath,
      details: { byteLength: byteLength(editorValue()), writeSequenceAtClick },
    });
    state.watchdog = setTimeout(() => {
      state.watchdog = null;
      if (state.writeSequence === writeSequenceAtClick && state.pendingWrites === 0) fallbackSave(clickId);
    }, SAVE_WATCHDOG_MS);
  }, true);

  document.addEventListener("keydown", (event) => {
    if (!(event.ctrlKey || event.metaKey) || event.key.toLowerCase() !== "s") return;
    const editor = document.getElementById("fileEditor");
    if (!editor || document.activeElement !== editor) return;
    event.preventDefault();
    document.getElementById("saveFileBtn")?.click();
  }, true);

  window.confirm = (message) => {
    if (canDismissUnsavedPrompt(message, editorValue(), state.verifiedContent)) {
      log({
        event: "false-unsaved-warning-bypassed",
        message: "The app displayed an unsaved warning even though the exact editor contents were verified on the server.",
        remotePath: state.context?.remotePath,
        details: { verifiedAt: state.verifiedAt },
      });
      return true;
    }
    return nativeConfirm(message);
  };

  window.addEventListener("error", (event) => {
    log({
      level: "error",
      event: "window-error",
      message: event.message || "Unhandled browser error",
      details: { filename: event.filename, line: event.lineno, column: event.colno, stack: event.error?.stack || "" },
    });
  });

  window.addEventListener("unhandledrejection", (event) => {
    log({
      level: "error",
      event: "unhandled-rejection-client",
      message: event.reason?.message || String(event.reason || "Unhandled promise rejection"),
      details: { stack: event.reason?.stack || "" },
    });
  });

  log({ event: "file-save-controller-ready", message: "File save controller and diagnostics initialized." });
}


// ===== frontend/modules/fileSaveDiagnostics.js =====
const CLIENT_LOG_ENDPOINT = "/api/client-debug";
const SAVE_ENDPOINT = "/api/files/write";
const READ_ENDPOINT = "/api/files/read";
const SAVE_TIMEOUT_MS = 90_000;
const MAX_CLIENT_DETAIL_LENGTH = 4_000;

function createId() {
  return globalThis.crypto?.randomUUID?.() || `${Date.now()}-${Math.random().toString(36).slice(2, 10)}`;
}

function safeJsonParse(value) {
  if (typeof value !== "string" || !value.trim()) return null;
  try {
    return JSON.parse(value);
  } catch {
    return null;
  }
}

function requestUrl(input) {
  if (typeof input === "string") return input;
  if (input instanceof URL) return input.href;
  return input?.url || "";
}

function requestBody(input, init = {}) {
  if (typeof init.body === "string") return safeJsonParse(init.body);
  if (input instanceof Request && typeof input.clone === "function") {
    return null;
  }
  return null;
}

function trimValue(value, maxLength = MAX_CLIENT_DETAIL_LENGTH) {
  if (value === null || value === undefined) return value;
  if (typeof value === "string") return value.slice(0, maxLength);
  if (typeof value === "number" || typeof value === "boolean") return value;
  if (Array.isArray(value)) return value.slice(0, 20).map((item) => trimValue(item, 500));
  if (typeof value === "object") {
    return Object.fromEntries(
      Object.entries(value)
        .filter(([key]) => !/password|passphrase|privatekey|authorization|cookie|content/i.test(key))
        .slice(0, 30)
        .map(([key, item]) => [key, trimValue(item, 1_000)])
    );
  }
  return String(value).slice(0, maxLength);
}

function filePathFromLabel() {
  const text = document.getElementById("editorPathLabel")?.textContent?.trim() || "";
  if (!text || /^no file selected$/i.test(text)) return "";
  return text;
}

function setSaveStatus(state, message) {
  const status = document.getElementById("editorSaveStatus");
  const button = document.getElementById("saveFileBtn");
  if (status) {
    status.textContent = message;
    status.dataset.state = state;
    status.title = message;
  }
  if (button) {
    button.disabled = state === "saving";
    button.dataset.saveState = state;
    button.setAttribute("aria-busy", String(state === "saving"));
  }
}

function showSaveNotice(message, kind = "info") {
  let host = document.getElementById("rthFileSaveNotice");
  if (!host) {
    host = document.createElement("div");
    host.id = "rthFileSaveNotice";
    host.className = "rth-file-save-notice";
    host.setAttribute("role", "status");
    host.setAttribute("aria-live", "polite");
    document.body.appendChild(host);
  }
  host.dataset.kind = kind;
  host.textContent = message;
  host.classList.add("is-visible");
  clearTimeout(showSaveNotice.timer);
  showSaveNotice.timer = setTimeout(() => host.classList.remove("is-visible"), kind === "error" ? 10_000 : 4_000);
}

function errorDetails(error) {
  return {
    name: error?.name || "Error",
    message: error?.message || String(error || "Unknown error"),
    stack: typeof error?.stack === "string" ? error.stack.slice(0, MAX_CLIENT_DETAIL_LENGTH) : "",
  };
}

export function initFileSaveDiagnostics() {
  const nativeFetch = window.fetch.bind(window);
  let lastFileContext = null;
  let saveInFlight = false;

  const sendClientLog = (entry = {}) => {
    const payload = {
      timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
      page: location.pathname,
      userAgent: navigator.userAgent,
      ...entry,
      details: trimValue(entry.details || {}),
    };

    nativeFetch(CLIENT_LOG_ENDPOINT, {
      method: "POST",
      headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },
      body: JSON.stringify(payload),
      keepalive: true,
    }).catch(() => {});
  };

  window.fetch = async (input, init = {}) => {
    const url = requestUrl(input);
    const pathname = (() => {
      try {
        return new URL(url, location.href).pathname;
      } catch {
        return String(url || "");
      }
    })();
    const body = requestBody(input, init);
    const startedAt = performance.now();

    try {
      const response = await nativeFetch(input, init);
      const durationMs = Math.round(performance.now() - startedAt);

      if (pathname === READ_ENDPOINT && response.ok && body?.connectionId && body?.remotePath) {
        lastFileContext = {
          connectionId: body.connectionId,
          remotePath: body.remotePath,
          authOverrides: body.authOverrides || {},
        };
        sendClientLog({
          level: "info",
          event: "file-read-context-captured",
          message: "Captured the active remote file context.",
          details: { connectionId: body.connectionId, remotePath: body.remotePath, durationMs },
        });
      }

      if ((pathname === READ_ENDPOINT || pathname === SAVE_ENDPOINT) && !response.ok) {
        const responseText = await response.clone().text().catch(() => "");
        sendClientLog({
          level: "error",
          event: "file-api-http-error",
          message: `${pathname} returned HTTP ${response.status}.`,
          details: {
            status: response.status,
            remotePath: body?.remotePath,
            response: responseText.slice(0, 2_000),
            durationMs,
          },
        });
      }

      return response;
    } catch (error) {
      sendClientLog({
        level: "error",
        event: "file-api-network-error",
        message: `${pathname || "fetch"} failed before receiving a response.`,
        details: { ...errorDetails(error), remotePath: body?.remotePath },
      });
      throw error;
    }
  };

  async function resolveFileContext() {
    const labelPath = filePathFromLabel();
    if (lastFileContext && (!labelPath || lastFileContext.remotePath === labelPath)) {
      return { ...lastFileContext, remotePath: labelPath || lastFileContext.remotePath };
    }

    const stateResponse = await nativeFetch("/api/state", { headers: { Accept: "application/json" } });
    if (!stateResponse.ok) {
      throw new Error(`Unable to determine the active terminal (HTTP ${stateResponse.status}).`);
    }
    const state = await stateResponse.json();
    const terminals = Array.isArray(state.activeTerminals) ? state.activeTerminals : [];
    const selectedLabel = document.getElementById("selectedTerminalBadge")?.textContent || "";
    const selected = terminals.find((terminal) =>
      selectedLabel.includes(terminal.title || "") && selectedLabel.includes(terminal.connectionName || "")
    ) || (terminals.length === 1 ? terminals[0] : null);

    if (!selected?.connectionId || !labelPath) {
      throw new Error("The active file context is unavailable. Reopen the file, then save again.");
    }

    return {
      connectionId: selected.connectionId,
      remotePath: labelPath,
      authOverrides: {},
    };
  }

  async function saveCurrentFile(source = "button") {
    if (saveInFlight) return;
    const editor = document.getElementById("fileEditor");
    if (!editor) {
      throw new Error("The file editor is not available.");
    }

    saveInFlight = true;
    const operationId = createId();
    const startedAt = performance.now();
    setSaveStatus("saving", "Saving…");
    showSaveNotice("Saving remote file…");

    try {
      const context = await resolveFileContext();
      const content = editor.value ?? "";
      sendClientLog({
        level: "info",
        event: "file-save-click",
        message: "Remote file save started.",
        details: {
          operationId,
          source,
          connectionId: context.connectionId,
          remotePath: context.remotePath,
          byteLength: new TextEncoder().encode(content).length,
        },
      });

      const controller = new AbortController();
      const timeout = setTimeout(() => controller.abort(new DOMException("Save timed out", "TimeoutError")), SAVE_TIMEOUT_MS);
      let response;
      try {
        response = await nativeFetch(SAVE_ENDPOINT, {
          method: "POST",
          headers: {
            "Content-Type": "application/json",
            "X-Request-Id": operationId,
          },
          body: JSON.stringify({
            operationId,
            connectionId: context.connectionId,
            remotePath: context.remotePath,
            content,
            authOverrides: context.authOverrides || {},
          }),
          signal: controller.signal,
        });
      } finally {
        clearTimeout(timeout);
      }

      const raw = await response.text();
      const result = safeJsonParse(raw) || {};
      if (!response.ok) {
        const error = new Error(result.error || raw || `Save failed with HTTP ${response.status}.`);
        error.details = result.details || null;
        throw error;
      }
      if (!result.ok || result.verified !== true) {
        throw new Error(`The server did not verify the saved file. Operation ${operationId}.`);
      }

      lastFileContext = context;
      const durationMs = Math.round(performance.now() - startedAt);
      setSaveStatus("saved", `Saved ${new Date().toLocaleTimeString()}`);
      showSaveNotice(`Saved and verified: ${context.remotePath}`, "success");
      sendClientLog({
        level: "info",
        event: "file-save-success",
        message: "Remote file save completed and was verified by the server.",
        details: {
          operationId,
          remotePath: context.remotePath,
          byteLength: result.byteLength,
          sha256: result.sha256,
          durationMs,
        },
      });
      window.dispatchEvent(new CustomEvent("rth:file-saved", { detail: { ...result, operationId, remotePath: context.remotePath } }));
    } catch (error) {
      const durationMs = Math.round(performance.now() - startedAt);
      setSaveStatus("error", `Save failed · ${operationId.slice(0, 8)}`);
      showSaveNotice(`${error?.message || "Save failed"} · Log ID ${operationId}`, "error");
      sendClientLog({
        level: "error",
        event: "file-save-failed",
        message: error?.message || "Remote file save failed.",
        details: { operationId, durationMs, ...errorDetails(error), apiDetails: error?.details || null },
      });
      console.error("[file save failed]", operationId, error);
    } finally {
      saveInFlight = false;
      const button = document.getElementById("saveFileBtn");
      if (button) button.disabled = false;
    }
  }

  document.addEventListener("click", (event) => {
    const button = event.target?.closest?.("#saveFileBtn");
    if (!button) return;
    event.preventDefault();
    event.stopImmediatePropagation();
    saveCurrentFile("button").catch((error) => {
      sendClientLog({ level: "error", event: "file-save-controller-error", message: error.message, details: errorDetails(error) });
    });
  }, true);

  document.addEventListener("keydown", (event) => {
    if (!(event.ctrlKey || event.metaKey) || event.key.toLowerCase() !== "s") return;
    const editor = document.getElementById("fileEditor");
    if (!editor || document.activeElement !== editor) return;
    event.preventDefault();
    saveCurrentFile("keyboard").catch(() => {});
  }, true);

  window.addEventListener("error", (event) => {
    sendClientLog({
      level: "error",
      event: "window-error",
      message: event.message || "Unhandled browser error",
      details: { filename: event.filename, lineno: event.lineno, colno: event.colno, ...errorDetails(event.error) },
    });
  });

  window.addEventListener("unhandledrejection", (event) => {
    sendClientLog({
      level: "error",
      event: "unhandled-rejection",
      message: event.reason?.message || String(event.reason || "Unhandled promise rejection"),
      details: errorDetails(event.reason),
    });
  });

  sendClientLog({ level: "info", event: "file-save-diagnostics-ready", message: "File save diagnostics initialized." });
}


// ===== frontend/modules/privacyMode.js =====
const STORAGE_KEY = "rth.privateSessions.default";

export function createPrivacyController() {
  let enabled = localStorage.getItem(STORAGE_KEY) === "true";
  const listeners = new Set();

  const notify = () => {
    document.body.classList.toggle("rth-private-default", enabled);
    listeners.forEach((listener) => listener(enabled));
  };

  return {
    isEnabled: () => enabled,
    setEnabled(next) {
      enabled = Boolean(next);
      localStorage.setItem(STORAGE_KEY, String(enabled));
      notify();
    },
    subscribe(listener) {
      listeners.add(listener);
      listener(enabled);
      return () => listeners.delete(listener);
    },
    initialize: notify,
  };
}

function findToolbarHost() {
  return (
    document.querySelector(".topbar-actions") ||
    document.querySelector(".workspace-toolbar") ||
    document.querySelector("header")
  );
}

export function initPrivacyToggle(controller) {
  const host = findToolbarHost();
  if (!host || document.getElementById("rthPrivateModeToggle")) return;

  const button = document.createElement("button");
  button.id = "rthPrivateModeToggle";
  button.type = "button";
  button.className = "rth-private-toggle";
  button.title = "New terminals will not persist logs or command history";
  button.innerHTML = `
    <span class="rth-private-indicator" aria-hidden="true"></span>
    <span class="rth-private-label">Private sessions</span>
  `;
  button.addEventListener("click", () => controller.setEnabled(!controller.isEnabled()));
  controller.subscribe((enabled) => {
    button.setAttribute("aria-pressed", String(enabled));
    button.setAttribute(
      "aria-label",
      enabled ? "Disable private mode for new terminals" : "Enable private mode for new terminals"
    );
  });
  host.prepend(button);
}


// ===== frontend/modules/appShell.js =====
function textContent(element, fallback = "") {
  const value = element?.textContent?.trim();
  return value || fallback;
}

function selectedTerminalLabel() {
  const selectedTab =
    document.querySelector("#terminalTabs .active") ||
    document.querySelector("#terminalTabs [aria-selected='true']") ||
    document.querySelector(".terminal-card.selected .terminal-title");
  return textContent(selectedTab, textContent(document.getElementById("selectedTerminalBadge"), "No terminal selected"));
}

function activeInspectorLabel() {
  const activeTab = document.querySelector(".panel-tabs .tab.active");
  return textContent(activeTab, "Workspace");
}

function installContextBar() {
  if (document.querySelector(".workspace-context-bar")) return;
  const workspace =
    document.querySelector(".workspace-column") ||
    document.querySelector(".main-column") ||
    document.querySelector("main");
  if (!workspace) return;

  const bar = document.createElement("div");
  bar.className = "workspace-context-bar";
  bar.setAttribute("aria-live", "polite");
  bar.innerHTML = `
    <div class="workspace-context-primary">
      <span aria-hidden="true">&#x25cf;</span>
      <span data-rth-context-terminal>No terminal selected</span>
    </div>
    <div class="workspace-context-secondary" data-rth-context-panel>Workspace</div>
  `;
  workspace.prepend(bar);

  const update = () => {
    bar.querySelector("[data-rth-context-terminal]").textContent = selectedTerminalLabel();
    bar.querySelector("[data-rth-context-panel]").textContent = activeInspectorLabel();
  };
  update();

  const observer = new MutationObserver(update);
  [
    document.getElementById("terminalTabs"),
    document.getElementById("selectedTerminalBadge"),
    document.querySelector(".panel-tabs"),
    document.querySelector(".terminals-grid"),
  ].filter(Boolean).forEach((node) => observer.observe(node, {
    subtree: true,
    childList: true,
    attributes: true,
    characterData: true,
  }));
}

function installAccessibleTabs(selector) {
  const tabs = [...document.querySelectorAll(selector)];
  if (!tabs.length) return;
  const parent = tabs[0].parentElement;
  parent?.setAttribute("role", "tablist");
  tabs.forEach((tab, index) => {
    tab.setAttribute("role", "tab");
    tab.tabIndex = tab.classList.contains("active") || index === 0 ? 0 : -1;
    tab.setAttribute("aria-selected", String(tab.classList.contains("active")));
    tab.addEventListener("click", () => {
      tabs.forEach((item) => {
        const active = item === tab;
        item.tabIndex = active ? 0 : -1;
        item.setAttribute("aria-selected", String(active));
      });
    });
    tab.addEventListener("keydown", (event) => {
      if (!['ArrowLeft', 'ArrowRight'].includes(event.key)) return;
      event.preventDefault();
      const direction = event.key === 'ArrowRight' ? 1 : -1;
      const target = tabs[(tabs.indexOf(tab) + direction + tabs.length) % tabs.length];
      target.focus();
      target.click();
    });
  });
}

export function initAppShell() {
  document.body.dataset.rthFrontend = "p2";
  installAccessibleTabs(".sidebar-filter-chip");
  installAccessibleTabs(".panel-tabs .tab");
  installContextBar();
}

// ===== fixes.mjs =====
// fixes.mjs
import fs from 'fs';
import path from 'path';
import { execFileSync } from 'child_process';
import readline from 'readline'; // Required for prompting the user

// Updated to use your specific Raspberry Pi path
const PROJECT_ROOT = '/home/luan_ngo/terminal';
const FIXES_DIR = path.join(PROJECT_ROOT, 'fixes');
const TEMP_EXTRACT_DIR = path.join(PROJECT_ROOT, '.temp_extracted_fixes');
const BACKUP_ROOT = path.join(PROJECT_ROOT, '.backup');

function exists(p) {
  return fs.existsSync(p);
}

function ensureDir(dirPath) {
  fs.mkdirSync(dirPath, { recursive: true });
}

// Helper to count lines in a file
function getLineCount(filePath) {
  try {
    const content = fs.readFileSync(filePath, 'utf-8');
    return content.split('\n').length;
  } catch (error) {
    return 0; // Fallback in case of an issue reading the file
  }
}

function expandZip(zipPath, destinationPath) {
  ensureDir(destinationPath);
  try {
    // Uses standard Linux unzip command
    execFileSync('unzip', ['-q', '-o', zipPath, '-d', destinationPath], { stdio: 'inherit' });
  } catch (error) {
    throw new Error(`Failed to unzip file. Ensure 'unzip' is installed on your system. Error: ${error.message}`);
  }
}

function walkDirs(startDir, out = []) {
  const entries = fs.readdirSync(startDir, { withFileTypes: true });
  for (const entry of entries) {
    const fullPath = path.join(startDir, entry.name);
    if (entry.isDirectory()) {
      out.push(fullPath);
      walkDirs(fullPath, out);
    }
  }
  return out;
}

function findExtractedProjectRoot(startDir) {
  const dirs = [startDir, ...walkDirs(startDir)];
  
  // Get a list of top-level directories currently in the project (client, server, agent, etc.)
  const projectDirs = fs.readdirSync(PROJECT_ROOT, { withFileTypes: true })
    .filter(d => d.isDirectory() && !d.name.startsWith('.'))
    .map(d => d.name);

  for (const dir of dirs) {
    const extractedItems = fs.readdirSync(dir, { withFileTypes: true })
      .filter(d => d.isDirectory())
      .map(d => d.name);

    // If this directory contains any folder that matches a project root folder, we found the root
    if (extractedItems.some(item => projectDirs.includes(item))) {
      return dir;
    }
  }

  throw new Error(`Could not find a valid project root inside the extracted zip.`);
}

function collectFiles(dir, baseDir = dir, out = []) {
  const entries = fs.readdirSync(dir, { withFileTypes: true });

  for (const entry of entries) {
    const fullPath = path.join(dir, entry.name);
    if (entry.isDirectory()) {
      collectFiles(fullPath, baseDir, out);
    } else if (entry.isFile()) {
      out.push({
        fullPath,
        relativePath: path.relative(baseDir, fullPath)
      });
    }
  }

  return out;
}

function filesAreEqual(fileA, fileB) {
  if (!exists(fileA) || !exists(fileB)) return false;
  const statA = fs.statSync(fileA);
  const statB = fs.statSync(fileB);
  if (statA.size !== statB.size) return false;
  
  const bufA = fs.readFileSync(fileA);
  const bufB = fs.readFileSync(fileB);
  return bufA.equals(bufB);
}

function parseApplyOptions(args = []) {
  return {
    createNew: args.some((arg) =>
      ['--create-new', '--create-missing', '--yes-create-new', '--yes'].includes(arg)
    ),
  };
}

// applyFixes is now async to handle user input pausing
async function applyFixes(zipFileName, options = {}) {
  const zipPath = path.join(FIXES_DIR, zipFileName);
  if (!exists(zipPath)) {
    throw new Error(`ZIP file not found: ${zipPath}`);
  }

  cleanupTempDir();
  console.log(`\nExtracting ZIP: ${zipPath}`);
  expandZip(zipPath, TEMP_EXTRACT_DIR);

  const extractedProjectRoot = findExtractedProjectRoot(TEMP_EXTRACT_DIR);
  console.log(`Found extracted project root: ${extractedProjectRoot}`);

  const sourceFiles = collectFiles(extractedProjectRoot);
  const results = [];
  const TIMESTAMP = new Date().toISOString().replace(/[:.]/g, '-');
  const CURRENT_BACKUP_DIR = path.join(BACKUP_ROOT, TIMESTAMP);

  // Setup readline for interactive prompts
  const rl = readline.createInterface({
    input: process.stdin,
    output: process.stdout
  });
  const askQuestion = (query) => new Promise(resolve => rl.question(query, resolve));

  for (const file of sourceFiles) {
    const sourceFile = file.fullPath;
    const destFile = path.join(PROJECT_ROOT, file.relativePath);
    const relativeToProject = path.relative(PROJECT_ROOT, destFile);

    const result = { action: 'skipped', file: relativeToProject, error: null };

    if (!exists(destFile)) {
      if (!options.createNew) {
        // Prompt user if they want to create the missing file
        const answer = await askQuestion(`\n[?] File not found in project: ${relativeToProject}\n    Do you want to create a new one? (y/n): `);
        
        if (answer.toLowerCase() !== 'y' && answer.toLowerCase() !== 'yes') {
          result.action = 'error';
          result.error = `File does not exist and creation was declined.`;
          results.push(result);
          continue;
        }
      }

      // User chose to create the new file, or --create-new was passed
      ensureDir(path.dirname(destFile));
      fs.copyFileSync(sourceFile, destFile);
      
      result.action = 'created';
      result.oldLines = 0;
      result.newLines = getLineCount(sourceFile);
      results.push(result);
      continue;
    }

    if (filesAreEqual(sourceFile, destFile)) {
      results.push(result);
      continue;
    }

    // Capture line counts before overwriting
    const oldLines = getLineCount(destFile);
    const newLines = getLineCount(sourceFile);

    // Backup existing file
    const backupFile = path.join(CURRENT_BACKUP_DIR, relativeToProject);
    ensureDir(path.dirname(backupFile));
    fs.copyFileSync(destFile, backupFile);

    // Apply new file
    ensureDir(path.dirname(destFile));
    fs.copyFileSync(sourceFile, destFile);
    
    result.action = 'updated';
    result.oldLines = oldLines;
    result.newLines = newLines;
    results.push(result);
  }

  rl.close();
  cleanupTempDir();
  printResults(results, CURRENT_BACKUP_DIR);
}

function revertFixes(timestamp) {
  const targetBackupDir = path.join(BACKUP_ROOT, timestamp);
  
  if (!exists(targetBackupDir)) {
    console.error(`\nAvailable backups in ${BACKUP_ROOT}:`);
    if (exists(BACKUP_ROOT)) {
      fs.readdirSync(BACKUP_ROOT).forEach(dir => console.log(` - ${dir}`));
    } else {
      console.log('  (No backups found)');
    }
    throw new Error(`Backup folder not found: ${targetBackupDir}`);
  }

  console.log(`\nReverting files from backup: ${timestamp}`);
  const backupFiles = collectFiles(targetBackupDir);
  const results = [];

  for (const file of backupFiles) {
    const backupFile = file.fullPath;
    const destFile = path.join(PROJECT_ROOT, file.relativePath);
    const relativeToProject = path.relative(PROJECT_ROOT, destFile);

    ensureDir(path.dirname(destFile));
    fs.copyFileSync(backupFile, destFile);

    results.push({ action: 'reverted', file: relativeToProject });
  }

  for (const res of results) {
    console.log(`REVERTED  ${res.file}`);
  }
  console.log(`\nSuccessfully reverted ${results.length} files.`);
}

function cleanupTempDir() {
  if (exists(TEMP_EXTRACT_DIR)) {
    fs.rmSync(TEMP_EXTRACT_DIR, { recursive: true, force: true });
  }
}

function printResults(results, backupDir) {
  const updatedCount = results.filter(r => r.action === 'updated').length;
  const createdCount = results.filter(r => r.action === 'created').length;
  const skippedCount = results.filter(r => r.action === 'skipped').length;
  const errorResults = results.filter(r => r.action === 'error');

  console.log('\n--- Operations Log ---');
  for (const res of results) {
    if (res.action === 'updated') {
      let warning = '';
      // Check if line count dropped by more than 10%
      if (res.oldLines > 0) {
        const decrease = res.oldLines - res.newLines;
        const percentDecrease = decrease / res.oldLines;
        if (percentDecrease > 0.10) {
          warning = '  ⚠️ WARNING: Line count reduced by > 10%';
        }
      }
      console.log(`UPDATED   ${res.file} (Lines: ${res.oldLines} -> ${res.newLines})${warning}`);
    } else if (res.action === 'created') {
      console.log(`CREATED   ${res.file} (Lines: ${res.newLines})`);
    } else if (res.action === 'skipped') {
      console.log(`SKIPPED   ${res.file} (no changes)`);
    } else if (res.action === 'error') {
      console.error(`ERROR     ${res.file} -> ${res.error}`);
    }
  }

  console.log('\n--- Summary ---');
  console.log(`Updated: ${updatedCount}`);
  console.log(`Created: ${createdCount}`);
  console.log(`Skipped: ${skippedCount}`);
  console.log(`Errors:  ${errorResults.length}`);

  if (updatedCount > 0 || createdCount > 0) {
    console.log(`\nBackup saved. To revert, run:\nnode ./fixes.mjs revert ${path.basename(backupDir)}`);
  } else {
    console.log('\nNo files were changed, so no backup was created.');
    // Remove empty backup dir if created
    if (exists(backupDir) && fs.readdirSync(backupDir).length === 0) {
      fs.rmSync(backupDir, { recursive: true, force: true });
    }
  }

  if (errorResults.length > 0) process.exitCode = 1;
}

// main is now async
async function main() {
  const command = process.argv[2];
  const target = process.argv[3];
  const options = parseApplyOptions(process.argv.slice(4));

  if (command === 'apply' && target) {
    await applyFixes(target, options);
  } else if (command === 'revert' && target) {
    revertFixes(target);
  } else {
    console.error('Usage:');
    console.error('  Apply a fix:  node ./fixes.mjs apply <zip-file-in-fixes-dir> [--create-new]');
    console.error('  Revert a fix: node ./fixes.mjs revert <timestamp-folder-name>');
    console.error('\nExample:');
    console.error('  node ./fixes.mjs apply my-patch.zip');
    console.error('  node ./fixes.mjs apply my-patch.zip --create-new');
    console.error('  node ./fixes.mjs revert 2026-03-23T12-30-00-000Z');
    process.exit(1);
  }
}

// Top-level execution wrapper
async function run() {
  try {
    await main();
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('\nERROR:', error.message);
    process.exitCode = 1;
  } finally {
    cleanupTempDir();
  }
}

run();


// ===== public/service-worker.js =====
const CACHE_NAME = "remote-terminal-hub-v6";
const SHELL_ASSETS = [
  "/styles.css",
  "/build/frontend.css",
  "/build/frontend.js",
  "/manifest.webmanifest",
  "/icons/icon.svg"
];

self.addEventListener("install", (event) => {
  event.waitUntil(
    caches
      .open(CACHE_NAME)
      .then((cache) => cache.addAll(SHELL_ASSETS))
      .then(() => self.skipWaiting())
  );
});

self.addEventListener("activate", (event) => {
  event.waitUntil(
    caches
      .keys()
      .then((names) => Promise.all(names.filter((name) => name !== CACHE_NAME).map((name) => caches.delete(name))))
      .then(() => self.clients.claim())
  );
});

self.addEventListener("fetch", (event) => {
  const request = event.request;
  if (request.method !== "GET" || request.mode === "navigate") {
    return;
  }

  const url = new URL(request.url);
  if (
    url.origin !== self.location.origin ||
    url.pathname.startsWith("/api/") ||
    url.pathname.startsWith("/socket.io/") ||
    url.pathname.startsWith("/download/quick/") ||
    url.pathname === "/login" ||
    url.pathname === "/register" ||
    url.pathname === "/logout"
  ) {
    return;
  }

  event.respondWith(
    fetch(request)
      .then((response) => {
        if (response && response.ok) {
          const copy = response.clone();
          caches.open(CACHE_NAME).then((cache) => cache.put(request, copy));
        }
        return response;
      })
      .catch(() => caches.match(request).then((cached) => cached || new Response("Offline", { status: 503, statusText: "Service Unavailable" })))
  );
});


// ===== public/pathTracker.js =====
function joinRemotePath(basePath = ".", relativePath = "") {
  const base = String(basePath || ".").replace(/\/+$/, "") || ".";
  const relative = String(relativePath || "").replace(/^\/+/, "");
  if (!relative) return base;
  if (base === "." || base === "") return relative;
  if (base === "/") return `/${relative}`;
  return `${base}/${relative}`.replace(/\/+/g, "/");
}

function normalizeRemotePath(basePath = ".", nextPath = "") {
  const raw = String(nextPath || "").trim();
  if (!raw || raw === ".") return String(basePath || ".") || ".";

  const base = String(basePath || ".") || ".";
  const absolute = raw.startsWith("/");
  const homeBase = base.startsWith("/") ? base.split("/").slice(0, 3).join("/") || "/" : "~";
  const expanded = raw === "~"
    ? homeBase
    : raw.startsWith("~/")
      ? `${homeBase}${raw.slice(1)}`
      : raw;
  const combined = absolute || expanded.startsWith("/")
    ? expanded
    : joinRemotePath(base, expanded);
  const prefix = combined.startsWith("/") ? "/" : "";
  const parts = [];

  for (const part of combined.split("/")) {
    if (!part || part === ".") continue;
    if (part === "..") {
      if (parts.length) parts.pop();
      continue;
    }
    parts.push(part);
  }

  const normalized = `${prefix}${parts.join("/")}`.replace(/\/+/g, "/");
  return normalized || (prefix ? "/" : ".");
}

function splitShellWords(input = "") {
  const words = [];
  let current = "";
  let quote = "";
  let escaped = false;

  for (const char of String(input || "")) {
    if (escaped) {
      current += char;
      escaped = false;
      continue;
    }
    if (char === "\\") {
      escaped = true;
      continue;
    }
    if (quote) {
      if (char === quote) {
        quote = "";
      } else {
        current += char;
      }
      continue;
    }
    if (char === "'" || char === '"') {
      quote = char;
      continue;
    }
    if (/\s/.test(char)) {
      if (current) {
        words.push(current);
        current = "";
      }
      continue;
    }
    current += char;
  }

  if (current) words.push(current);
  return words;
}

function pathFromCdCommand(currentPath = ".", previousPath = "", command = "") {
  const firstCommand = String(command || "").split(/&&|;|\|\|/)[0]?.trim() || "";
  const words = splitShellWords(firstCommand);
  if (words[0] !== "cd") return "";

  const target = words[1] || "~";
  return target === "-"
    ? previousPath || currentPath
    : normalizeRemotePath(currentPath, target);
}

export {
  joinRemotePath,
  normalizeRemotePath,
  pathFromCdCommand,
  splitShellWords,
};

  <dialog id="helpModal">
    <form class="dialog-form compact-help-form">
      <div class="help-header">
        <h3>Help & shortcuts</h3>
        <button type="button" data-close-dialog="helpModal">Close</button>
      </div>
      <details open>
        <summary>Layouts and panes</summary>
        <ul class="help-list">
          <li><strong>Grid mode</strong> shows multiple live SSH terminals at once.</li>
          <li><strong>Tabs mode</strong> shows one focused terminal with a tab strip.</li>
          <li><strong>Vertical stack mode</strong> gives each terminal a full-width row.</li>
          <li><strong>Focus mode</strong> hides side chrome so the active terminal gets more room.</li>
          <li>Use the sidebar and right pane toggle buttons to collapse major panes.</li>
          <li>Saved connections, quick commands, sessions, pinned commands, and recent commands can be collapsed individually.</li>
          <li>The file tree, editor, and AI transcript can each be collapsed for a denser layout.</li>
        </ul>
      </details>
      <details open>
        <summary>Keyboard shortcuts</summary>
        <div class="shortcut-grid">
          <div><kbd>F1</kbd><span>Open help</span></div>
          <div><kbd>Ctrl</kbd><kbd>K</kbd><span>Open command palette</span></div>
          <div><kbd>Ctrl</kbd><kbd>B</kbd><span>Toggle sidebar</span></div>
          <div><kbd>Ctrl</kbd><kbd>Shift</kbd><kbd>B</kbd><span>Toggle right pane</span></div>
          <div><kbd>Ctrl</kbd><kbd>I</kbd><span>Open inline AI in selected terminal</span></div>
          <div><kbd>Ctrl</kbd><kbd>Shift</kbd><kbd>key</kbd><span>Send Ctrl+key to the selected terminal</span></div>
          <div><kbd>Ctrl</kbd><kbd>Shift</kbd><kbd>F</kbd><span>Focus remote path box</span></div>
          <div><kbd>Ctrl</kbd><kbd>Shift</kbd><kbd>L</kbd><span>Focus AI prompt</span></div>
          <div><kbd>Alt</kbd><kbd>T</kbd><span>Switch to tabs mode</span></div>
          <div><kbd>Alt</kbd><kbd>G</kbd><span>Switch to grid mode</span></div>
          <div><kbd>Alt</kbd><kbd>V</kbd><span>Switch to vertical stack mode</span></div>
          <div><kbd>Ctrl</kbd><kbd>Shift</kbd><kbd>←</kbd> / <kbd>→</kbd><span>Cycle open terminal tabs</span></div>
          <div><kbd>Alt</kbd><kbd>←</kbd> / <kbd>→</kbd><span>Cycle open terminal tabs</span></div>
          <div><kbd>Alt</kbd><kbd>R</kbd><span>Toggle file tree</span></div>
          <div><kbd>Alt</kbd><kbd>E</kbd><span>Toggle file editor</span></div>
          <div><kbd>Alt</kbd><kbd>Y</kbd><span>Toggle AI transcript</span></div>
          <div><kbd>Shift</kbd><kbd>Esc</kbd><span>Exit focus mode</span></div>
          <div><kbd>Ctrl</kbd> <kbd>T</kbd><span>New terminal</span></div>
          <div><kbd>Ctrl</kbd> <kbd>W</kbd><span>Close selected terminal</span></div>
          <div><kbd>Ctrl</kbd> <kbd>J</kbd><span>Toggle right panel</span></div>
          <div><kbd>Ctrl</kbd> <kbd>Shift</kbd> <kbd>E</kbd><span>Open Files panel</span></div>
          <div><kbd>Ctrl</kbd> <kbd>Shift</kbd> <kbd>A</kbd><span>Open AI panel</span></div>
          <div><kbd>Ctrl</kbd> <kbd>1</kbd>-<kbd>9</kbd><span>Switch to terminal</span></div>
        </div>
      </details>
      <details open>
        <summary>Copy and paste</summary>
        <ul class="help-list">
          <li><strong>Ctrl+C</strong>, <strong>Ctrl+V</strong>, and <strong>Ctrl+X</strong> go directly to the terminal.</li>
          <li><strong>Ctrl+Shift+C</strong> copies selected terminal text.</li>
          <li><strong>Ctrl+Shift+V</strong> pastes clipboard text into the selected terminal.</li>
          <li><strong>Ctrl+Shift+X</strong> cuts selected terminal text from the browser selection.</li>
          <li>Other Ctrl+Shift combinations send the matching Ctrl command to the terminal.</li>
          <li>On mobile, use the Ctrl shortcut row above each terminal for common shell controls.</li>
          <li>Use <em>Copy recent</em> to copy the latest terminal output without selecting text.</li>
          <li>Use <em>Paste text</em> when browser clipboard permissions are blocked or the paste needs checking first.</li>
        </ul>
      </details>
      <details open>
        <summary>Mobile and touch controls</summary>
        <ul class="help-list">
          <li>The bottom dock gives one-tap access to navigation, terminal maximize, panel minimize, files, AI, and new connections.</li>
          <li>Use the dock maximize button to make the selected terminal full screen, and the down button to minimize open mobile panels.</li>
          <li>The Ctrl shortcut row sits directly above each terminal on phones, tablets, and touch screens.</li>
          <li>Swipe the shortcut row sideways to reach Ctrl+C, Ctrl+X, Ctrl+R, Ctrl+D, Ctrl+L, Ctrl+Z, Ctrl+A, Ctrl+E, Ctrl+U, and Ctrl+W.</li>
          <li>Use the top toolbar category menus for view, file, AI, and text-size actions.</li>
        </ul>
      </details>
      <details>
        <summary>AI workflow</summary>
        <ul class="help-list">
          <li>Select terminal output and click <em>Use selected output</em> or press <em>Ask selection</em> on a terminal card.</li>
          <li>Press <strong>Ctrl+I</strong> inside a terminal to open an inline assistant like an advanced editor workflow.</li>
          <li>AI answers with shell code let you <em>Run</em>, <em>Insert</em>, or <em>Copy</em>.</li>
          <li>The right-hand assistant stays available as a persistent chat panel for broader context.</li>
        </ul>
      </details>
    </form>
  </dialog>
